Bowere s'oomat Ik'o bo k'oniyakon bokishono boats gedt wosh bok'iri.
Barnabasnat Sawln S'ayin shayiron wosheyat Selewik'iyo maats boami. Manokno markabon K'op'ros maats boami.
Selamis kitots bo bodtsok'on ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni mootse Ik'i aap'o bodani, Yohanis Mark'oswere bonton wotat boosh bodabiri b́teshi.
Aatso gúrts K'op'ros datsu k'ut't p'afuyi bo bodtsok'on Baryesusi eteefo ayhudits ik'ets ash iko daats bodek'i, bímó kootets nebiyiya b́ tesh.
B́befonuwere Sergyos P'awlosi eteets t'iwintsdek'ts dats k'eezfontoni b́tesh, dats k'eezfan Bernabasnat Sa'oln s'eegt Ik' aap'o k'ebo b́ geyi.
Ernmó Griki noon keew keewon «Elimas» ett s'eegets ik'etso Beryesus dats k'eezfo bíamanerawok'o geeyat Bernabasnat Sa'oln b́ k'efi.
P'awlosi eteetso Sa'olmó S'ayin shayiron s'eent ashman t'iwintsdek't s'iilt hank'owa bísh bíet,
«Nee Dabilos naayo! ar jami t'alatono! dirshonat gond jamon s'eentsono, kááwu wottso doonzo weerindo k'uuriyo k'azalk neeneya!
Andoor hambe! doonzo kisho neen togetuwee, doogonowere wotitune, muk' gizewosh aawu shaano be'atsnee.» Manoor bíaawwotsi bampulonat t'aluwo ipb́k'iri, b́ kisho deshde'er jishit asho b́ ganoke geyo dek'b́tuwi.
Dats k'ezfonuwere wotts jamo b́ bek'tsok'on bíamani, doonzo jangosho b́shishts danon bíadi.
Maniyere okoon P'awlosnt b́ tohuwotsn Markabats keshdek't P'afutse P'nflyo maantse daatseyiru P'erge maants boami, Mark'osi eteyiruwo Yohanismó boatse k'aleyat Iyerusalem maants aanat bíami.
Boomó P'ergeyiyere tuut P'isdyayitsi datsatse fa'a Ans'okiyo maats boami, sanbati aawon ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni moots kindt beebowutsi.
Muse nemonat Nebiyiwots mas'afwots nababeyakon Ayhudi Ik' k'oni maa naashuwots «T eshuwotso, ashuwotsi kup'it izo detsfte wotiyal keewwere» ett P'awlosots maants asho bo woshi.
Mansh P'awlos tuut ashosh kishon b́koli, hank'o ett b́keewi, «Isra'el ashuwotsnat Ik' shatiru Ik' ash woterawwotso! k'ewere!
Israe'el ashaanotsko Izar Izewer yoots no nihotsi galre, Gbs'datsatse boteshor een ashuwotsi boon b́woshi, bí een angonowere datsmanatse boon b́kishi.
Hab́natonoshowere woruwotse boon b́ k'ami,
Kan'an datsatse shawat nugúsuwotsi t'afit bodatso bíashwotssh b́naatiyi,
Jaman awd bale balk'ats naato b́ ishi, maniyakowere nebiyo Samu'el dúrosh b́ borfetso Mesafntiyotsi b́ imi.
«Manats dabt nugúso boosh b́ naashituwok'o Ik'o bok'oni, Ik'onuwere Biniyam jir wottso K'is naayi Sa'oli hab natosh boosh b́ naashiyi.
Sa'olno naashatse b́ orshiyakon Dawiti b́ naashiyi, Ik'onu Dawit jangosh b́ gawor, ‹T shuntsok'o wottso, tshunono fintso, Isey naayi Dwiti daatsre› etre.
Ashaan naarotse Ik'o b́ jangits keewok'on Isra'eli kashituwo Iyesusi boosh b́ tuuzi.
Iyesus b́ waraftse shinon Yohanis Israe'el ash jamosh naandrone err gupeyo nabre b́teshi.
Yohanis b́ fino b́ ishtsok'on ‹Taa kone itsh tiari? Taahe Mesihiyo taanaliye, ernmó b́ c'aami tiponoru dab bitsosh tborawo t shutsatse k'osho weetuwe› bí etfoni.
«It Abraham naaratse shuwets eshuwwotsnat itwere Ik' shatiru Ik' ash woterawwotso! bín kashet wóóshan woshe noshee
Iyerusalemn beyiru ashuwotsnat boon jishiruwots Iyesus kashitso b́ wottsok'o danatsne, sanbati aawu aawon nababeyiru nebiyiwots mas'aafwotsi t'iwintso bok'aztsosh bíats boangshor bek'on keewetso b́s'eenetuwok'o woshrne.
K'irosh bín betsit keewo eegoru bíatse datso bok'azaloru bín boosh b́ úd'ituwok'o P'ilat'osi bo k'oni.
B́ jangosh guut'ets jamo b́s'eeniyakon jitatse orshdek't boduki,
Ernmó Ik'o k'irotse bín b́tizi.
Geliltsere Iyerusalem maants bínton waatsuwotsshowere ay aawosh boats b́ be'eyi, boowere and ashuwots shinatse b́ gawwotsiye.
No itsh detsdek' nowatso Ik'o nonihotssh jangit b́ ímts doo shishiyi keewoniye.
Ik'o Iyesusi k'irotse b́tiztsotse b́jangitsano noosh bo nanaúwotssh finats jitsre, manuwere gitli Dubotse, ‹Nee tnay neene, taa neen hambets shuure,› ett guut'etsok'one.
B́ o'awok'o Ik'o k'irotse b́ tiztsok'o daniyosh, ‹S'ayin amanets deero Dawitsh jangit imetso itsh imetuwe› ett keewure.
Dabt k'osh dubotse, ‹N Naayi S'ayino b́ ok'etwok'o woshatsne› bí eti
Ernmó Dawit b́ dúr jamo b́ fino Ik'i shuntso b́s'eentsyakon k'irre, nihwotsntonuwere duukere, ok'ree.
Ik'o k'irotse b́tiztsonmó oa'atse.
Eshe tí eshuwotso! Morrosh oorowe eto datsetuwo Iyesusn b́wottsok'owo itsh nabetsok'o dande'ere,
Bín amants jamo Muse weeron imets nemo nas'o kisho b́ falawu morr jamatse nas'o keshituwe.
Mansh nebiyatiyotsn Ik'o hank'o ett b́ keewetso itats b́ borawok'o korde'ere,
‹It aatsnirwots s'iilere! adúwere! t'afuwere! Konuworu asho itsh b́ keewure It amanerawu fino itdúroon finitwe.› »
P'awlosn at Barnabasn ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni mootse bokeshfere keewan weet sanbatots aani boosh bokewituwok'o ashuwotsi bok'oni.
Ayhudi Ik' k'oni moots ko'etswots bad'bowutstsok'oon ay Ayhudi jirwotsnat Ayhudi imnetiyots kindt Ik' Ik'iru Ashuwots P'awlosnt Barnabasn shuutso botuwi, P'awlosnt Barnabasnowere ashuwotsi danit Ik'i s'aaton kup'ar bobetuwok'o boosh bogawiyi.
Weet sanbatono kitotse beyiru ashuwotsitse aywots, Ik'i aap'o shishosh ko'ebowutsi,
Ayhudiyots ash ashuwots ay bowottsok'o bo bek'tsosh okooron s'een bowutsi, b́ keewono k'efefetst P'awlosi boc'ashi,
P'awlosn at Barnabasnomó hank'o ett ááwu shuk'on bokeewi, «Ik' aap'o shini itsh keewo geyife, it de'atsone it etalomó dúre dúr kasho itsh b́ woterawok'o it tookats it angshtsotse hamb no Ik' ash woterawwots maants wongrer ametuwone.
Manowere nok'alitiye doonzo, ‹Kasho dats daarats b́borfetso n doowetuwok'o Ik' ash Woteraw ashuwotssh shááno neen woshre› ett b́ azaztsotsne.»
Ik' ash woterawwots han boshishtsok'n geneú bowutsi doonzo aap'o bomangiyi, dúre dúr kashosh gaalets jamwotswrere boamani.
Doonzo aap'onuwere dats jamanats bad'b́wutsi.
Ayhudi jishiruwotsmó ayhudi imnetiyo amaniru gaalets mááts máátsuwtsenat kititsi een een ashuwotsi gondon P'awlosnat Barnabasn gishetuwok'o bowoshi, bo datsatsnowere boon bokishi.
P'awlosnat Barnabasn boats botufatsi k'undo tebazt Ik'oniyon maants boami.
B́ danifuwosuwere gene'onat S'ayn shayiron bos'eeni.
Ik'oniyonitse P'awlosnat Bernabasn towaat ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni moots bokindi, manoknowere ay ayhudiwotsnat Ik' ash Woteraw ayidek't ayts ashuwots bo amanefetsosh bodaniyi.
Amaneraw ayhudiwotsmó Ik'i ash woterawwotsi tuzit eshuwotsats shit'o b́weetwok'o bok'ali.
Mansh P'awlosnat Bernabasn doonzo keewo ááwu shuk'on keewfetst manoke ayi gizewos boteshi, doonzonwere milikitwotsnat adits keewwotsi bokishon bofinetwok'o alo boosh imt, b́ s'aati aap'o ariko b́wottsok'o b́kiitsfoni.
Kitutse beyiruwotsmó, gitoko kayaat bado ayhudiwotsnton bado woshetswotsnton bowoti.
Ik' ash woterawwotsna ayhudiwots bo naashuwotsnton wotdek't P'awlosnat Bernabasn kaarar shútson togosh bogeyi,
P'awlosn at Bernabasn man bodantsok'on Lst'ranat Derbeyi eteef Lik'a'on kituwotsnat bogúúratse fa'a datsats giifat boami.
Manoknowere doo shishiyo bonabi.
Lst'ra datsatse b́ tufo lasha'awutsts ash iko fa'e b́tesh, ashaan b́ shuweetson tuut dura b́teshtsotse b́ tufoon sha'a danaka,
Ashaan P'awlos b́ keewor bedek'tni b́ k'ebiri b́ tesh, P'awlos ashman t'iwintsdek't s'iilt kashosh bín betsit imnetiyo b́ detso b́ bek'tsok'on,
«Kaawde'er ntufoon need'owe!» ett k'aari eenon b́keewi, ashmanwere t'oolat tuut hake bak b́sha'i.
Ashuwotswere P'awlos b́ k'altso bo bek'tsok'on, bok'aaro eenshdek't «Ik'uwots ash aron wotdek't nok oot'rnee!» ett Lik'aoni noon keewu keewon bokeewi.
Bernabasshower «Dya» boeti. Keewu keewiruwo P'awlosi b́ teshtsotse bísh «Hermeniye» boeti.
Kitoniyere úratse fa'o diyako s'ayin máá kahniyo minzi wrwotsnat k'odets funduwotsnowere kiti fengesho maants dek'wat ash ashonton ikwotdek't P'awlosnat Bernabasnsh wosho t'intsosh b́geyi.
Wosheets, P'awlosnat Benabasn man boshishtsok'on shiyanon botaho bo gaat'i, ash asho maantsowere wos't kuhefets hank'o boeti,
«It ash ashuwots eegishe han itk'aliri? Nowoor itnk'o ash noone, Noo hanok nowaa it hank'o k'awuntsal keewu jamatse wokar daro, datso, aatsk'aronat bogitsotse daatseyiru jamo aztso Kashetso Izar Izewer maants it aanituwok'o sheeng keewo shishiyishee,
Beshts dúrowotsitse ash jamo botook weeron boametuwok'o Ik'o boon kazb́k'ri,
Wotowa bako bíaawuk'o sheengo Izar Izeweri b́ wottsok'o gaawit sheeng fino k'alo need'iratse, darotse awusho itsh bútsiree, maay kakuwi shashwotsi itsh b́ imi, Mishonat geneeúon itn b́woriyi.»
Wosheetsots mank'o dabt bokeewiyalor ash asho boosh wosho t'intso b́k'azetuwok'o bobazi ayidek' kic'oone.
Ayhudiwotsmó Ans'okiyonat t Ik'oniyonn manok waat ash asho tuzdek't P'awlosi shútson botogetuwok'o bowoshi, k'irb́wutstsok'o bíarere geets dek't kitotse kishbok'ri.
Ernmó b́danifuwots waat bín gúúrdek't boned'fere P'awlos tuut kitots b́kindi, yaats guurok'onowere Bernabasnton Derbe maants bíami.
P'awlosnat Bernabasn Derbe datsatse doo shishiyo danit ay ashuwotsi amantsuwotsi bowoshiyakon Lst'ronat Ik'oniyonn beshat P'sdiyin fa'úts Ans'okits boami.
Dats jam manotsatsnowere amantsuwots boamantsats kup'bodek'etuwok'o boon kup'iyonat izosh «Ik'i mengstots kindosh ay gondo noosh geyife» etfetst boon bdaniyi.
Ik' k'oni maa mootse eenash eenashuwotsnowere boosh bonaashi, s'omat Ik'o bok'oniyakonowere bín boamants doonzosh adaro imbok'ri.
P'sdiyanowere beshat P'nfli maants boami,
P'ergeyitsnowere Ik' aap'tso bodaniyakon At'aliyi maants boami,
Maniyere hakonowere bok'alts Ik'i s'aatosh adaro boosh ímeets Ans'okimaants markabon boami.
Manok bobodetsok'on amantsuwotsi ikok kakudek't Ik'o awuk'o k'alt bonton wotdek't b́fiints jamonat Ik'i ash woterawwotswor boamanituwok'o awuk'o k'alt fengesho boosh b́k'eshtsok'o bokeewi
Manoknowere amantsuwotsnton ay aawo boteshi.
Ash ik ikuwots Yhuditsere Ans'oki maants amt «Musesh imets nemok'on gofo it amala bako kasho falratste» ett amantsuwotsi daniyo dek'botuwi.
P'awlosnat Bernabasn manjangosh ash ashuwotsnton wed'eyat moosho bomooshi, Maniyere okoon P'awlosnat Bernabasn Ans'okitse fa'e k'osh muk' eshuwotsnton wotde'er Iyerusalemits amr b́jango woshetswotsnat eenashuwotsnsh bot'intsituwok'o woshi.
Mansh bo Ik'i moon wosheyat boami, Fink'enat Semaritse bobesheferowere Ik'i ashwoterawwots Ik'o maants boaano bokeewi, keewetsanuwere krstiyani jametsuwotsi b́geneúshi.
Iyerusalemits bobodtsok'on Ik'i moowunat woshetswotsn, eenashuwotswere boon bodek'i, wosheetsuwotswere Ik'o bonton wotdek't b́ fintso boosh bokeewi.
Ernmó Ferisawino eteefuwots jirwotsits wotts ik ik amantsuwots tuut «Ik'i ash woterawwots gofo amr Muse nemo bokotetuwok'o k'alo geyife» boeti.
Woshetswotsnat eenashuwotsn keewan shuu'ar s'ilosh kakuwebodek'i,
Ay moosho mosheyakonowere P'et'ros tuut boosh hank'o bíeti, «Eshuwwotso, Ik'i ash woterawwots taan Doo shishiyo k'ewur boamanituwok'o taan ititse galb́dek'tsok'o danfte.
Ash nib dantso Izar Izewer, S'ayin shayiro noosh b́imtsok'o booshowere imtni b́ gawi.
Bonibo amanon b́ s'ayntstsosh noonat bodagotse eegoru k'osh k'osho woshratse.
Eshe, nonihotsi wotowa noo kuro nofalrawu k'ambariyo amantsuwots bimbats kuriyon and Ik'o eegishe itfadiri?
Noo nokashit bokok'o doonzo Iyesus s'aaton b́ woto amaniruwone.»
Manoor kakuwets ash jamo s'ik ett Bernabasnat P'awlosn boweeron Ik'o Ik' ash woterawwots dagotse b́ fints milikitonat adits keewu jamo bokeewure adt k'ebeyi.
Bo keewut boishiyak, Yak'ob hank'o ett bíaniyi «Ti eshuwotso! aab taan k'ewere!
Ik'o b́ shútson s'eeget ik ikashuwotsi bo dagotse galdek'osh shinshino awuk'o k'alt Ik' ash woterawwotsi waa b́s'iiltsok'o Sim'on keewure.
Hasabiyantonuwerfe nebiywots keewuts keewo manee, hank'o ett guut'etsok'one,
‹Haniyehak aani weetuwe, Gahtso Dawit moo agetuwe, B́ gahts tiish tishonowere tizde'er aaniy need'ituwe.
Hanowere t k'alit oorts ashuwotsnat T shútson s'eegets Ik'i ash Woteraw jamwots Ik'o bogeytuwok'owee,
Yootstson jaman danitso Ik'o taa hank'o etiruwe,›
«Mansh tiaasabiyo Ik'omaants aanits Ik'i ash woterawwotsi nokic'irawok'owee.
Maniyere ‹Woterawu ik'uwotssh t'iintsotse kiimts woshi misho máák'ayere, widatse wokoore, shukeerawonat b́ s'atso b́kud'erawo guuk'at k'irts gizi meetso máák'ayere, s'atsonowere máák'ayere› err boosh guud'one.
Yootstson b́ tuutson Muse nemó sanbati aawu jamon ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni mootse nababefe b́teshi, Ik'i keewuts keewonowere kitt kitotse nabefee.»
Maniyere hakon woshetswotsnat eenashuwotsn Ik'i maa ash jamonton wotdek't kakuweetsmanotsitse k'ats ashuwotsi marat'dek't P'awlosnat Bernabasnton Ans'okimaants daamiwosh k'ut'bok'ri, Mansh eshuwotsitse jiishon shútsi sheengo detstswotsi Bersabasi eteetso Yhudnat Silasn marat'bodek'i.
Guut'ets woshi work'ato bokishon bo damiy, Wosh detsts work'atmanuwere hank'o etka b́tesh, «Noo woshetswotsnat eenash eenashuwots it eshuwots, Ans'okinat Soryon, Kilk'iyitsnowere beyiruwots Ik'i ashwoterawwots jirwotsi wottsuwotssh no eshuwotssh jamo itsh t'intsiruwone.
Noyitse ik ik ashuwots noo boon noazazerawon it maants waat itsh bokeewts keewon iti bokic'itsok'onat itn bodanditsok'o shishrone.
Mansh ikok ko'enowutsiyakon woshetuwotsi marat'de'er shuneets no eshuu eshuwwots Barenabasnat P'awlosn ton itmaants woshosh no shiyeyi.
Barnabasnat P'awlosn doonzo Iyesus Krstos jangosh bo kasho beshidek't imknee.
No guut'tsonowere noonon dabr itsh bo keewituwok'o Yhudnat Silasn wosherone.
Itsh not'intsts geyit keewanotsiyere okoon k'osh mang kuro itats nokurirawok'oyish noo S'ayin shayironton sheeng b́wotere daatsrone.
Woteraw ik'osh t'intsetsotse kiimts misho maak'ayere, gúúk'at k'irts gizi meetsono maak'ayere, s'atsono maak'ayere, widatsnowere wokoore, jamkeewanotsatse it atso it kotal sheenge itk'aliti, jamon beewere.»
Wosheetswotswere deen bok'rere Ans'oki maants boami, amantsuwotsnowere kakudek't wosheets work'atman boosh imbok'ri.
Amantswotswere wosheets work'ato bonababor bitsi kúp'its woshmann ayidek' boon b́ geneúshi.
Yhudnat Silasn nebiyiwotsi boteshtsotse eshu eshuwotsi ay Ik'i keewon izt boon bokup'shi.
Yhudnat Silasn muk' aawwotssh manoke boteshiyakon amants eeshuwwotsoke deneyat boon woshtsuwotsok aanat boami.

P'awlosnat Bernabasnowere eshu k'osh ayuwotsnton wotdek' Doonzo keewuts keewo danifets nabfetst muk' aawosh Ans'okitse boteshi.
Muk' aawwotsiyere hakon P'awlos Bernabassh «Wowe anaanar haniyere shin doonzo keewts keewo boosh noshishits kit jamwotsitse fa'a eeshuwuwotsi s'iilone, awuk'o bowottsok'onowere danonee» bí eti.
Bernabasuwere Mark'osi eteetso Yohans bonton towaar bíamo b́ geyi.
P'awlosmó ashman bonton bíametuwok'o eekeratse, eek b́k'aztsonuwere bí P'nfiliyitse boatse k'aleyat b́ oortsonat fino maantsowere bonton amo b́ k'aztsoshe.
Manatse tuutson P'awlosnat Bernabas dagotse mooshi eeno b́tuure k'ale bowutsi, mansh Bernabas Mark'osi detsdek't markabon K'op'ros maants k'azbíami.
P'awlosmó Silasi marat'b́dek'i, eeshuwotswere P'awlosi doonzo s'aatosh adaro beshidek't boimiyakon k'azbími.
Bíwere Ik'i moowuwotsi kup'ifere Soriyonat Kilk'iyi weeron b́beshi.
P'awlos Derbenat Lst'ra maants bíami, Lst'rn T'imotiwosi eteets amants jawets iko fa'e b́tesh, bínd ayhudiyi ash wotat amank krstiyani btesh, b́ nihmó Grik dats asha b́ tesh.
T'imotiyos Lst'ronat Ik'oniyonitse fa'a eeshuwwotsokere sheeng shútso detsfe b́ teshi.
P'awlos T'imotiyosi de'er amo b́getsotse manokere beyru ayhudiwotsatse tuutson gofo b́ ametuwok'o b́woshi, mank'o b́ k'aluwere bo T'imotiyos nih Giriki dats ash b́ woto bodantsotse bojangosha etniye.
P'awlosnat Silasn kit kitotse beshefetst Iyerusalemn fa'a woshetswotsnat eenashuwotsn eteets nemo amantsuwotssh bodanifere b́teshi, finatsowere bojitsituwok'o boosh bogawifere bo teshi.
Mansh Ik' moowwots imnetiyon kup'bowutsi, botaawonúwere dabfere bí'amiri.
P'awlosnat Silasn Isiyi datsatse Ik'i aap'o bokeewurawok'o S'ayn shayiro boosh b́ bazitsotse Frgyiyinat Gelatiyi daarok k'az bobeshi,
Misiyi daarok bobodtsok'on Bitanimaants amoosh gawtni botesh, ernmó Iyesusko S'ayin shayro man maants boametuwok'o eekeratse.
Mansh Misya weeron beshat T'iroadi bo oot'iye.
Manoke t'ú Mek'edoni ash iko need'dek't «Mek'edoni maants kimr noon te'úwe!» ett bín b́ k'onfere bek'on b́bek'i.
P'awlos bek'man b́bek'iyakon manoor Mek'edoni maants amoosh no geyi, Man b́wotuwere Mek'edoni ashuwotsshowere doo shishiyo nodaniyituwok'o Doonzo noon b́ s'eegtsok'o nodani.
T'iroadiyere Markabats keshdek'at kááwon Samtrak'e maants noami, yaats guurok'on Nap'ule maants no ami.
Maniyere tuwat Filip'isyosits nobodi, Filip'isyus Mek'edonitse fa'a kit eenunat Rom dats ashuwots dets bodek'ts datsi b tesh, kitmanitsnowere muk' aawwotsi nobeshi.
Sanbati aawotsowere Ik' k'onosh boko'efok kitoniyere úratse fa'a foki gúrok noo ami, manoke bedek'at ko'edek'ts máátsuwotssh Ik'i aap'o nodaniyi.
Nokeewirman k'ebiru máátswotsitsere iku Tiyat'ros kitotse shuwetsu tahi biro jaakiru Lidiya eteets máátsu fa'a b teshi, biwere Ik' Ik'iru máátsiye b teshi, doonzo b nibo bish b́ k'eshtsotse P'awlos bíaap'iru b k'ebfere b teshi,
Binat b meyitsi fa'a ash jamwots bo gupeyakon, «Doonzo ti amantso arik b́woto itkitsitka wotiyal waar t moots beewere,» etaat kup'idek'at noon b k'oni.
Ik aawu Ik' k'oneyiruwok noamfere shino maants wotit keewo keewit kim shayiro biyatse fa'a ik'ets Gon baarna'ú weerindatse noon b datsi, Gonmanuwere Ik'o oot'at b doonzotssh ay oot'o b datsifo b teshi.
Biwere noonat P'awlosn shuutso shoydek'at sha'at, «Ashaanots een Ik'o gutswotsiye! boowere kash weerindo itsh keewitúnee!» etaat b kuhefooni.
Hanoewre ay aawosh aani aani bk'alfoni, P'awlosmó nibok'úúnwutsat wongr et aanat kiimshayirman «Iyesus Krstos shútson biatsotse nkeshetuwok'o neen azazere!» bí eti. Kim sharonuwere manoor k'azb́keshi.
Bin keezfwotswere b weeron bodatsit oot'o boatse k'ut'b́wtstsok'o bek'bok'rtsok'on P'awlosnat Silasn detsbodek'i, geetsferowere jebomaants dek'amt naashwots shinats t'intsbok'ri.
Rom dats naashuwotsokowere dek'wat hank'o boeti, «Ashaanots Ayhudi jírnee, no kitotsnowere dimbro botuziri,
Noo Rom dats ashuwots dek'o nofalrawu niwo noosh bodaniyiri.»
Ashjamonwere ik wotdek't boats b́tuwi. Naash naashuwotsuwere P'awlosnat Silasn taho sholbazt gumbon botogetuwok'o boazazi.
Ayidek't botogeyi hakon t'ip'moots kindsh bok'iri, tipi maa kotiruwonuwere k'up'ide boon b́kotetuwok'o azazk'reyi,
Kotiruwo azazetsman b́dek'iyakon, tipi maaman gitsotsi kayuts boon kindsh b́k'ri, botufonowere gindonat gindi dagots detsidek't tipb́k'ri.
T'ú Taali titso maantsowere P'awlosnat Silasn Ik' k'ononat dubon Ik'o údfetstni boteshi, tipeets k'oshuwotswere bóóna bok'ebiri botesh.
Gawerawonowere tipimaaman b́ned'oko b́gaahefetsosh een dats shek'eyo wotb́wtsi, fengesh jamwotswere k'eshebowutsi, tipetswotsi boon tipeets habiliyo ik ikon bish b́wutsi.
Kotiruwonuwere b́tokrootse tuut tipimaa fengesuwots k'eshewutsat boere bek't tipetswots k'azbokeshtsok'o bísh bíarere b́ tooko úd'osh b́shiko kaas'b́dek'i,
Ernmó P'awlos, «No no únetswor hanok noone! manshe ntokats gondofink'aye!» ett k'aar eenon b́kúhi.
Manoor kotiruwo c'eesho de'eweetuwok'o wosht gitsots b́kindi, k'eewufetst P'awlosnat Silasn tufi shirots b́baron gúp'nb́wútsi.
Úrats boon kishdekt «T Doonzotso! kashosh eegk'ale taan b́geyiyti?» bí eti.
Bowere «Doonzo Ieyesusn amanowe, kashituwune, nmeyitsi ashuwotswere kashitúne» boeti.
Doonzo aap'onowere bínat b́meyitse fa'a jamwotssh bokeewi.
manoori sa'aton t'úwon tipimo kotiruwo dek'amt bogaawo bo atse b́mashi, manoor bínat b́maa ash jamwots bogúpeyi.
Maniyere hakon P'awlosnat Silasn b́mook dek'amt misho boosh b́t'intsi, Ik'onowere bí amantsosh b́meyitsi ashuwotsnton geneú b́wutsi.
B́ gatstsok'onowere naash naashuwots «Ash manots faksheewunee» ett polisuwotsi bowoshi.
Tipi maa kotfonuwere «It it faksheetuwok'o naash naashuwots asho bowoshtsotse eshe keer jeenon ameree» ett Silassh b́keewi.
P'awlosmó «Rom datsi ashnowotefere nayiralon jebatse noon jot't tipimoots noon kindshrnee. Andowere tipi mootse ááshon nokeshetuwok'owe bok'aliri? Woteratse! bo botookon waar noon kishunee!» ett bíaani.
Poliswots keewuman naash naashuwotssh bokeewi, naah naashuwotswere P'awlosnat Silasn Rom dats ashuwotsi bowoto bodantsok'on shatbowtsi.
Mansh waat naandrone ett aatt tipimootse boon kishbok'ri, kitmanitsnowere boametuwok'o boon bok'oni.
P'awlosnat Silasnowere tipi mootse kesht Lidiy moots bokindi, manoknowere eshu eshuwotsi daatsdek't boon kup'sht kitmanowere faksht k'azbo ami.
P'awlosnat Silasn Anfip'olisnat Ap'olon weeron beshat Teselonk'e maants boami, manoknowere ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni moo fa'ee b́teshi.
P'awlos maniyere shin b́ k'alfok'o ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni moots b́ kindi, keez gawuyiwoshowere b́k'ut'raawon S'ayin mas'aafotse ash ashosh kish kitsfetstni b́ danifo.
Krstos gond bek'o de'er k'irotse tuwo bín b́geyituwok'o kitsit danifetst «Taa itsh b́ jangosh doo tshishyiru Iyesus Krstosiye» bíetfera b́tesh.
Mann boyitse ik ikuwots b́ aap'o t'iwintsdek't P'awlosnat Silasnton ikbowoti, mank'owere Ik' Ik'iruwotswere aydek't ayts Ik'i ash woterawwots, kitutse daneets ay máátsuwots b́ aap'o t'iwintsdek't bínton ik bowoti.
Ayhudiwotsmó okoort fay tizitu fin deshawwotsi weer weeratse kakudek't tuuz bok'ri. Kitutse fayo b́tuwitwok'o bo woshi, P'awlosnat Silasn kishde'er ash ashosh imosh Iyason moo guurbodeki.
Ernmó boon bo t'ut'tsok'oon Iyasonnat amants ik ikuwotsi kitmanitsi naashuwotssh t'intsosh geetsfere dek't boami, hank'o etfetst bokuhiri boteshi, «Hanots datsjamo gaak rne ando hanok waarnee!
Iyasonwere boon dek't ibiree, ‹Iyesusi eteets k'osh nugúso fa'ee› ett Rom Naashi Naasho alo bok'efiri.»
Ash ashonat kitutsi naash naashuwots man boshishtsok'on dimbr bowutsi
Iyasonnat k'oshuwotsn wusho s'eegiyit fakshbokri.
Eshu eshuwots P'awlosnat Silasn káári t'úwon Bery maants bo amtuwok'o bowoshi, Manok bo bodtsok'on ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni moots bokindi.
Beriyan fa'a ayhudiyots Teselonk'en fa'wotsiyere bogo kááwu finek boteshtsotse b́ aap'o gene'úwi eenon bodek'i, b́ aap'o ar b́ wotok'o kitsosh aawu aawon S'ayn mas'afotsi bos'ilfoni.
Mansh boyitsere ayuwots boamani, ay Grik datsatsi gaaletswots máátswots ay Grik datsatsi nungushuwots boamani.
Ernmó Teselok'en fa'a ayhudiyots P'awlos Beriyon Ik'i keewuts keewo b́ nabiruwok'o bodantsok'on manoor waat ashuwotsi gondon tizt bowaac'rituwok'o botizi.
Manoor eshu eshuwots káári P'awlos aats k'ari ganok b́ ametuwok'o bowoshi Silasnat T'imotiyosnmó manoke Beriyon bo oori.
P'awlosi deents ashuwots Ateni bobetsi «Silasnat T'imotoyosn ja'araniye káári tiyok woonee» etiru P'awlos tzaziyo detsdek't Beriyo maants boaani.
P'awlos Atenon wotdek't Silasnat T'imotiyosn b́ kotfere kitutsere dozets ik'uwots bos'entsok'o b́bek'tsotse ayidek't nibo b́k'uni.
Mansh ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni mootse ayhudiyotsnat Ik'osh Ik'iru ashuwotsnton jebatse aawu aawon b́ daatsiru ashuwotsnton b́mooshiri b́tehi.
Epikorosotsnat Istokotsi eteets bog danetuwots b́ maants waatni bomooshfoni. Ik ikuwots «Ooshiyiruwan eeg etee b́geyi?» bo etor, k'oshuwotsmó «Handr ik'uwots janga arefee b́ keewiri? boetiri, man boetiruwere P'awlos Iyesusnat k'irotse b́tuwi doo shishi keewi jango b́ danitsoshe.
Mansh P'awlosi detsdek't Ariyosfagosi eteets beyokoke kakuwets ash ashok dek'wat bísh hank'o boeti, Nee ndaniyiru handr danan eeg b́wottsok'o dano falituwonowáá?
Ib wotts ik ik keewwotsi noosh shiyirnee, mansh keewanots eeg bowottsok'o dano geefone.»
Man etts Atenitse beyirwotsnat Atenitse beyiru úridatsi ash jamwots handr keewu keewonat k'eboke bogizeyo beshiyo boshunfotsne.
Manoor P'awlos Aryosfagosn kakweetswots shinatse need'dek't hank'o bíet, «Ateen ashuwotso! jam weeron ayidek'at ik'uwotsi shatiru itwottsok'o t'iwintsdek'at dandek're,
It kitotse gúúrat ananat it Ik' it ik'irwoko t s'iile ‹Danerawo Izar Izeweri› ett guut'etsoko wosh biyatse t'intseyiru t'arap'ezo daatsre, eshe taa and itsh t keewir it danawo bín it ik'iruwo Izar Izewer jangoniye.
Bíye Datsonat datsatse fa'a jamo aztsoniyee, Daronat datsonsh doonze, bíye ash kishon ageets Ik'i moots beerake,
Kashonat kash jongon, k'osh keewwotsnowere ash jamosh imfo bí b́wottsotse bísh eegor shaprake, asho bín b́ tep'onowere bísh geyiratse.
Bíye ash naar jamone ik ashaatse azree, dats jamatsnowere bo beetuwok'o woshre, tiitsets duruwotsnat beyokuwotsnowere boosh b́ beezi.
Man b́ k'aluwere ashuwots doonzo geeyar daatso bofalituwok'owe, b́wotiyalor bí no ik iketsatse woka etaliye.
‹Kasho daatsir nogiwit, Noo beetuwere bíne,› Manuwere itk wotts jááwetswots ‹Noo noúnets b́ nana' noone› bo ettsok'onee.
Eshe noo b́ nana'a nowotiyakon ‹Ik'o ash danon, hasabiyon awntson wee ambaron wee shútson dozets aroniye bíari› err gawo noosh geyiratse.
Eshe ashuwots yoots dúr dáron bok'altso Ik'o kabiraniyere k'az beshere, andomó dats datsatse fa'a ash jamwots naandrone boetetuwok'o azazere,
Bí b́marat'ts asho weeron dats jamatse arikon b́angshit aawo beezdek're, hanowere jametsosh daniyidek't b́bek'sh b́marat'ts ashman k'irotse b́tuztsotsnee.»
«K'irotse tuuwa» etiru aap'o boshishtsok'on ik ikuwots bín boaatsni, k'oshuwotsmó «Han jango k'osh aawots nkeewure k'ebetuwonee» boeti.
Maniyere hakon P'awlos kakuwets ashuwotsoke kesht k'az bíami,
Ash ik ikuwotsmó bínton ik wotat boamani, amants ashuwotsitsnowere Aryosfagosn kakuwetsuwotsitso Diyonasyosi eteets ashonat Demarisi eteets mááts ikunu, k'oshuwotswere boyitse fa'ano.
Maniyere hakon P'awlos Atenitse tuut K'orontosi bíami,
Manoke P'ant'os datsatse shuwek wottso Ak'ili eteetso Ayhudi ash iko b́daatsi, Rom naashi naasho K'elawudiwos Ayhudi jamo Romitse bokeshetuwok'o azazat b́ teshtsotse Ak'il b́ máátsu P'rsk'lntoon It'aaliyitse manoora b́waa, mann P'awlos book amt bonton b́daneyi,
B́fiino ari bokok'o dunkani shipo b́teshtsotse bonton towaat beedek'tn b́fiinefo.
Sanbati aaw aawonowere ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni mootse datseyar mooyr ayhudiwotsnat Grik dats ashuwots keewman bo dek'etwok'o b́wooshfoni.
Silasnat T'imotiwosn Mek'odonitse bowatsok'on P'awlos «Iyesusye Mesihyoniye» eton ayhudiwotssh kup'dek't gawefetst daniyoke bíaawu jamo b́beshifoni b́tesh.
Ernmó bín k'efat boc'ashor b́ tahatsi k'úndo tebatt «Eshe itats angsheyal it took t'afiyonee! taan bítse aateratse, haniyak Ik' ash woterawwotsok k'ay ametuwe!» bí eti.
Mann boatse k'aleyat Titos Iyost'osi eteets asho mook k'azbiami, ashaan Ik'o Ik'if asha b́tesh, b́moonwere ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni mooniyere beshaatni b́tesh.
K'ersp'osi eteefo ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni maa jishiruwo b́meytsi ash jamonton Doonzo bíamani, ay K'orontos ashuwotswere P'awlos b́ keewufere shisht amanat bogúpeyi.
Doonzonuwere t'ú bek'on P'awlossh hank'o bíeti, «Shatk'aye, keewwe, s'k etk'aye,
Taaye neentonye tfa'oni, kitanitsere ay asho tdetstsotse gondo niyats betsosh falituwo konuworu aaliye.»
Mansh P'awlos Ik' aap'o ashuwotssh danifere ik natonat badosh manoke b́teshi.
Galiyos Akayiya datso altsi wotat b́ naashor ayhudiyots ik wotdek't P'awlosats botuwi, angshituwots shinatso bín dek'amt,
«Ashaan Muse nemo b́ k'efts weratse ashuwots Ik'o bo ik'ituwok'o b́ woshiri!» boeti.
P'awlos boosh aaniyosh k'andek't b́befere Galyos ayhudiwotssh hank'owa bíet, «It Ayhudi jirwotso! itats gondo wee weralo finere wotink'ere it t'intsts s'aamiyo k'amde tk'ebank'oni b́teshi,
Ernmó aap'uwotsnat shúts jango it nemi jangosha it mooshiri wotiyal man it took kis'e, taa keewanotsats angshosh geeratse.»
Hank'o ett moosh mooshiruwoke boon b́kishi.
Manoor jamwots ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni maa jishiruwo Sostensn detsdek'et angishiruwots shinatse boojot'i, jaman b́wotefere Galyos kis'odeshatse.
P'awlos eshuwotsnton ay aawosh K'orontosi b́teshiyakon jamiyere Soriyo maants bíami, P'irsk'lnat Ak'iln bíntoni boteshi, ernmó wosho b́detstsotse bíamoniyere shinon Knkiriya eteyiru datsatse b́tooko b́ s'ageyi.
Efesoni bobodtsok'ono P'rsk'lonat Ak'ilon manoke oori bok'ri, bímó Ayhudi Ik' k'oni moots kindt ayhudiyotssh keewo b́ keewufoni.
Ay aawosh bonton b́teshetuwok'o bok'oniyalor eekeratse.
Ernmó «Ik'o bí eteetka wotiyal k'oshoor itok aanarr weetuwe» etk'raat Efesonitsere markabots kinddek't k'azbíami.
K'isarimaantsowere b́bodtsok'on maniyere Iyerusalem maants kesht Ik'i meyitsi ashuwotssh jamo b́ t'intsiyakon aanat Ans'okiyi maants k'az b́ oot'i.
Manoknowere muk'i b́teshi, maniyere hakon Gelatiynat Frgiy datsatse ikoke tuut ikok gúúrefetst amantsuwotsi b́ kup'iyi.
Iskndri datsatse shuwetso Ap'losi eteets Ayhudi asho Efesoni b́weyi, bí S'ayin mas'aafwotsi t'iwintsdek't dankoonat noon keewonowere sheengshdek't keewo falk asha b́tesh.
Doonzo weerindi jangonowere dandek't S'ayin shayronowere aat'k wotat Iyesus jangonowere kaatsdek' nabfetst b́danifoni, wotowa eree bí b́danfo Yohans gupo s'uzi b́tesh.
Bí ááwushuk'on ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni mootse keewo dek't b́tuwi, ernmó P'rsk'ilnat Ak'iln b́ keewiruwo boshishtsok'on bo gal dek'amt Ik'i weero baltsoniyere bogo kaatsdek bitsdek't bísh bokitsi.
Ap'los Akayiyo maants amoosh b́gawtsok'oon eshuwots b́keewuman botep'i, Akayiyitse fa'a eshuwots bí sheengon de'er boibituwok'o work'atats guut'ets wosho woshbok'ri, manok b́bodtsok'oonowere Ik'i s'aaton amantsuwotsi wotosh bodtswotsi ayidek' b́ tep'i.
Iyesus Mesihiyo b́wotsok'o S'ain mas'afwotsitse Ik' aap'o biitsdek' keewut kup'ts mooshon ayhudiwotsi b́ da'afoni.
Ap'los K'orontositse b́teshor P'awlos danbani datson beshat Efeson maants b́bodi, manokno muk' Krstaniyotsi daatsdek't
«It amanor S'ayn shayiro dek'rteya b́teshi?» ett bíaati. Bowere «De'atsone, S'ayn shayiro b́beyonoru dab shish danaak noone» ett bo aani.
P'awlosu «Eshe aawu naari gúpe it gúpetsoni?» bí eti. Bowere «Yohanis gúponiye» boeti.
P'awloswere «Yohans guponiyere naandrone etosh k'aleke, ash ashosh b́keewutsonuwere ‹Taayere il wetuwonee amanore› etfetstni b́tesh, bíwere Iyesusiye» etreboosha.
Man boshishtsok'on Doonzo Iyesus shútson bogupeyi.
P'awlosu b́ kisho boats b́gedor S'ayin shayiro boats b́ od'eehandr noon keewon bokeeweyi, bek'ono keewo dek'tbotuwi.
Ash jamwotswere tatse gitne boteshi.
P'awlos ayhudiyots Ik' k'oni mook amt keez shashok'owosh Ik' mengst jangosh mooshfetst ash ashuwotssh kish keewut ááwu shuk'ona b́ danifoni.
Ik ikuwotsmó maac' kup'o wotat doonzo weerindo ashuwots shinatse c'ashfetst amaneratsone boettsosh boatse k'azb́woki, amantsuwots boaali T'iranosi eteef maa eenok dek'amt aawu aawon boon b́danifoni.
P'awlos hank'o b́k'al git natok'osha, manoor Isiy datsatse beyiru ayhudiyotsnat Ik' ashwoterawwotsn doonzo aap'o shisho bofali.
Ik'o ayidek't adits keewu wotts milikituwotsi P'awlos kishon b́finefoni.
Manatse tuutson P'awlos atsats bodts tahonat marabon dek'amt shodetsuwotsats bobetsor boshodotse bokashefoni, kim shayirwotswere boyitse bokeshfoni.
Fo'erawono ashaatse kishfetst ikoke tuut ikok guuriru Ayhudi ik ikuwots «P'awlos b́ nabiruwo doonzo Iyesus shútson it kesheetuwok'o iti azazerone» eton fo'erawo ashaatse kishosh bo etfoni.
Ayhudiwots kahinwotsatsi naasho wottso Ask'ewu nana'a shawatuwotswere mank'owa bok'alfo.
Ernmó kim shayiro «Iyesusi danfee! P'awlosnor danfee! Eshe it konots itne?» bí eti.
Kim shayiro bíatse s'eents ash ikonwere t'oolat gúúk' dek'on boats b́kup'i, bonowere da'ab́dek'i, gaawutnuwere araatswtsaat meyitse giifat bokeshi.
Keewumanuwere Efesonitse beyiru ayhudiwotsnat Ik' ash woterawotsoke b́ shishetsotse jametso shatb́wtsi, Doonzo Iyesus shútsonowere ayi eenb́wutsi.
Amantsuwotsitse ayuwotsuwere bogond fino kish keewut naandrone err bowaafoni.
Atetswotswere bodaniyi mas'aafwotsi kakudek't ash ashi shinatse mitsbok'ri, mas'afmanoots k'awuntsonuwere taanere balk'ats kum ambari katso wotatni b́daatsiyi.
Mank'oon doonzo keewo ayidek't gawunfetst da'afera bí amfo b́teshi.
Jaman b́wotiyakon P'awlos Mek'edonitsnat Akayiyiweeron beshat Iyerusalem maants amoosh b́gitsoon gawuk'rat «Manok t bodiyakon Rom maants amo taash geyife» bíetí.
Mann Ik'i fino finiru ashuwotsitse gitetsuwotsi, T'imotiwosnat Erast'osn Mek'edoni maants woshat bí b́tookon Isiyi datsatse muk' aawosh b́teshi.
Manoor doonzo weeri jangosh Efesonitse dimbiro tuub́wtsi.
Dimet'rosi eteef ambaar wos'if iko Art'emisn ik' maa aro ambaron doozt ambaar wos'iyiruwotssh ay oot'o b́daatsifoni.
Mansh ashaan ambaar wos'iyiruwotsnat bo fini naari fin detsts k'osh ashuwtsi kakudek't boosh hank'o bí eti «It ashuwotso! Noo gaalo nodaatsir finan finat b́wottsok'o danfte,
P'awlosan ‹Ash kishon dozets aranots Izar Izewerotsiyaliye› ett Efeson s'uzitse b́woterawo muk' datsuniyere okoon Isiyi dats jamatse awuk'o ayts ashonton keweek'rat bí amanitsok'o it it tookon bek'aat it shishtsoniye.
Eshe hank'on nofino b́ gac'ewoniye, manmec'ro b́woterawon Isiyotsnat dats jamatse ash jamo bin b́ ik'yiru een izar izewer Art'emis Ik'i moo dats baashon b́ ooroniye, bi een wotonwere b́wonewoniyee.»
Ashuwotswere man boshishtsk'on fayat, «Efesontsu Art'emisiye eeniye!» etfetst bokuhi.
Kitunuwere jamon shek'e bwutsi, ashuwotswere Mek'odoni datsatse shuwets P'awlosnton tohaat sha'iru b́ tooh gituwots Gayyosnat Arst'rokosn detsdek't geetsfere ash ashuwots bokoeyiruwok bowos'i.
P'awloswere ashuwotsok amoosh geyatni b́tesh, b́ danifuwotsmó bíamawok'o bobazi.
Isiy datsatsi naashuwotsitswere b́shuntsuwotsitsi ik ikuwotsi P'awlosok asho woshat «Ashuwots ko'eyiruwok amr n be'erawok'owa» ett bok'oni.
Ashuwots dagotse wac'ro b́teshtsotse aywots eegosh bokoetsok'o dab danatsno b́teshi, man jangosh iko ik keewo keewt b́kuheere k'oshonuwere k'osh keewo keewut b́kuhiri.
Ik ik Ayhudi jirwots Iskndiri eteets asho ash dagotsere gifnidek't shinats bot'ntsi, ashuwotsitse ik ikuwots sheengshde'ere b́moshetuwok'o boizi, Iskendiruwere ashuwots s'k boetetuwok'o b́kishon kitst bín kishit keewosh k'anb́dek'i.
Ernmó Iskendr Ayhudi b́wotok'o ash jamwots bodantsok'on «Efesontsu Art'emis eeniye!» et fetst git sa'atok'osh ik k'aaron bokuhi.
B́s'uwatse kitutsi guut'f naash eeno, ash asho s'k boaayituwok'o wosht hank'o bíeti, «It Efeson ashuwotso! Efeson kitutse beyiruwots, eenu Art'emis ik' moonat darotse oot'ts bí'aro bokotetuwok'owo jametsuwotsoke daneke.
Han haalitwo konuwor bíaaltsotse s'k it eteetuwok'o, kááronowere gond keewo k'aloniyere it atso kor itdek'tuwok'o geyife.
Ik'i moo c'ayawotsnat noko Izar Izeweri c'ayawu gond keewono keewuraw ashuwotsi hanok dek'at waartee.
Dimet'rosnat bínton fa'a k'is' k'is'fuwotsi s'aamiru asho b́beyalowere angsh imet aawwots fa'ane, naashuwotsuwere fa'ane, manoke mooynee.
K'osho it geyiru keewo b́beyaalmó nemon k'oorosh beyiruwotsn s'iiletuwe.
Maniyere okoonmó hambets k'aleets keewo ‹Dimbiro tuuzre› err no s'aamirawok'owa shatituwe, ‹Baad'eyan eegatsneya b́tuwi› err noon aatewor no aaniyituwo deshatsone»
Dimbro b́ neediyakon P'awlos amantsuwotsi ikok s'eegt izon boon b́kup'iyi, boon jamik'ratnuwere Mek'edoni eteets datso maantsan bíami.
B́ beshiru datsmanotsatsno amantsuwotsi ay izon kup'ifere Grik datso maants bíami.
Manokno keez shasho b́ teshi, maniyere hakon markabon Soriy datso maats amoosh b́gawi, ayhudiyitsmó bín fayosh botutsok'o b́dantsotse Mek'edoni weeron anoosh k'ut'b́dek'i.
P'irhus naay Sop'at'ros Beriyotse, Arst'rokosnat Sikondusn Teselonk'en, Gayyosn Derben, T'imotiwos, Tikik'osnat T'rofimosn Isiyon bínton tohaat boami.
Bowere shin shino amt T'iroadn noon bokoti.
Noomó tush meyet baalio b́ beshiyakon Filp'isyusitse Markabats keshat úúts aawon bo bobeyiruwok T'iro'adayits bodat bíyokere shawat aawo nobeshyi.
Torbanotsere shnts aawots misho tishde'er iknon moowosh nokakweyi, P'awlos yats gúrok'on bíametwootse ko'ets ashuwotssh b́ keewiri, b́ keewono talitiitso b́borfetso b́geezi.
No no ko'ets dadratse ay c'eesho fa'e b́teshi.
Ewut'ek'isi eteets jawets na'iko meskotiyatse beedek'tniye b́ teshi, P'awlos b́ keewo b́ geezitsotse jawetsman tokri eeno detsb́dek'i, tokro bín b́ datsotse keezl dadratsere dashan b́dihi, ashuwots bok'awere k'irt b́datseyi.
Ernmó P'awlos oot't na'ats tuumt matdek't «And kashone b́ fa'oni bíeti, tek'k'ayere!» bí eti.
P'awlos dadrats aani kesh waat misho tiitsdek't amantsuwotsnton b́meyi, datso b́gatsfetsosh ashuwotsnton keewefetst b́teshiyakon k'azbíami.
Ashuwotswere kashts jawetso moots dek'boami, mannowere ayidek't kup'bowutsi.
P'awlosi markabots kindshosh nogawutsatse noo shinat markabots Asosits noami, man nok'aluwere P'awlos Asosits b́borfetso b́ tufoon amoosh bí ettsosh hank'o no k'alituwok'o noon b́ azaztsotsne.
Bínton Asositse nogonkewor markabots bín kindshdek' milit'its maants towaat noami.
Yaats guurok'on manoke tuwat Kiyositse shinatse fa'a datsuwats markabon amnobodi, yaatsok'o Samos maants kimaat yaats guurok'on Milit'iyits amnobodi.
P'awlos Isiyotse t teyawok'wa ett Efesoniyere beshat k'ay amo b́ geyi, man b́ k'aluwere P'ent'ek'ost'yi baaliyo Iyerusalemitse daatseyo gawut b́teshtsotsna b́tesh.
P'awlos Milit'itsere Efeson maants asho woshat Ik'i maa eenashuwotsi b́ s'eegiyi,
Bíyok bowatsok'on boosh hank'o bíeti, «Isiyots tkindts aawotstson tuut jam aawo itnton awuk'o tbeetsok'o itwoor danfte,
Ayhudiwots tiats bo malts k'od'atse tuutson gondbek'o tiats b́bodaloru ttooko dashan detsonat eeponee doonzo fino t finefoni.
Jebatsnowere it maa mootsnowere itsh tdaniyor itsh t'ak'amitu jamoni tkeewi bako eegoru itsh t shapitso aaliye.
Ayhudiyotsi wotowa Ik' ash woterawwots naandrone err Ik'o maants bo aanituwok'o doonzo Iyesus Krstosi bo amanituwok'oye b́gawi.
Andoor bíyok tbodor tiyats bodetwo eeg b́wto t dartsotse s'ayn shayirosh aleyat Eyerusalem maats ti amoniye.
Wotowa eree kit kitotse tipewonat gond bek'on taan b́kotiruwok'o S'ayin shayiro taash keewure.
Doo shishi keewo Ik' s'aaton daniyosh doonzo Iyesusoke t k'aaútdek'ts fino tishink'ere t kashi jango k'awuntsots gerawunk'e, t kashoshowere kis'o deshawnk'e.
«Andish b́borfetso it jamets dagotse ananat Ik'i mengsti jango t nabiri, haniyere okonomó ititsere konuworu t shiitso b́ jamon b́ be'awok'o danfee.
Mansh ititsere ikdonzworu b́t'afiyal b́ s'atsotse taan aaterawok'o hambets aawon itsh danirwe.
Ik'o bí'asabts jamo itsh keewuni tishi bako eegoru t oorits keewo aaliye.
S'ayn shayiro jintswotsi woshdek't iti naashire, eshe it tokonat it jiniru gizi s'eeni jangosh it atso korde'ere, Ik'o b́ naay s'atson keewudeb́k'ts Ik'i moo korere.
Taa ti amiyakon gizi s'eenosh máác' k'ewerawo elahok'o maac' kup' wotts ashuwots bits bokindituwok'o danfee.
Mank'owore ash ik ikwots ititse tuur k'úúr daniyo daniyir ayi amantsuwotsi bomaants geetsitune.
Eshe it ik iketsi keez natosh t'úwonat aawon ti aac'uwo kuut'fetsat itn ti'iztsok'o gawufetsr itatso korde'ere.
«Andoor iti kup'shr S'ayinwots dagotse rstiyo imosh falitu b́s'aati aap'onshowere adaro iti imre.
Taa kon ambaaronowere, awntsonowere wee taho tewunratse.
T took kishon finefetsat ttooko wotowa ttohuwotsi t tep'fok'o it tookon danfte.
‹Dek'iruwoniyere bogo imiruwo deereke› etiru doonzo Iyesus aap'tso gawufetsr, nokishon angmaawtswotsi tep'o noosh b́ geyituwok'o ay weerindon itsh kitsre.»
Maniyere hakon P'awlos jametsuwotsnton tuk'maldek't Ik'o b́k'oni.
Jametsuwots eept P'awlosi matdek't bojoobi.
Dabtnu aydek't shiyanatnuwere, «Haniyak tshitso be'atste» boosh bí'ettsatse tuutsone, Markabok b́ borfetsosho bín bodeni.
Boo'atse nok'aleyakon Markabats keshdek'at kawon K'osi eteets ats k'aron gúrts datsuk noami, yats gúúrok'on Rúdi eteets ats k'aron gúrts datsuk nobodi, manokno P'at'ray eteets kitots no'ami.
Manokno Fink'e datso maants amiru Markabu daatsat bíyats keshdek'at sha'osh notuwi.
K'op'ros aats k'aron gúrts datsu nogiro maants k'azk'rat Sori datso maants amaat Tiros aats k'ari gúroki datsuk no'ami, markabunwere bkuro manok orsho bín geyfe bteshi.
Manokere amantsuwotsi geeyat nodatsiyakon bonton shawat aawosh manoke noteshi. Bowere S'ayn shayiron jisheyat P'awlossh «Iyerusalem maants amk'aye» ett bokeewi.
Manoke no ja'ats aawman b́ s'uwutsok'on boatse k'aleyat sha'o notuwi, jametsuwotsuwere bomááts máátsonat bonana'uwotsnton wotat kitoniyere nokeshfetso noon bodeni, aats k'ari gúrats tuk'maldek'at Ik'o no k'oniyakon nok'aleyi.
No jamiyakon no markabots no nokindre bo bomoo maants k'az bo aani.
T'rositse tuwat P'et'elemays maants nobodi, manokno amantsuwotsnton gonkeyat jamo no'ateyakon bonton ik aawo nojini.
Yaats guurok'on manokere keshat K'isariyo maants no'ami, bíyokno shawat Dak'oniyotsitsere ik wottso doo shishiyo nabiruwo Filp'os meyits kindat bínton nobeyi.
Bíwere bek'on keewo boosh imets awd baar nana'a mááts amawwotsi detsfe b́teshi.
Ay aawosh manokere nobemanoor Agabosi eteets Nebiyo Yhud datsatse b́weyi.
Nebiyanuwere nook t'int, P'awlos edo k'aaúdek't b́ took kishonat b́tufuwotsi tipt «S'ayin shayiro eedan doonzi Iyerusalemn fa'a ayhudiyots hank'o tifde'er Ik' ash woterawwotssh beshide'er imetune etfe» bí eti.
Man noshishtsok'on noowere manoke fa'a ashuwotswere P'awlos Iyerusalem maants bíamawok'o nok'oni.
P'awlosmó «Hank'o eepat eegishe tnibo shiyanon it tiitsiri? Taa doonzo Iyesus shúts jangosh Iyerusalemitse tipee mec'r b́woterawo k'irosh k'andek'ktaane» ett bíaani.
Bo izono de'atse bíere «Beree doonzo bíettsok'o wotowe» etaat k'aznok'iri.
Manokno muk' aawwotssh noteshiyakon nok'ac'o k'anidek'at Iyerusalem maants noami.
K'isariyitse fa'a amants ik ikuwots noonton tohaat boweyi, boowere Mnason meyts nokashdek'etwok'o b́moo maants noon bojishi, ashaamanwere shini amantso K'op'ros datsatse shuweke b́teshi.
Iyerusalemits nobodtsok'on amantsuwots geneúwon noon bodek'i.
Yaats guurok'on P'awlos noonton Yak'obok bíami, Ik'i maa eenash jamwots manokna botesh.
P'awlos jametsuwotsi jamo b́aatiyakon b́weeron Ik'o Ik' ashwoteraw ashuwotsitse b́k'alts jamo ik ikon b́ keewi.
Man boshishtsok'on jametsuwots doonzo boúdi, P'awlosshowere hank'o boeti, «Eshuwonoo! ay kumon taawetu amantsuwots ayhudiwotsitse bo beyiruwok'onat jametsuwotswor bo nemosh okooretsuwotsi bowottsok'o danfnee,
Nee Ik' ash Woteraw ashuwotsitse beyiru ayhudiyi jamwotssh ‹It nanaúwotsi gofo damik'ayere wee nemok'o fink'ayere› etaat daniyat Muse nemo b́ gahituwok'o nk'aliri ett keeweyirwo bo shishrne.
Eshe eeg k'ale b́ geyiyiti? n woono arikon shishrne,
Eshe no no'etetuwo k'aluwe, noyitse wosho detsts awd ashuwots fa'ane.
Boon de'amr bonton wotar ntooko s'ayintsuwe, botook s'iiro bos'agetuwok'o Ik' moosho imet mebi gizono nee boosh daye, hank'o n k'aliyal níats keewets jamo k'awuntsalk b́wottsok'onat neewere n tookon Muse nemosh alek nwottsok'o jametsuwots danetunee.
Ik' ashwoterawwots jirwotsitse amantsuwotsmó Woteraw ik'osh b́ t'intsotse kiimts woshi misho maak'ayere, s'atsonowere maak'ayere, guuk'at k'irts gizi meetso maak'ayere, widats wokoore ett guutt'eets keewu detsts woshi work'ato guut'dek'at itsh wosherone.»
Maniyere hakon P'awlos ashuwotsi dek'amt yaats guurok'on b́tooko b́s'ayintsi, bos'ayinet aawwots awur bo s'uwitwok'onat ik ikuwots jangoshowere Ik'osh imet mabi gizo b́ dashet gizwo awur b́wottsok'o daniyosh Ik'i moots b́kindi.
Shawt aawu manu beshosh b́t'intsk'on Isiyon waats ayhudiyots P'awlosi Ik'i mootse bobek'tsosh ash jamo bíyats tizt bín bodetsi,
«Israe'el ashuwotso! noosh gaatsowere! no ashonat no nemon, beyokanowere c'ashfetst dats datsatsi ash jamonowere daniruwo ashaaniye, hanuwere boratse ett Ik' ash woteraw ashuwotsi Ik' moots kindsht s'ayin beyokan k'imhsre!» ett bokuhi.
Hano boetuwere maniyere shin Efesonn shuwetso T'rofimos bínton kitotse bek't boteshtsoosh P'awlos bín Ik' moots dek't b́kindtsok'o boosh bíarernee.
Kit jamunwere dimbir bwutsi, ash jamonuwere wos'fere ikwotdek't waat P'awlosi detsdek't geetsfere Ik'i mootse bokishi, Ik'i maa fengeshuwotswere iknun is'ebowutsi.
Ashuwots P'awlosi úd'osh bogeetsok'on «Iyerusalem kitu bjamoon dimbir bwutsi» etiru wosho Rom datsatsi kes' naashok b́bodi.
Mansh bí kes'fuwotsnat bali naashuwotsi b́shuutsats jishdek't ashuwots maants kaari wos'fere bíami. Ashuwotswere kes'fuwotsnat boon jishiruwon bobek'tsok'on P'awlosi jot'o k'azbok'iri.
Jishiruwonuwere P'awlosok t'int detsdek't git habliyon b́tipetuwok'o bíazazi, maniyere hakon koni b́wottsok'onat eeg b́k'altsok'owo danosh geeyat bíaati.
Ash ashonwere ik ikwots ik keewo boere k'oshuwotsuwere k'osh keewa boetfera botesh, azazirumanwere ash ash kuhatse tuutson ari keewo dano b́maawtsotse P'awlosi kes' kes'fuwots kot bokotiru gimbiyok de'er boametuwok'o bí azazi.
P'awlos bíyats need'dek' dambaan kesheyirwok b́bodtsok'on ash jamo ayidek't b́faytsatse tuutson gondo biats betsosh bogeyiruwosh kes' kes'fuwots bín kurdek't k'azboami.
Ash ashonwere «Bín úd'ewe» etfere b́shuutso bosha'i.
Kes' kes'fuwots bo koti gimbiyok bín kindshosh bot'intsok'on P'awlos kes'iruwots abaatse alirwoh «Ik keewo neesh t keewituwok'o eekituneya taasha?» bí eti. Altsmanuwere «Grik dats noon keewu keewo danfiya? bí eti.
Eshe, and karnon fayo tizat awd kum kash úd'tswotsi woruwo maants dek't t'afts Gbs' asho nenalneya?»
P'awloswere «Taa Kilk'iyitse fa'a daneek wotts T'erses kitutse shuwets Ayhudi ash taane, oona neesha ashuwotssh t keewituwok'o taash eekowe» bí eti.
B́ keewituwok'o b́ ektsok'on P'awlos bíyatsneedeyiruwats need'dek't ash ashuwots s'ik boetetuwok'o b́kali, ash asho s'ik boettsok'on Ibrayist'iyi noon keewon hank'o ett keewo dek'btuwi.
«Ti eeshuwotsnat tnihotso! eshe and itsh tt'intsiru aani tdek'etuwo tiko k'ewere!»
Ibrayist'i noon keewu keewon b́ keewufere boshishtsok'on iki s'k etbowtsi, P'awloswere b́keewiru keewo b́ need'irawo hank'o bí eti.
«Taa Kilk'iyitse daatseyiru T'erses kitotse shuwets ayhudiwi taane, tieenmó Iyerusalem Kitmanitsne. Taan danifonuwere Gemalyailiye b́teshi, nih nihwots nemono shengshdek'at danre, hambets it k'aliruwank'o Ik'osh ookorona tfinefoni.
Krstni imneti shuuts sha'iryiru jamwotsi k'irosh borfetso t gishfoni, nungushuwotsnat máátsuwotsn tifde'er tipi moots bokindituwok'o twoshfoni.
Manuwere ar b́wottsok'o kahni naashonat eenashuwots taash gawitune. Eshe Demask'on fa'a ashaanotsi tifde'er Iyerusalem maants dewar boon Seziyosh taan falituwo Demask'on fa'a jirwotsoke guut'ets worek'ato tdek'iye boowokne.
«Taa Demask'o maants amfetsat kituk tt'infere aawu taalon t gawuraniyere een shááno darotse t gúratse b́goli.
Manoor dattsats dihi twutsi, ‹Sawulo! Sawulo! eegishe taan ngishiri?› etiru k'aaro tshshi.
Taawere ‹Doonzono! kone nee?› t eti, bíwere ‹Taahe nee ngishiruwo Nazrettso Iyesus taane› bí eti.
Taanton beyiru ashuwotswere shaanmani bobek'i bako taan b́keewiyor b́k'aaro shiyatsne.
Taawere ‹Doonzono! eeg k'aluta!› t eti. Doonzonuwere ‹Tuur Demask'o maants amee, k'alo neen b́geyit keewu jamo manoke neesh keewetuwe› bí eti.
Shanman goltsatse tuutson bek'o tfalrawotse taanton teshts ashuwots tkisho detsdek't taan jishfere Demask'oyi bobetsi.
«Manoke Hananiy eteef ash iko fa'e b́teshi, Demask'oyitse beyiru Ayhudi jamwotsoke udetso, Muse nemo kottsonat shayiri ashe b́teshi.
Bí waat t ganok need' dek't ‹Tieshu Sawulo! ni'aawo aani be'e!› taash bíeti, manorun tiaawo b́ bek'i, bínowere tbek'i.
Bíwere hank'o taash bíeti, ‹Nonihotsko Izar Izeweriye bíettso ndanetuwok'o kááwono be'er b́k'aronowere nshishetwok'o shin shino neen marat'ere,
Man b́k'aluwere bín bek'aat nshishtsotse ash jami shinatse bísh gawu nwotishe.
Eshe and eebi nkotiri? tuur b́shútso s'eer gúpeyowe, nmorratsnowere mashowe.›
«Maniyerehakon Iyerusalem maants aanat Ik'i mootse Ik'o tk'onfere tgitsotse t'iwintson bek'o tbek'i.
Doonzonwere taash be'eyat ‹Nee t jangosh n imet gawo bode'awotse nja'arawo káári Iyerusalemitse kee› bí eti
Taawere hank'o tieti, ‹Doonzono! Ayhudi Ik' k'oni maa mootse neen amants jamwotsi t tiptsok'onat tjot'tsok'o bo botookon danfnee.
N gawu teshtso Ist'ifanos úd'ewor taawere ttookon úd'iruwots ganok need'dek'at bonton keewumanats shiyeyatniye tteshi, botaahono tekotfere b́teshi,›
Doonzonuwere ‹Wokooke fa'a Ik' ash Woteraw ashuwotsok neen twoshitwotse tuur amee!› bí eti.»
Han b́ borfetsosh ash jamwots P'awlos keewiru keewo bok'ebfere boteshi, maniyre hakon bok'aaro eenshdek't, «Hank'o ashaan datsatse t'afuwe! hank'o ashaan kashon beyo bísh geyiratse!» ett bokuhi.
Bowere kuhefetst botaho shap'fetst shawono darots bobad'ri.
Altsonuwere man b́bek'tsok'on P'awlosi kes' kes'fuwots galots bokindshituwok'o bíazazi, ash ashonwere eegosh hank'o bíats bokúhiruwok'o danosh jod'fetsr aatetuwok'o bíazazi.
Ernmó shaak'on tifde'er jot'osh bok'anefere P'awlos b́ganoke need'iru bali naashosh «Rom dats ash iko tafiyalo njot'etuwok'o neesh faletuwá?» bí eti.
Bali naashonuwere han b́shishtsok'on alirwok amt «Eeg k'alishe? Ashaan Rom datsi ashe!» bí eti.
Mansh alirwo P'awlos maants t'int «Ab taash keewwe, nee Rom datsatsi ashneneya?» bíeti, bíwere «Ee taane» bí eti.
Azazefonuwere «Rom dats ashok'o taaweyosh ay gize tkishi» bíet, P'awloswere «Taayere Rom dats asho woto tdaats shuweyonee» bí eti.
Mansh bín aatosh k'andek't teshts ashuwots manoor bíyatse k'azbowoki, azazirwonuwere Rom dats asho habliyon b́tipo danb́k'rtsok'on shatb́wtsi.
Yaatsok'on azaziruwo, ayhudiwots P'awlosi bos'amitso arikon eegosh b́wottsok'o dano b́geyi, mansh kahni naashuwotsnat mooshiruwotsitsi jamwots bokakuweetuwok'o bí azazi, P'awlosnowere bits dek'amt boshinaats bí t'intsi.
P'awlos moosheyiruwok kakuweetsuwotsi t'iwintsdek't s'iilt «Ti eshuwotso! hambetsish b́ borfetso jam aawo Ik'i shinatse sheeng beyon tbeetsok'o t nibon danfee» bí et.
K'eesi naasho Hananiyimó P'awlos noono botogetuwok'o P'awlos ganoke need'iru ashuwotsi bíazazi.
Manoor P'awlos Hananiyish, «Nee nooron futets maa dir artsono! nenowere Ik'o togetuwee! nemok'on tjangosh angshosh beedek'atniya nemalon taan botogetuwok'o niazaziri?»
Manoke teshts ashuwots P'awlossh «Ik'i kahniwots naashoneya nc'shiri?» boeti.
P'awloswere «Ti eshuwotso! kahaniwotsatsi naasho b́wottsok'o danatse b́teshi, manwere eegoshe ‹Ni ashaatsi naashatse gondo aap'k'aye› etiruwo guut'ere» bí eti.
P'awloswere manoke fa'a ashuwotsitse k'atsuwots Seduk'awiya etetsuwotsi k'atsuwotswere feresawi etefuwotsi bo wotok'o dant «Ti eshuwotso! taa feresawi etetswotsatse feresawi taane, hamb! and angsheyiruwo tt'iniye noosh jangit imets k'irotse tuwi jangoshe» ett b́ k'aaro eenshdek't mooshiruwots taalotse b́ keewi.
P'awlos han b́ keewutsok'on feresawiyotsnat Seduk'awiya eteefuwots dagotse fayo tuut mooshiruwotsi gitok kay b́k'ri.
Seduk'awiya eteefuwots «K'irotse tuwo aaliye, melakiywotswere aalne shayironwere aaliye» boere feresawiyotsmó «Jamanots fa'ane» ettniye boamanefo.
Manoor dimbri eeno wotb́wtsi, ferisawi jirwotsitse ik ik nem danifuwots tuwut «Noo ashaanatse eegoru gond keewo daatsratsone, Shayro wee melakiyo bísh keewure b́wotiti, no eegoru danatsone?» ett bomooshi.
Fyonuwere kup'efere bíame ashuwots P'awlosn yec' yec'ay tiish ishitune ett shatt azaziruwo «Od'er P'awlosi ashuwots dagotse kishde'er woowere! kes'fuwots galots dek' boami!» et wotaderwotsi bíazazi.
Yatsok'ono t'úwun doonzo P'awlos ganok need'dek't «Shenono! Iyerusalemn taash n gawutsok'o, mannk'o Romits taash gawo neen geyituwe» bí eti.
Datso b́ gatstsok'on ayhudiyots kakuweewutsat «P'awlosn noo úd'raniyere mááyo máárátsone, aatsono úyatsone» ett botaareyi.
Malaanats shiyeets ashuwots taawonwere haboniyere bogfno boteshi.
Bowere kahni naashuwotsnat eenashuwotsok amt hank'o ett boosh bokeewi «P'awlosi nó úd'raniyere maayo nonots nogerawok'o kup'shdek'at taareerone,
Mansh it mooshiruwotsnton shiyede'er kúp'de'er bín it aatit keewok'o aride'er P'awlosi itsh bodewetuwok'o azaziruwo aatuwere, noowere hanok b́ boraftsere shinon úd'osh k'andek'rone.»
Ernmó P'awlos mish naay mal man b́shishtsotse kes' kes'fuwots galots amkindt P'awlossh b́keewi.
P'awloswere bali naashuwotsitse iko s'eegdek't «Na'an kes' azaziruwosh b́keewit keewo b́detstsotse bíyokde'er t'ine» bí eti.
Bali naashonuwere na'aman azaziruwok dek' kindt «Tipetso P'awlos taan s'eegt na'an neesh b́keewit keewo b́detstsotse niyok t t'intsituwok'o taan b́k'oni» bí eti.
Azaziruwonuwere na'o kisho detsdek't okaan dek'amt, «Taash nkeewituwo eebi?» ett bíaali bíaati.
Na'onuwere hank'o bíeti, «Ayhudiwots P'awlos keewo katsidek' k'ebiruwok'o araat yaats mooshiruwots shinaanats boosh nt'intsitwok'o neen aatosh ik wotwutserne.
Ernmó boosh eekfne, bín noúd'raawo mááyo máratsone, aatsonowere úyatsone ett taarts haboniyere bogts ashuwots bín úd'osh aashdek'rne, and bo bokotir boosh nkeewituwo s'uziye.»
Azaziruwonuwere «Keewan taash n keewutsok'o konshor daniyik'aye» ett na'o deen b́k'ri.
Maniyere hakon kes' azazefman bali naashwotsitse gituwotsi s'eegdek't «Ilitsi keez sa'ato b́wottsok'on K'isari maants git bal kes'fuwotsnat shab farshetsuwotsi, git bal gin shap'fuwotsnowere k'aniwere,
P'awlosshowere farsho it k'anire dats keewiruwok Filksok jeenon b́bodetuwok'o woshwore» bí eti.
Hank'o etiru woshonowere work'atats guut' b́k'ri,
«K'elawudiyos Lusyosoke, mangts dats k'eezfo Flkissh! jeeno neesh wotowe!
Ashaan ayhudiwots detsdek't úd'oshe boteshi, taamo Rom dats ash b́woto tdantsosh kes' kes'fuwotsnton bodat bín t wooriyi.
Eegatse tuutson bos'aamitsok'o danosh geeyat mooshiruwotsok t'intsree b́teshi.
Bos'amiwere bo nematse tuuts keewon b́wottsok'o tdaatsi, ernmó k'irosh wee tiposh bín betsit keewo aaliye.
Ashaan údosh maletsok'o tshishtsok'on manoor níyok twoshi, s'amiruwotsuwere bíyatse bodetsts s'aamiyo nshinatse bot'intsituwok'o boosh keewure.»
Mansh kes'kes'iruwots boon azazetsok'o Pawlosi t'úwon dek'amt Antip'at'risok bobetsi.
Yatsok'on Farshetsuwots P'awlosn ton boametuwok'o wosht boowere k'es' kes'fuwots gálo maants k'azboaani.
Farshetsuwotsuwere K'isariyo bo bodtsok'on worek'atats guut'ets woshman dats k'eziruwosh imt P'awlosi b́shinats bot'intsi.
Dats k'ezirowonu worek'atats gút'ets woshman b́nababi hakon P'awlossh Aawoki dats ashnene? ett bíaati, Kilik'iy dats ash b́ woto b́ dantsok'on
«Neen s'amiruwots boowor njango shishetuwe» bí eti. Herodis mengst moots b́ koteetuwok'owere bíazazi.
Úúts aawoniyere il kahni naasho Hanani eenash ikikuwotsnat T'ert'elusi eteef Nemo sheengshdek' dantsonton K'isari maants bíami, boowere dats k'eeziruwo Filiksok t'int P'awlosi bo s'aami,
P'awlosi s'eegdek't t'intsetsok'on T'ert'elus hank'o eton s'aamiyo dek't b́tuwi. «Shiimetso Filikso! niyatse tuwtson ay jeeno daatsrone, n sheeng k'eezonowere noashosh sheeng wonewo daatsere,
Ayidek'at mangtso Filikso n k'alts sheeng keewan jamoke jam weeron een údone nodek'iri.
Andmó t ja'irawo k'awunon neesh t keewit keewo n doon noon nk'ebetuwok'o neen k'oniruwe,
Ashaan noosh gondshoodo wotwutsere, datsatse fa'a Ayhudi jamwotsats dimbiro b́tuuziri, noimnetiyatse k'aldek'ets naazrawiwotsi eteefwotsshowere boon jishirwooniye.
Ik' moonowere kimshosh bíetfere bín nodetsi, bíyats not'intsts s'aami jaman ar b́ wottsok'o nee ntookon bín aatr dano falitune.» ik ik bitsuwotsitsere han boyits dabfno [No nemok'on bíyats angsheyish gawurone b́teshi, Ernmó gin jishiruwo Lusyos waat angnon nookishotse fos'dek't bíami, bín s'aamirwotsu níyok boweetwok'o bíazazi]

<range>
Ayhudiyots «Jam keewan aree» Etfetst s'amiyosh ik wotbowtsi.
Dats k'eeziruwo Filiks b́kishon kolat P'awlos b́ keewitwok'owa bíeti, P'awlos hank'o ett bíaaniy. «Ay dúrosh datsan keewutso nwoto tdantsosh taan s'amiyets keewosh aani tdek'etuwok'o nshinaats tt'intsor ayidek'at geneeúwefetsatniye,
Ik' k'onosh Iyerusalem maants ti'amron tatse git aawoniyere b́bowok'o nee ntookon danofalfnee,
Ik'i mootse wotowa ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni mootse wee kitotse kontonuwor t mooshfere wee asho dimbirosh ttuuzfere taan daatsratsne,
And tiats bot'intsts s'amiyosh gawo b́jamon neesh t'intsosh falratsne.
Ernmó han neesh kish kitso shunfee, bo kooti dana bo etiru imnetiyi kayo no nihotsko Izar Izeweri Ik'irwe, Muse nemonat Nebiyiwots mas'aafotse guut'ets jamo amanirwe.
Bowere bojangirwok'o taawor kaawwotsnat morretsuwots k'irotse botuwitwok'o Ik'on jangirwe.
Mansha Ik'onat ash shinatse nib s'ayino tdetsetuk'o jamaawo kup'irwe.
«Iyerusalemitsnowere tkeshiyak ay natuwots bobeshiyakon t jirwotssh tep'wotit gizonat Ik'osh imet mebi gizo dek'at tweyi.
Ik'o mootsnowere taan daatstsuwots man tk'alfere, manoori gizeyonuwere s'ayini fino fin tk'rtsok'one, taantonuwere ay asho aaliye b́teshi, dimbironwere tuuratse.
Ernmó Isiyon waats ayhudiwots manoke fa'ane boteshi, bo taan bos'aamit keewo detsfno wotiyal nshinaats t'inr keewune.
Haniyakonowere moosh mooshiyiruwots shinats tt'iinoor t t'afitso fa'ewotiyal t'ints ashaanots keewune.
Arikon bo taalotse need'dek'at ‹K'irtsuwots tuwo fa'e tiettsosh hambets angshosh it shinats t'inre› etaat een k'aaron keewure, haniyere okoon k'osho tk'alts keewo aaliye.»
Filiksmó Krstiyani imnetiyi jango sheengshdek't b́dantsotse «Kes' azazefo Lusyos b́waatsok'on itjangosh angshituwe» ett boon deenb́k'ri.
P'awlosi kotiru bali naashoshowere «Ayide b́ kic'irawonat b́ jaguwotswere bish k'alo bogetso baziyerawon b́kotetuwok'wa» bí eti.
Muk' aawwotsiyere hakon Filkis Dursili eteets b́mááts ayhudiyunton b́weyi, P'awlosnowere s'egiydek't Iyesus Krstos shútson amani jango b́keewufere b́shshi.
P'awlos kááwu woti jangonat took kewdek'i jango weet angshonowere b́keewor Filiks shatt «And k'ayamee, taash b́k'anoor k'osh aawots neen s'eegituwe» bí eti.
Filiks P'awlosoke gubo dek'osh jangitniye b́tesh, mansh ayoto P'awlosi s'eegiyir b́keewifoni.
Git natoniyere okoon P'ork'iyos Fist'os Filikis shegro b́beyok b́beeyi, Filiks ayhudiwotsi geneúshosh geeyat P'awlosi b́ tipetsok'on k'azb́k'ri.
Fist'os bí alguro K'isariyotse kindt keez aawo b́ teshiyakon manokere Iyerusalm maants bíami
Manoknowere kahni naashwotsnat ik ik een een Ayhudi jirwots Pawlosats bo s'aamiyo bot'intsi, «P'awlosi Iyerusalemi deewáár noosh sheeng keewo k'aluwe» ett bok'oni, han boettsonuwere P'awlosi weerindatse korde'er úd'osh bo geetsotsne.
<range>
Fist'osmó «P'awlos K'isariyon tipi mootsne koteyiri, taawere kaari and aanar b́maants ametuwe,
It naash naashuwotsuwere taanton K'isariyo maants amnee, P'awlos b́ fints gond fino b́beyal manoke s'amiwune» bí eti.
Fist'os shmt aawoniye wee tats aawoniye bowawu aawwotsi bonton b́ beshiyakon K'isariyo maants no ami, manok nobodtsok'on yaatsok'on naashi jorats bedek't P'awlosi bíyok de'er bot'inetuwok'o bíazazi.
P'awlos b́ t'intsok'on Iyerusalemn waats ayhudiyots gúrdek't need'at gaawu deshaw ay een een s'amiyotsi bí'ats bot'intsi,
P'awloswere «Taa ayhudiyots Nemats wotowa Ik' maats wee Rom nugúsats t fints gond fino aaliye» ett bí'atse bíaniyit keewo b́keewi.
Fist'osmó ayhudiyotsi geneúsho geeyat P'awlosi «Iyerusalem maants amr han jangosh manoke tshinatse angsho dek'osh geefneya?» bí eti.
P'awlosmó hank'o ett bíaani, «Hambe! taa b́shinaatse mooshosh Rom nugúso angshi jori shinatse t need'iri, nee sheengsh dek'at ndantsok'on ayhudiyotsats t fints gond fino aaliye.
Morretso twotiyal wee k'irosh betsit fayo tiats betsit morro finere wotiyal woruna eraatse, ernmó bo s'amiyan k'awuntsalka wotiyalmó konuwor bosh taan beshide'er imo falratse, taa Rom nugúsosh taash s'iilewe etaat t'intsree.»
Manoor Fist'os bín izfwotsnton keewedek't «Romko nugúso taash s'iile etri wotiyal nugúsok ametunee» bí eti.
Muk' aawwotsiyere hakon Nogúso Agrip'nat Bernik'e Fist'ossh «Dan jeenon waarne» etosh K'isari maants boweyi.
Manoknowere ay aawosh beyat boteshtsosh Fist'os P'awlos jango hank'o ett Nuguso Agrip'sh b́ keewi, «Filks tipk'rat k'az b́k'rts ash iko hanoke fa'e b́teshi,
Taa Iyerusalemitse tteshor kahni naashuwotsnat Ayhudi eenashuwotsn ashaan bos'amiye hakon bíats t angshituwok'o boaati.
Taamó ‹Ash iko bín s'amiruwots shinats t'inr bín bos'amirumansh b́keewude'aniyere s'amiyetsman beshide'er imo Rom datsatsi ashuwots neemaliye› etaat boosh tiaanyi.
Mansh ashaan s'amiruwots ko'eyat hanok bowatsok'on ja'araniyere yaatsok'on angshi jorats bedek'at P'awlosi t shinats bot'intsituwok'o ti azazi,
Bín s'aamirwots keewosh b́ganok need' bodek'tsok'on bí gond fino finere ett tgawtsok'o bín s'amiyosh betsit keew eegonoru bíats t'intsratsne.
Ernmó bínton bomooshiru moosho bo haymanoti jangonat k'irt teshtso P'awlos ‹Kashetsiye› bí etiruwo Iyesus jange.
Taawere hannaari keewo s'ilosh taan b́kic'ire P'awlosi ‹Iyerusalem maants amr bíyoke keewan jango angsho daatso shunfiya?› tieti.
Bímó bí jango Rom nugúsoke bísh s'ileyish geeyat nugúsok taash s'iilewe bíettsosh manok tdaamifetsosh tipi moots b́teshetuwok'o tiazazi.»
Agrip'were Fist'ossh «Taawor ashaan b́keewufere k'ebo geefe» bí eti. Fist'osuwere «Yaats bín k'ebetunee» bíet.
Mansh yatsok'on Agrip'nat Bernik'e bo naashi taho tahdek't een baatson wotdek't kes'iruwotsatse naashuwotsnat kit kitotsi een een ashuwotsn deneyat waat angshi maa eenots bokindi, maniyere hakon Fist'os P'awlosi b́ s'eegiyi.
Hank'owere bíeti, «Nugúso Agrip'o! Itwere noonton fa'a ash jametsuwotso! ayhudiwots ‹Ashaan haniyere hakon kashon beyo bísh geyiratse› ett kuhefetst Iyerusalemitse, hanoknowere ti angshituwok'o taan boaattso it bek'iru ashaaniye.
Taayere bíyatse k'irosh bín betsit gond fino daatsratse, bí Rom naashi naashosh ‹t jango taash s'iilewe› bíettsotse hanok woshosh t k'ut'i.
Wotowa eree b́jangosh t doonzsh tguut'etwo daneets keewo deshatse, mansha s'ileyakon tguut'etuwo tdaatsituwok'owa etaat it shinats bítsnor iki Nugúso Agrip'o! nshinaats t'intsree.
Tipetso danbaan dameeyor bí s'amiyets jango kits k'azo dartsi araatniye taash b́be'eyi.»
Agrip' P'awlossh, «N took jangosh keewundek'etuok'o taaro neesh imere» bíet, Pawlosuwere b́kisho jargdek't hank'o ett keewut aani b́dek'i.
«Nugúso Agrip'o! Ayhudiwots taan bos'aamits keewujamosh hambets nshinatse keewur aani tdek'or ayiniye t geneúwiri.
Bítsnowere nee ayhudiwots niwonat moosh jamo t'iwintsdek'at danfnee, mansh k'amoon taan nk'ebetuwok'o neen k'onirwe.
«Na'ortson tuwat awuk'o t beetsok'owo ayhudiwots danfnee, shintson tuwat tiash ashi dagotsnat Iyerusalemitse t be beyo danfnee.
Ando aani gawo bogeyiyal no haymanotiwotse kup'idek'at nonemo kotiru kayuwotsitse ferisawi wotat tbewok'owo shintson detst danfnee.
Andmó angshosh hanok tneed'ir Ik'o nonihotssh taart b́ imts b́ jangiitsoshee.
Jangiyetsanok bodosh no jir tatse gituwots Ik'o t'uwe aawo Ik'ifetstni bokotfo, Nugúsono! taawor ayhudiwotsn taan bos'aamits jangiyetsan jangatsne.
Ik'o k'irtswotsi b́tuuzitwok'o eegoshe itoke amano maawek b́woti?
«Taa t tookish Nazrettso Iyesus shútso tfaltsok'on k'efo taash geyife etaat asaabefe b́teshi.
Iyerusalemitse tk'altsonúwere haniye b́teshi, kahni naashuwotsoke t dek'ts alon amantsuwotsitse ayuwots tipimoots bokindituwok'o k'alre, boon boúd'orowere úd'iruwotsnton ik wotere.
Ayoto ayhudiwots Ik' k'oni mootse boon jod'r doonzo boc'ashetuwok'o woshfee, boon ayide fayarnuwere k'osh úratsi kituwotsokor kesh amaat boon giishefe.
«Han jangosho kahni naash jamwotsoke alonat tzaziyo dek'at Demask'o maants tí amifere tteshi.
Nugúsono! weeratse t befere aawu taalon aawu sháánoniyere bogo sháánts shááno tbek'i, sháánanuwere tiyatso taanton sha'irwots gúúratso darotse sháániyi b́k'ri.
Noúnetswere datsats dih s'uwat nobefere ayhudiwots noon keewu keewon ‹Sawul! Sawulo! eegishe taan ngishiri? Shiki shashats nned'iyal neesh b́ gonditi!› etiru k'ááro tshishi.
Taawere ‹Doonzono! nee kone?› tieti, doozonuwere, taash hank'o bíeti, ‹Taa nee ngishiruwo Iyesus taane.
Andmó tuur n tufoon need'owe, taa neesh tbe'eyiye and taan nbek'tsannat shino maants neesh tbe'et keewosh gútsonat gawo nwotitsh tgetsotsne.
Israe'el ash ashuwotsnat bo maants neen twoshit Ik' danawu ashuwots kishotse neen farituwe.
Bo aawo n k'eshituwok'onat t'aluwotse shááno maants nkishituwok'o Shed'anosh keeweewotsno Ik'o maants ni aanituwok'o woshituwe, boowere taan bo amantsi jangon bo morrosh orowa eto daatsitune, galdek'etsuwotsnton ritstiyo kaydek'etune.›
«Eshe nugúso Agrip'o! daaratse taash imets bek'osh k'aztso woteratse.
Ernmó shino Demask'on fa'a ashuwotsi, maants dabat Iyerusalemnat Yhud dats jamatse, Ik' danawu ashuwotsi naandrone err Ik'o maants bo aanituwok'o tdaniyi, naandrone boettsok'ono kitsit fino bo finituwok'o boon tdani.
Han jangosh ayhudiyots Ik'i mootse t befere taan detsdek't úd'osh boeti.
Hambetsish b́borfetsosh Ik' tep'o tiyatse k'aleratse, manshe múk'osho enosho gawefetsat hanoke ned'iruwe, nebiyiwotsnat Musen shino hank'o wotituwe boetts keewo keewoniyere okoon k'osho eegoru keewuratse.
Bowere bokeewu ‹Mesihiyo gond bek'o dek'etuwe, k'irotse tuwonowere shintso wotar kashi sháánono Israe'el ashuwotsnat Ik'i ash woterawwotsnsh kitsituwe› ettniye.»
P'awlos man keewoke b́befere Fist'os «P'awloso! ando geewutsernee, ay ndano neen geyomants betsk'rere!» ett kuhat b́keewi.
P'awlosmó hank'o ett bíaniyi, «Ayidek' shiimetso Fist'oso! arikonat kaawu keewoni tkeewiri bako geeyaliye tgeyi.
B́ shinatse keewan tkeewiru nugúso keewan danfee. Hanwere ashon k'alerawo b́wottsotse nugúso b́dantsok'owo danfee.
Nugúso Agrip'o! nebiyiwotsi amanirunosha? Ni'amaniruwok'o danfee.»
Agrip'were P'awlossh, «Nee k'awun sa'atanitse taan krstiyani woshk'rishale» bí eti.
P'awloswere, «K'awun gizewotse wotowa geenz gizewotse n s'uzi b́woterawon hamnbets tkeewuts keewo shishts jamo t tipeyaniyere okoon taank'o bowotish Ik'o k'oniruwe!» bí eti.
Haniyere hakon nugúso, altsonat Bernik'ewu bonton bedek't teshts ash jamwots k'az botuwi.
Manoke kesht boamferowe, «Ashaan k'irosh wee tipewosh bín betsituwo eegoru k'alratse» boeti.
Agrip'were Fist'ossh, «Ashaan Rom nugúsoke tkeewo taash s'iilewe eto b́ k'azink'ere hank'on fakshk'ryank'e» bí eti.
It'ali datso maants markabon no ametuwok'owa eteetsok'on P'awlosnat k'osh k'osh tipetswotsn Rom dats k'eeziru Awugst'osi eteetso kes' jishiruwots kayotse teshtso Yuliyosi eteets bali abaatsi naashosh boimi,
Isiyon aatsi k'ari gúratse markabi bíyok need'irwok amiru Adramit'yon markabats keeshdekat no sha'i, mek'odeni awurajotse fa'a Teselonk'e kitotsi asho Arst'rokoswere nontoniye b́teshi.
Yaatsok'on Sidoni amnobodi, Yulyus P'awlossh sheengo b́teshtsotse b́ shunfwotsok amt bísh geyit tep'o bish bok'alituwok'owa bí eti.
Manoke tuwatnwere jongo noshinaatse noats b́ jongiruwotse K'op'rositse aats k'aritsi datsu te'o woshdek'at markabatsi sha'o dek'atnotuwi.
Kilk'iyanat P'infiliyo ganoke fa'a aats k'aro nokimiyakon Lik'iyon fa'ú Mura kitto nobodi.
Manoke bali abaatse altso It'aliyomants ametuwo Iskndr markabo daatsdek't bíats nokeshetuwok'o b́woshi.
Ay aawo t'awaash dek'at sha'at ay gond bek'on K'enidos kitu ganok amnobodi, jongonwere shinomaants noamawok'o noon b́bazitsotse Selmona dats gúúri ganoke beshat k'ert'es aatson gúrets datsu naaydek'at noami.
Ay gondbek'on gúr gúron nobeshiyakon Lasiy kitu ganoke daatseyiru, «Markabi need'ok sheengi» eteef beyokuk amnobodi.
No weeratsnowere ay gizewo hank'on b́ís'uure s'oomi gizeyo b́beshtsotse manoor aats k'aratse sha'o ayidek' shatiko b́teshtsotse P'awlos ashuwotssh hank'o ett bo atso bokotetuwok'o b́woshi,
«It ashuwotso! haniyak nosha'it sha'o shatiyits keewo bítse b́beyok'o taash be'eyiruwe, Kuronat markaboon s'uzats b́woterawo ash kashatsor kup'ts t'afonat s'uwo bodetuwe.»
Bali abaatse altsonmó P'awlos izoniyere markabu azaziruwonat markabudoonz boetiruwoni b́ k'ebiri.
Markabwots need'okman jooshi kimoosh sheengo woto b́k'aztsotse ay ashuwots, «Shinomaants sha'arr faletkawotyal gaar weeron, muur aawukindomantsi fengesho maantse fa'o Fink'eyi eteefo K'ert'esitse markab ned'efok borr manoke joosho beshiwone» ett bo asaabiyo bot'intsi.
Muur maantse muk' jongu b jongefere bobek'tsok'on boasaabtsok'o boosh b́wottsok'o bíarere markab bín bojokiru bitsdek't aatsatse sha'o dek't botuwi, markabi ned'iruwoke tuut k'ert'es ganoke gúr gúron bobeshi.
Ernmó muk'i boteshiyakon, «Gaar maantsi aawu keshon eegurahi jongo» kup'ts jongo aats k'aro bin gúrts datsuatse tuut aats k'aromaants bomaants b́weyi.
Markabonwere b́gifniyetsonat jongmansh b́maawutsotse s'k etaat jongon jokeyat noami.
K'eda eteets aats k'aron gúrts datsu naaydek'at nosha'or ay gond bek'on Markabuko jelbo detsdekat nokishots geddek'o nofali.
Markab jookiruwots jelbu markabots geetsdek't bokishiyakon markabu gúridek't jokon bo s'aas'i, markabu Surtisi eteets shiyi datsu maants bdihirawok'o shatt sharo k'o'úbazt jongon jokefere boami.
Egúrahon were kup'efere bíamtsotse yatsok'on markabats kuryets k'ac'o ik ikon aats k'aromaants juwo dek'botuwi.
Keezl aawots markabi k'ac'o bokishon k'aaúdek't shap't bojuwi,
Ay aawosh aawuno wotowa, k'eeno bo bee'awotse jongonwere kup'efere bíamtsotse haniyere hakon kashosh falatsonee ett maac'o k'ut'bodek'i.
Ashuwots misho b́jamon bomarawo ay aawo boteshi, mansh P'awlos bodagots need'dek't hank'o bíeti, «It ashuwotso! taa tiettso shishat T'ersesn turatste wotink'ere awaashonat t'af jamann itats borawnk'ee b́teshi.
Andoor markabo s'uzi awaashiti bako ititse konatsor t'afo boratse, mansha shenuwotso shatk'ayere! etaat itn iziruwe.
Oots t'ú bík twottso bín t Ik'iruwo Izar Izewer b́woshts melakiyo t ganok need'de'k't
‹P'awloso! shatk'aye! Romko naashi naasho shinatse need'o neesh geyife! hambe neenton sha'iru jamo Ik'o neesha err k'irotse worituwe› ett taash keewure.
Manshe it ashuwotso shatk'ayere! Ik'o taash b́keewuts jaman b́jamon b́s'eentsituwok'o bín amaniruwe.
B́woteferemó jongo noon aatson gúrts dats ikuk de'amr juuk'rituwe.»
Tatse aauwdl t'úwotse Adriyay aats k'ari taalotse jongon jod'efe noamfere taali titson markab jookiruwots datsomants bot'intsok'o boosh bíari.
Mansha aats k'ari woko bín indeef joko dek't boindere dashan b́woko habigit indok'o wotat b́datseyi, muk'i boteshiyakon ando boindere shiits indok'o dashan b́geenztsok'o bodaatsi.
Nomarkabo aats k'ari gúúratse fa'a shutsuwotsats b́gawerawok'o shatt markabi shutsomantse markab bín jookef awdwotsi aatsots oorsh bok'ri, maniyere hakon t'úwo beshar bíere aawo boosh b́weetuwok'o Ik' k'ono dek' botuwi.
Markabu jookiruwots markabutse kesht wos'o geeyat boteshtsotse markabu shinomaantse bín need'iyeyiru biro dashan juwiruwo araat markabutse fa'a jelbu aats k'aromaants bojuwi.
Manoor P'awlos bali naashonat kes' kes'fuwotssh «Markabu jokirwots markabatse giwuk'ayr bobeyala bako it faro falratste» bíti.
Mansh kes' kes'fuwots jelbu detsts joko k'ut'k'raat aatsats juubok'ri.
Datso gatsosh bíetfere jametsuwots misho bo meetuwok'o P'awlos k'ont boosh hank'o bíeti «Eegonor mook'zat koto dek' it tuwiyako hamb hambetson tatse awdl aawe.
Manshe maayo it nonots itgedetwok'oye iti tk'oniri. Mannowere faritute, it took s'iirotse ikunwor dats fed'eratsatsane.»
Man bietihakon misho k'aaúdek't jamishinaatse Ik'o b́údi, titsdek'tnuwere moo dek'b́tuwi.
Mann jametsuwots kup'at misho bomeyi.
Markabutse b́ jamon git baalona shabe shrt ashuwotsn fa'ane noteshi.
Jamwots máát boworiyakon Markabats kuriyets Sindeyo aatsi k'aro maats juwat bíyatsi kuro boketi.
B́ gatstsok'on bobodoko danatsno botesh, wotowa bako shiyo bítse be'eyiru aatsi k'aro bo bek'i, boosh b́faleyal markabu b́ maants gifnir úratse kishosh bogawi.
Markabo bín bneed'iru bíro bítsdek't aats k'arots faksh bok'iri, manoor bín markabo jokeyiru jokono bítsbok'ri, man kaawats fa'a sharono jongo maants dambaan k'aaúdek't aatsi k'ari gúúro maants keshosh boami.
Ernmó markabu kakuwets shiyats bgaawetsosh dashan gúp'n bwutsi, b́shino maantsno dashan k'ons'ewtsat giwo bk'azti, b́shuutso maantsnomó jongi gifniyatse tuwtson tisho b́tuwi.
Tipetswotsitsere ikonuworu wáákr b́keeyawok'o kes' kes'fwots úd'osh bogawi.
Baalats naashonmó P'awlosi oriyosh b́getsotse boetts man de'atse, dab waak faltso shini markabots aatsi k'aro maants t'olar datsats k'ayi bokeshetuwok'o bíazazi.
Oortsuwotsmó Markabi is'uwotsnat markabi tishats bede'er bokeshetuwok'o bíazazi, mank'oon jamwots jeenon datsats bo bodi.
K'aznofariyakon biats nobodts aats gúrdek'ts datsu Maltayi eteefu b wottsok'o dan nok'ri.
Aatson gúrts datsmanatse beyiruwots adits shuno noosh bokitsi, manorowere awusho b́buye ak' b́wottsotse tawo aat'idek't noon s'eeg dek't boibii.
P'awlos shooto kakudek't taawots b́gedfere, k'ees'manatse tuutson dawunz ik kesht b́kishats deshwutsat joor b́wutsi,
Malta dats ashuwots dawunzo P'awlos kishats joorat b́befre bek't «Arikon ashaan kash údk ashe! aats k'aratsi jongotse jeenon b́keshalor Izar Izewer angshotse oorat kashon beyo falratse» boeti.
P'awlosmó dawunzo taawots tebdek' juuk'rat eegor gondo bín b́datsrawo b́oori.
Ashuwotswere «Andemo andek'úna bíatso b́gaapiti, wee danerawon k'irr b́dihiti» ettni bokotfera botesh. Ernmó ayoto bokore bíats gondo eegoru bodo b́k'aye bobek'tsotse boaasabiyo wonidek't «Hanuwo Izar Izeweriye!» boeti.
Manok noteshts beyok man ganoke aats gúrts dats mani altso puplyus datso fa'e b́tesh, ashaan b́ meyits nondek't keez aawosh sheengshdek't noon b́ ibiyi.
Manoor puplyos nih atsik'es'onat ac'uwoo bín detsbde'e shoodtni b́k'eyiri b́tesh, P'awlos bíyok kindt Ik'o bísh b́k'oni, b́ kishonowere bíats geddek't kashiyib́k'ri.
Man b́wotiyakon aatson gúriyets datsmanatsi k'osh shodetsuwots waat bokashi.
Ash ashuwotswere ime keewo noosh dek't boweyi, noon bomangitsok'onowere noosh bokitsi, markabon amoosh notuworowere noosh geyitu jamo markabats noosh bokuriyi.
Keez shashosh Maltan noteshiyakon joshman aats kaaron gúrts datsmanatse no beshitso Eskndriyaa markabats keshdek'at notuwi, merkabunu Diyosk'orosi eteetso Woteraw maat ik'wots milkito btookatse detsfe b́teshi.
Srakus kitamots no bodtsok'on manoke keez aawo nobeyi.
Mokno aats k'aaro gúúrat Regiyum kitu nobodi, manoke ik aawo nobeshiyakon muur jongo b́ jongtsosh gitl aawots putiyolus maants noami.
Eshumanotsnowere daatsat bonton shawat aawo nobeysh noon bok'oni, maniyere hakono Rom maants noami.
Romitse fa'a amantsuwots nojango boshishtsok'on Afiyos gawuyonat «Keez k'eewokuwotsi» eteefuwotsok b́borfetso noon dek'osh boweyi, P'awlos boon b́bek'tsok'on Ik'o udat kup'b́wutsi.
Romits nokindtsok'on P'awlosi kotet kes' kes'f iko imt bíyal b́ beetuewk'o wosheyi.
Keez aawoniyere okoon P'awlos Romitse fa'a ayhuditsi een een ashuwotsi b́ s'eegiyi, bokakuwetsok'ono hank'o bíeti, «Tieshuwotso! Israe'el ash ashonat nihwots nemats tk'altso egonuworu gond fino aaliye, wotowa bako Iyerusalemn tipeyat Rom ashuwotssh besheyat ti'imeyi.
Rom ashuwots taan boatiyakon k'irosh taan betsit weero datso bok'aztsotse hank'on taan fakshosh gawtniye boteshi.
Ayhudiyotsmó taa hank'on tfakshewo bok'eftsotse Rom nugusoke taash s'iilewe eto geyik b́woti, b́wotiyaloru ti ashuwotsi ts'aamit keewo deshatseb́teshi.
And itn ts'egiye itn bek'osh geeyat manowere itsh keewoshe, taa habiliyan ttipe Isra'elsh jangit imets keewi jangoshe.»
Bowere hank'o ett bísh boaani, «Yhud datsatse njangosh gúút'ets wosho noosh boratse, hanok waats ashuwotsitse konuworu ngondo keewtso aaliye.
Namaniru haymanotiyan b́ be beyoke ash ashuwots bok'efiruwok'o danfone, mansh níasabtso eeg b́wottsok'o shisho geefone.»
Aawo bísh bodetsiyakon aywotdek't b́ beyiru moo maants boweyi, bíwere guurtson kooc'ish b́borfetsosh Ik'i mengsti jangosh gawon bíasabiyo boosh kish b́ kitsi, boon amaniyoshowere Muse nemonat nebiyiwots mas'aafotse kitsfetst Iyesus jangosh boosh b́daniyi.
Ik ikuwots b́aap'o boamani, k'oshuwotsmó amaneratsno.
Bowere boatsetseyo ik bowoterawon bok'aleyi. B́wotefere bok'aleyoniyere shino P'awlos b́keewo b́ ishoor hank'o ett b́keewi, «S'ayin shayiro Nebiyiwo Isayasn it nihotssh b́ keewtso arikee b́teshi!
B́ keewts aap'o hankowa b́wotiti, ‹Ash ashaanotsok amrniye Shishonere shishetute, ernmó t'iwintsratste, Bek'onere bek'etute, ernmó nibn de'atste eree boosha,
Ashaanots nibo kup'wtsere, Bowaazonuwere ipewutsere, boaawonuwere is'ewutsere, Hnk'o wotob́k'azink'ee, Bo aawon be'er, Bowaazon shide'er, Bonibonowere t'iwintsde'er Tmaants bo aanere, Taawere boon tkashyank'oni b́teshi.› »
«Eshe Ik'i kashiyi wosho Ik'i ash woterawwotssh woshetsok'owo dande'ere, boowere eekar bín dek'etune.
[P'awlos han b́keewiyakon ayhudiwots k'up'shdek't mooshfere manoke kesht boami.]»
P'awlos b́kirayits mootse gitnati s'eeno b́beeyi, b́maants weyiru ashjamwotsno dek'fee b́teshi,
Ik'i mengstonowere nabfetst doonzo Iyesus Krstos jango konuwor bín b́bazirawon ááwu shuk'on b́danifoni b́teshi.
Iyesus Krstossh guuts wottso woshosh s'egetsoke, Ik'i doo shishiyo daniyosh marat'etso P'awlosoke wosheets wosho.
Doo shishiyanwere Ik'o nebiyiwots weeron S'ayn mas'aafotse shin shin jangiyets aap'oniye.
Doo shishiyonuwere Ik'i na'o b́ naaron Dawit naarotse b́shuweetsok'o kitsitkee,
Mank'owere no doonz Iyesus Krstos b́ S'ayin shayiron k'irotse b́tuwon Ik' na'a b́wottsok'o bíangi eenon b́daneyi.
Krstos shúúts jangosh Ik' ash Woteraw jamwots bo amanituwok'onat boaletwok'o woshosh b́ weeron wosh na'o wotosh noon betsit s'aato dek'rone.
Itwoor Iyesus Krstosk itwotituwok'o Ik'o b́ s'eegts jirwots taalots itne.
Eshe Romitse beyiru, Ik'o iti b́ shuntswotsnat b́jiro it wotituwok'o itn s'eegts jamwotso! Noo nih Ik'oknat nodoonz Iyesus Krstos s'aatonat jeenon itsh wotowe.
It imneti shúútso dats jamats b́shishetsotse, jamoniyere shinon Iyesus Krstos weeron it únets jangosh Izar Izeweri údituwe.
Jam aawo Ik'o tk'onor itn t gawiruwok'o b́ naay jangosh keewiruwo doo shishiyo daniyosh t nib s'eenon bísh t finiruwu Ik'o taash tgaawoniye.
Ando dabr s'uwanatse itok wosh Ik' shuno b́ wotere t weerindo b́káátsituwok'o jam aawo Ik'o t k'oniri.
Imnetiyats it kup'ituwok'o itn woshituwo shayiri imo itsh betsosho, itn bek'osh tewuniruwe.
Man ti etiruwere taa it imnetiyon, itwere t imnetiyon no atsatsewo nokup'itwok'owe.
Ti eshuwotso! k'osh k'osh Ik' ash woterawwotsitse ay amantsuwotsi tdatstsok'o mank'o ititsnoru shuwo daatsosh geeyatniye tteshi, ernmó itok wosh ay aawo tk'anere andish b́borfetso taash k'ano b́k'aztsok'o it danetwok'o geefe.
Salat'antswotsi wotowa salat'anerawotsi wotowa dantsuwotsi wotowa danawu ashuwotsi daniyo fal k'ayaatse.
Eshe itsh Romn beyiruwotssh doo shishiyo daniyosh tewuniruwe.
Taa doo shishi aap'on jitseratse, doo shishi aap'o shino ayhudiyotssh, bíyats aanat Ik' ash woterawwotssh, Mank'o amants ash jamwotsi kashiyosh falit Ik'i angoniye.
Kááwu wotituwo imnetiyon kasho daatsituwe ett guut'ere, Ik'i kááw woto doo shishyon b́be'etsotse b́ jamon asho kááw b́ wotit imnetiyone.
Ashuwots bogondon aro b́daneerawok'owe bok'aliri, Ik'onowere shato bo k'ztsotse bo gondi jangosh jametsats daaratse Ik' fayo be'etuwe.
Boon b́ sezituwere Ik' jango dano boosh b́ geyituwok'o Ik'o b́tookon b́kitsre dant boteshtsotsne.
Datso bíazetson tuut ashuwotssh be'erawo Ik'i doyo, manuwere dúre dúri bí angonat Izar Izeweri b́woton bí bíazts keewwots weeron sháánt b́be'eyirwonat t'iwintsosh ashuwots bot'afits t'afiyosh bo etetuwo deshatsne.
Bowere Ik'o dant bísh wotit mangonat údon imatsne, bohasabiyon woterawo bowoti t'iwintsraw bonibo t'alu b́wtsi,
«Dantsuwots noone» ett dartsuwotsi bowoti.
Besherawu Ik'o mangiyoniyere beshit asho aro wotts ariyetso, Kafon, awd tuf detsts gizuwotsn, datsatse geetseyiru dins'otswots aron arit finetsuwotssh mango boími.
Mansh boatsatsewo botook atsats jitsit fino bok'alitwok'o Ik'o kimon s'eents bonib tewunosh keewetswotsi bowotitwok'o k'azb́k'iri.
Man b́wotuwere Ik' aro kooton bowonitsosh, aztso shegro azeetso boik'itsonat bísh guuts bowottsoshe, Ik'onmó dúre dúrosh údeke! Amen.
Ashuwots man bok'altsotse Ik'o Woteraw wic'ets tewunosh beshidek't boon bí imi, bo mááts máátsuwots dab azeewon daneets gonkewo daneerawu gonkeyi naaron woni bok'ri.
Mank'o nungushuwotswere daneets gonkewo máátsuwotswotsnton wosho k'azt boatsatsewo bogúsiyon bomis'i, mansh nungushuwots nungushonton jitsits keewo bofini, bo sheeltsi jangosho boosh wotit fayo bomeetson bodek'i.
Ashuwots Ik' dano geyo bok'aztsotse wic'ets keewo bo finituwok'o Ik'o Woteraw nibosh beshidek't imb́k'ri.
Mansha morron, gondon, jaalon, weerigondon, okooron, kashúd'on, shid'eyon, dirshon, gond tewunon s'eent, ando oonetswotsiye,
Ash shúúts t'afiyruwots, Ik'o shit'iruwots, ash ketiyiruwots, mishetswots, noona boguwotsi etiruwots, gond finosh malo geyiruwots, bonih indosh azazerawwots,
T'iwintsde'awwots, keewetso gakiruwots, shuno deshawwots, maac'kup'uwotsiye.
«Keewanotsi k'aliru jamwots k'ire boosh wotiti» etiru Ik'o nemo danfetstniye jaman bok'aliri, k'al mec'ro woterawon, man k'alirwotsnowere bokup'iri.
Nee k'osh ashaats angshirwono nee ntokish bíyats nwebitwo deshatsne, k'osh ashaats ni angshor n tookatse niangshiri, nee k'osh ashaats angshfetsat, n angshts ashman b́ k'alirwoniye nk'aliri.
Mank'o k'aliru ashuwotsats, Ik'o boosh wotituwo boosh b́ angshiruwok'o danfone.
Nee ashono! mank'o k'aliru ashuwotsats angishfetsat, bo bok'aliruwo nk'alor Ik' angishi shirotse nkeeshtsok'o neesh arefa?
Himo Ik'o b́ sheeng wotonat jam falk b́woto, noosh b́ k'amonwere bí ankattsono ngac'iri? Ik'o sheeng b́ woto noosh bíayiyi, neen n morrosh naandre eto maants jishosh b́wotok'o danatsneya?
Eshe nee n morrosh naandre eto nk'aztsotsnat maac'o kup' nwottsotse Ik'i fayonat ari angshon b́be'et aawots fayo niats bí ayituwok'owe nk'aliri.
Ik'o ik ikuwotssh bofinok'oye boosh b́ imeti.
Sheeng finats kup'de'er údonat mangon t'afrawu kashonowere geyiruwotssh Ik'o boosh dúre dúri kasho imetuwe.
Botooki keewo geyiruwotsi, ari keewosh azazerawwotsnat gondosh azazeyiru gonduowotsatsomó Ik'i fayonat kaak k'iro boats weetuwe.
Shin shino ayhudiwotsats maantsnowere Ik'i ash woterawwotsats gond finiru ash jamwotsats gond bek'onat kic'on weetuwe.
Ernmó sheeng keewo kaliru ash jamats Ayhudi wotowa Ik'i ashwoterawwotsi wotowa údono mango jeeno boosh imetuwe.
Ik'oniye ashuwotsi boga bogshraake.
