Nemo bodeshawo morr finiru jamwots nemo bot'ut'alor t'afitúne, nemonowere deshfetsr morr finiru jamwotsmó nemon bo ats angshetuwe.
Ik' shinatse kááwu wotituwots nemo shisht finats jitsiruwotsiye bako nemo shisht finats jitsrawotsiyaliye.
Nem deshaw Ik' ash woterawwots bo azeewon nemo bí azaziru keewo kalirune, man weeron nemo bot'ut'aloru botookk wotts azeeyi nemo bodetstsotse k'alosh boon b́geyituwo danfnee.
Bo keewanúwere nemi etiru jam keewo bo nibats b́ guut'ets b́ wotok'o kitsiruwe, aaninuere bonibo boats gawituwe, ikn ikno boon bonibo b́gac'iti, ikn iknonomó boon b́ tep'eti.
Han sháánon b́be'etwere, taa t nabiru doo shishi aap'ok'on Ik'o Iyesus Krstos weeron ashuwots ááshon bofints keewats b́ angshit aawotse.
Hamb, nee «Ayhudi taane» etirune, nematse nte'eyiri, Ik'k nwottsosho bogtaana etaat ni'it'iri.
Nee Ik' ettso danfnee, Muse nemo ndantsotse sheeng fino danfnee.
«Nee dogwotsi jishiruwo taane, t'aluwotse faúwotssho sháán taane,
Danawwotssh dano kitsituwe, nanaúwotsno danituwe» níetiri, mank'o, «Muse nemon dano s'eenon detsfe» níetiri,
K'oshuwotsi daniruwo nwotor bére ntooko eegishe daniyo nk'azi? úp'mk'ayere nietiri, nemon úmp'e n úmp'iri,
Wido amk'ayere etirune, nemo wide niamiri, nee Woteraw Ik'uwotsi wic'irune, bo Ik' k'oni moowwotsno fa'o nbiik'iri.
Nee Ik'i nemwotsne n'it'ri, ernmó b́nemman gakat Ik'o ngac'iri.
Manuwere, «It ayhudiwotsatse tuutson Ik'i shútso Ik' danawu ashuwotsoke c'ashetwe» ett guut'etsok'one.
Gof amo arikon neesh b́ sheenget nemo nkotaale, nemo n gaaketka wotiyalmó gof niamo gofo niamawok'owe b́taaweti.
Mansha gof amaaw Ik' ashwoterawwots jiro nemi tzaziyo b́kotetka wotiyal gofo am b́ k'azo gof bíamtsok'o tawetwoshna?
Nee guut'ets nemo detstsonat gof amtso wotar nemo ngakal b́ meetson gof amawo wotar nemo s'eentsiru Ik' ash woteraw jiro níyats angshituwe.
Eshe shúúts mec'ron Ayhudi wottso ari ayhudiyaliye, mank'owere úratse be'eyiru meetson gof amo ari gof amaliyee.
Ari Ayhudiwo b́gitsitse Ayhudi wottsoniye, ari gof amonwere Ik'i shayiron S'ayinon wotit nibotse gof amoniye bako nemon guut'etsok'on meetson gof amaliyee. Eshe hannaari asho údo b́dek'et Ik'okna bako ashoknaliye.
Beree ayhudiyots Ik' ashwoterawwotsiyere bok'an eegoneya? Gof amo ayhudiwotssh eebi b́ k'aliti?
Arikon Ayhudi woto ay weeron k'anefe, bog keewo Ik'o aap'o ayhudiyotssh adaro bíimtsoniye.
Eshe Ayhudiyotsitsere ik ikuwots amanek wotar daatseyo bok'azal, bo amanetsuwotsi wotbok'azo Ik'o amanek b́ woto ooritúwa?
B́ jamon oriratse! «N aap'ts aap'atse tuutson arikeewetsoniye nwotiti, N mooshorowere angshon da'itune» Ett guut'etsok'on ash jamo kootetso b́ wotiyalor Ik'o arikeewetske.
Ernmó no morro Ik' kááwo b́ kitsitka wotiyal eshe eebi no'eteti? Ik'o nomorrosh noon b́seziyal kááwon angshratse eteya b́ wotiti? Hanoke t keewiruwo ashkok'one.
B́ jamon woteratse! hank'o b́wotitkawotiyal Ik'o datsuwats aak'oneya b́ angshiti?
Ernmó kootetsi twoto Ik'o ar keewutsi b́woto kitsre, b́mangi ayono kitsitk b́ wotiyal, bere taa morretsok'o tiyats angshet eegoshe?
Ik ik ashuwots «Bére, Sheeng keewo b́weyish gond keewo eege nok'aliyala?» etaat tdaniruwok'o woshdek't taan bo s'aamiyir, mansh mank'owwotsats angshet angsho kááwe.
Bére no ayhudiyots Ik' ash woterawwotsyere k'anefone eteya? Mank'o woteratse! k'osh ash jamo Ayhudi wotowa Ik' ashwoterawwotsi wotowa morretsuwotsi bowottsok'o shin shin kitsre.
Hank'o ett guut'etsok'on, «Dab ikonúwor kááwu asho aaliye, ik doonzuwor aaliye,
Nibetsonuwere aaliye, Ik'onowere geyiruwo ikdonzwor aaliye.
Jametsuwotswere weeratse k'az keshrne, Ik wotdek't darwutserne. Doo fino finiruwo dab ikdoonzuwor aaliye.
Bogogo k'eshets dook'oyiye, bo alberonowere antelcerne, bonoon keewi shuwonwere dawnz marziyok'oyiye
Bonoonuwere c'ashonat s'aamon bín s'eenwtskee.
Botufo ash úd'osh káárke,
Boweeratse daatsetuwere t'afonat dash aanone.
Jeeni weeronowere danatsne,
Ik'onowere b́ jamon sharaatsne.»
Muse nemi tzaziyo b́ s'iilfo nemmaniyere dashe fa'úwotsi b́wottsok'o danfone, manatse tuutson ashuwots bíyats boweebituwo t'ut't s'k bo etiri, dats jamonuwere Ik'i angshi shirots wotitwe.
Mansha asho konuwor Ik'o shinatse, Muse nemo s'eentson Kasheratse, Nemman b́kitsir ash jamo morretsi b́wotoniye.
Andmó Ik'o ashuwotsi kááwu b́ woshit weero nemalon b́ woteraawok'o be'ere, manuwere Muse nemonat nebiyiwots mas'aafotse gawere.
Mansha eshe Ik'o b́ k'osh k'oshirawon Iyesus Krstosi amanon amaniru jamosh kááwu woto imetuwe.
Ash jamwots morro finernre, Ik'o boosh b́'imts mangonowere t'ut'rnee.
Mansh ashuwots Iyesus Krstos b́ k'alts kashiyi fino Ik'i s'aat mec'ron kááw wotitune.
Ik'o Iyesus Krstosi wosho woshdek't b́ t'ints bín amanitu jamwots b́ s'atson bomorrosh oorowe eto bodatsishee, Ik'o man b́k'al b́k'amoon morr shintso k'azoon ar wotts b́took kááwo kitsoshe.
And dúranatse Ik'o b́ tookon kááwu b́woto b́kitsir Iyesusi amants jamwotsi kááwu woshoshe.
Haniyak bín noít'et keewo eebi fa'oni? Eegonor id'atsone! bín no id'awok'o woshitwonúwere eebi? Nemo no s'eenirwosheya? Woteratse, ernmó imneti nemone.
Mansh eshe Ik'i asho kááwu b́ woshit, asho nemi fino b́kaltsosh b́woterawo imnetiyon b́wottsok'o t'iwintsdek'etwone.
Himó Izar Izewer ayhudiwots s'uzshe Ik' b́woti? Izar Izewer Ik'i ash woterawwotsshor bokooshna? Arikon Izar Izewer Ik' ash woterawwotsshor boke.
Ik'o ike, ayhudiwotsi wotowa Ik' ash woterawwotsi bo amanere kááwu woshituwo bíne.
Bére, imnetiyatse tuutson nemo gaketuwone eteya? Iya'a, iki nemo kup'ide'erniye nodetsetiye.
Eshe meetson nonih wottso Abraham daatsre noetetuwo eebi?
Abraham kááwu b́wot finona wotink'ere, bín b́ it'et keewo daatsiyank'e b́teshi, ernmó Ik'i shinatse it'o falratse.
S'ayin mas'aafo, «Abarham Ik'on amanere, bíamantsonwere kááwu b́wottsok'o wotatniye bísh b́taaweyi» etfe.
Finiru asho b́ daatsitwo bí angi k'awnts wottsoni bako bísh imet imoniyaliye.
Asho sheeng fino b́t'ut'alor dab́ morretswotsi Kashitwo Izar Izeweri bíamaniyal bíamantso kááw wotar bísh taawetwe.
Dawit b́kaaton Ik'o sheeng finalon kááw b́woshit asho awuk'o derek b́wottsok'o b́ kitsor hank'owe bíeti,
«Bo daro boosh oorowe eteetsuwotsnat Bomorro boosh ipk'reets ashuwots Derekne!
Doonzo b́morro bíats b́taawurawu asho Deereke!»
Bére, Dawit b́keewuts deeran gofdamiyetsuwots s'uzsheya? Himó gof damiyerawwotsshe? Gof daamiyerawtsshowere, «Abraham Ik'o bíamanere bíamantsman bísh kááwu wotat b́taaweyi» etrone.
Eshe Abrahamsh b́imnetiyo kááwu wotat bísh b́taawe awure? Gofo bíamftse shinemó gofo bíamiyake? Gofo bímfetsere shina bako gofo bíamiyakaliye.
Abraham gofo bíamfetsere shino b́imnetiyo kááwu wotat b́datsetsok'o kitsosh milikito bísh b́wotituwok'o gofo bí amiye, hanuwere ando gofo boamaawo amanitu jamwots kááwu wotar botaawetuwok'o boosh niho b́wotishe.
Mank'owere Abraham gof amtsuwotsshor nihe, gof amtsuwotssh niho b́wottsonuwere gof boamtso s'uzosh b́woterawo bí gofo bí amfetsere shino b́detsts imnetiyi shuutso sha'iruwotsshe.
Abrahamnat b́ naaro datsu b́naatetwok'o Ik'o b́ jangiyi imnetiyon b́daatsts kááwona bako nem kotonaliye.
Ik'o b́jangitsman naatetwots nemo s'eentsde'e kotet ashuwotsi wotiyalma imnetiyo k'awuntso deshatse, b́jangtsonwere k'awntsalke.
Nemo b́dowet Ik'i faye, ernmó nemo bíaalink'e morro berawuk'ee.
Mansh Ik'o b́jangitsman bodaats imnetiyona b́ tesh, Ik' jangitsanwere Abraham naar jamwotssh Ik'oki s'aaton imek b́woto arikee. Manúwere nemo shoydek't sha'iru ashuwots s'uzsh b́woterawo Abrahamkok'o amants jamwotsshe, mank'onowere Abraham noúnetssh nihe
Abraham jangosh, «Ay ashuwots niho neen woshre» ett guut'ere, bí k'irtsuwotsi tuuzituwonat aalo b́ fa'ok'o woshituwo Izar Izeweri bí amantsotsne.
Abrahamsh n naaro ayider ayituwe ett keewetsok'on ay ashi niho b́wotituwok'o bí amananat b́ jang eegoru jangosh wotit keewo bíalefere.
B́ idmewo bal natok'o b́teshtsotse b́ meetso b́maawutsotse k'irts ashok'o b́wottsotse shuwo b́falrawonat Sarawwere mahanat gawertsu b́wottsotse shuwo b́falrawok'o b́danaloru b́ imnetiyon maawk woteratse.
B́ imnetiyon kup' wotat Ik'osh manga b́ imi bako Ik'o bísh b́ jangitsatse aman k'azoon b́jamon hakebaka eraatse.
Ik'o b́jangitsonowere s'eentsitwo b́wotok'o b́ maac'i s'eenona bíamnefo b́teshi.
Mansha b́ amantso kááw wotat b́ taaweyi.
Ernmó, «Kááwu wotat bísh taawere» ett guut't aap'etso Abraham s'uzsh b́woterawo
noshorniye, nodoonz Iyesusi k'irotse tuuztso Izar Izeweri amaniruwotssh nooshor no amantso kááwu wotar b́taaweti.
Nodoonz Iyesuswere no morrosha ett k'irosh beshyat b́imeetsonat nonowere kááw woshosh k'irotse tutsoniye.
Eshe no kááw woto nodaats amanon b́ wottsotse no doonz Iyesus Krstosn Ik'onton jeeno detsfone.
And kup'dek'at nodatseyiru s'aatok nokind bín amanon b́wottsotse Ik'o noosh b́jangits b́ mango kayitwotsi nowottsosh mann it'irwone.
Hanmec'ron b́woterawo gond bek'o k'amo noosh b́daatsitwok'o nodantsotse noo gond bek'on it'iruwone.
K'amotsnowere fadeyar kup'o, kup'otsnowere jangiyetso daatsetwe.
Noosh imets S'ayin shayri weeron Ik'i shuno nonibotse b́ s'eentstsotse b́ jangitso noon jitsiratse.
Maawk wotat nobefere Ik'o bíetts aawon Krstos morretswotssha ett b́k'iri.
Kááw ash shegro wotar k'irit asho daatso ayide'er kic'ike, b́woteferor doo ash shegro kirosh daneraka daatso faletuwe.
Ernmó noo morretswotsi wotat nofa'e noshegro Krstos k'irre, manuwere Ik'o noosh b́detsts shuno awuk'o een b́wottsoniye b́kitsiri.
No kááwutso Iyesus Krstos s'atsona wotiyal ikibogshr Ik'i fayotse no kashit b́weerone.
Noo Ik'o balangarwotsi wotat nobefere b́naay k'iron Ik'onton no manerone, and Ik'onton nomaneyakon b́ naay kashi weeron iki bogo kashituwone.
Han mec'ronaliye, Ik'onton mano bín nodatstso nodoonz Iyesus Krstos weeron Ik'on ít'irwone.
Ik ashaatse tuutson morro datsuwats b́weyi, morratse tuutsonowere k'iro b́weyi, mank'owere ash jamo morro b́fintsotse ash jamats k'iro b́weyi,
Muse nemo b́ imftsere shin morro datsuwatse fa'e b́teshi, ernmó nemo bíaltsoke morro b́ tookon morrok'o taaweratse b́ teshi.
B́ wotiyaloru Adamkok'o nematse beshat morro finerawotsworu dab bo'orerawo k'iro Adamatse tuut Muse ats b́ borfetso ash jamatse alo b́ daatsi, Adamwere shinomaants weetu Krstossh bí aroniye.
Ernmó Ik'o b́ s'aati imo ash morronton nuutsaliye, ik ash morri jangon aywots bo k'irtsok'o mank'o Ik' s'aatonat ik asho Iyesus Krstos weeron daatsets s'aaton imetso ayuwotssh bogshdek't imere.
Mank'owere Ik'o beenon b́doots imo s'aati oot'o ash iko morro b́doots oot'ok'oyiyaliye. Ash iko morratse tuutson imetso angsho b́doyi, ay morratse tuutson imets imo kááwe wot b́dowi.
Ash iko morratse tuutson k'iro ash jamatse alo b́detsiyakon bére Ik'i ay s'aatonat beenon imetso s'aat bín kashitu ash jamwots Iyesus Krstos weeron kashon naashitune.
Eshe Adam iks'uzo morri fayi angsho ash jamats b́dootsok'o mank'o Krstos ikoko kashi fino ayuwotsi fayotse kishr kasho imetwe.
Ash iko aleyo b́k'aztsatse tuutson ayuwots morretswotsi bowottsok'o mank'o ash iko bíaletsatse tuutson ayuwots kááwitune.
Morro bíayitsotse nemo b́weyi, ernmó morro bíaytsok'on Ik'i s'aato iki bogsht bíayi.
Man b́wowwere k'iratse tuutson morro b́naashtsok'o mank'o ando aani nodoonz Iyesus Krstos weeron dúre dúri kasho b́ daatseyish Ik'i s'aato kasho imon naashituwe.
Eshe eebi noeteti? Ik' s'aato bí ayituwok'o morrats kup'ar beyonowa?
Woteratse! no k'iron galetsok'o morratse galetswotsi wotefetsr aawk'oneya morratse kup'ar nobeeti?
Krstos Iyesusnton ik wotosh gupets jamwots, b́ k'irono kaytswotsi wotosh, no guupetsok'o danatsteya?
Gupon bínton noduukeyor b́k'ironowere kaytsuwotsi woterone, mansh Krstos Niho mangon k'irotse b́ tuutsok'o noowere handr beyon beetuwone.
B́ k'iron bínton ik nowottsok'o k'irotse b́tuwon bínton ik wotituwone.
No ats morretso no atse b́tuwituwok'o morrosh guuts nowoto b́ oritwok'o no ats nato Krstosnton jitetsok'o danfone.
K'irts asho morrosh kewewotse nas'o keshre.
Eshe Krstosnton nok'iriyakon bínton kashon nobetuwok'o amanituwone,
Krstos k'irotse b́tuutsi jangosh gitlo b́ k'irawok'onat k'ironuwere bíyatse alo b́deshawok'o danfone.
K'iroone b́jamon iknoto morrosh k'irre, kashon b́beyonmó Ik'oshe b́beyiri.
Mank'o it k'iron k'alwok'o k'alewon morratse it k'aletsok'o Krstos Iyesus weeron Ik'osh kashon itbeyirwok'o taawwere.
Mansh morro it ats k'iritwatse alo b́detsetwok'onat it meets tewnosh keewetswotsi itn b́woshitwok'o eekk'ayere.
Mank'o it atsi kayuwotsi gondosh k'ac'o woshder morrosh kewik'ayere, ernmó k'irotse tuwat kashetswotsi it wottsok'o woshde'er it tooko Ik'osh t'intsuwere, it atsi kay jamwotsi kááwu finosh k'ac'o woshde'er Ik'osh kewiwere.
And it beyir s'aatoniyere dasha bako nemoniyere dash wot b́k'aztsotse morro itn b́ keewo geyiratse.
Eshe eege no eteti? Nemoniyere dash nowoto b́ oorere s'aatoniyere dash wotar morro finone eteya? B́jamon woteratse!
Bísh alewosh guutswotsi wotosh it tooko bísh it t'iintsiruwosh, bísh it aleyirwosh b́guutsuwotsi it wottsok'o danatsteya? K'irosh morri guutswotsi wee kááwwotosh aleyi guutswots itne.
Itiye shin morrosh guutse it teshi, andmó itsh imets danosh it nibon itazazetsotse Ik'osh údo wotowe.
Morrosh guuts wototse nas'o keshat kááawu woti guutswotsi woterte.
Taa hank'o ashosh b́wotit noon keew keewon tkeewir ash azeyon maawuk it wottsatsne. Shin shin it atsi kay kayuwotsi bokiimish weeri gondonat nemalon beyosh guutswotsi woshdek'at it t'intstsok'o andoor itatsi kayuwots bo S'ayinetwok'o kááw wotosh guutswotsi woshde'er t'intswere.
Morrosh guutso itteshor kááwo fino finosh kic'erak itne b́teshi.
Bére, manoor eebi it daatsi? And iti b́ jitsiyiruwoniyere okoon eegor daatsatste, keewhan b́ s'uwo k'ire.
Andmó morri guuts wototse nas'o keshat Ik'o guutsuwotsi itwottsotse S'ayin woto daatsitute, weeronwere b́s'uwatse dúre dúri kashe.
Morrotse daatset k'awuntso k'ire, Ik'oke imet imonmó nodoonz Iyesus Krstosn daatset dúre dúri kashoniye.
Tieshuwotso! han danatsteya? Tkeewir nemo dants ashuwotsshe, nemo ashaatse alo b́ detset asho kashon b́befetso s'uziye.
Aab s'iilere mááts amts máátsu b́kenih kashon b́befetsosh bínton nemon tipekiye, bkenih b́k'iriyalmó btipets nemotse s'aynat keshraniye.
Mansh bkenih kashon b́befere k'osh kenihosh máátso bi amal widetsuniye bish eteti. Bkenih b́k'iryalmó bínton btipets nemotse nas'o keshetuwane, k'osh kenihosh máátso biamalor widetsuni eteeratse.
Ti eshuwotso! it keewonuwere hank'oyiye, it Krstos atsi kaywotsi it wottsotse k'iron k'alewok'o k'alewon nematse k'alerte, mansh Ik'i finon shuwo noshuwitwok'o k'osho k'irotse tuutsosh b́ jirwotsi woterte.
Meets shunon ananat noteshor nemon tuwiru morri tewuno k'irosh shuwo noshuwish noatsi kayutsitse finefe b́teshi.
Andmó noon tipdek' teshts nemo k'iron galetsok'o no'atse b́ galetsotse nemi tipotse keshrone, mansh haniyere oki bísh nofinit handr shayiri jishona bako shin guut'etsnat wotts nemi jishonaliye.
Eshe eebi no eteti? Nemo b́tookon morreya? woteratse! ernmó morro eeg b́ wotok'o nodanish woshtso nemoniye. Nemo «Tewunk'aye» eto b́k'azik'e tewuno eeg b́wotok'o danawuk'e b́teshi.
Morro nemoke waats tzaziyon gowo daatsdek't jam naari tewuno ti'atsotse b́tuwitwok'o b́woshi. Nemo bíalink'ermó morro k'irke.
Shinon nemo bí aalor taa kashone tbeefoni, nemi tzaziyo b́ watsok'onmó taa tk'irre morro kasho b́daatsi.
Kashosh imetso nemi tzaziyo tiats k'iro b́doy.
Morro nemi tzaziyo weeb woshdk't taan b́ ant'elci, tzaziyanatse tuutsonowere taan b́úd'i.
Mansh nemo S'ayine, tzaziyonuwere S'ayinona, k'ááwonat sheenge.
Bére sheeng wotts keewan tiats k'iro dek'waare eteya? Iya'a! ernmó morro, morr wotar b́be'etuwok'o sheeng keewatse tuutson k'iro tiats dek'b́weyi, mansha morro tzaziyatse tuutson iki bog morretso b́woti.
Nemo shayiri weero b́wottsok'o danfone. Taamó morri guutso wotosh kemeets meetsik taane.
Taa t k'aliruwo danatse, t shunts keewo k'alo k'azat tshit'ts keewo k'alirwe.
Eshe taa t k'alir tshunaaw keewoni wotiyal nemo sheeng b́wottsok'o gawituwe.
K'alo tgeeraw keewo k'aliruwo tiatsotse fa'a morroni bako taanaliye.
Tigitsotse wee tmeets doyotse eegor sheeng keewo k'alosh falaatsetsee.
K'alosh tgeyiru sheeng keewo k'alratse, ernmó tgeerawu gond keewoniye tk'aliri.
K'alosh t geerawu gond keewoni tk'aliri wotiyal han k'aliruwo tgitsotse fa'o morroni bako taanaliye etee.
Eshe nemo finats b́jine bek'etuwe, sheeng keewo tgeefere gond keewo tik'altwok'o taan b́woshiri
Tgitsi atson Ik'i nemon geneúwituwe.
Wotowa eree nibots nemonton k'efefetst ti'atsotsi kayuwotsitse finiru morri nemosh tipetso taan woshiru k'osho azeewon taan jeep'iruwo ti atsi kayuwotsitse b́ beyok'o bek'iruwe.
Aawuk'o woteraw ash taane! k'iritu tiatsanowere kone taan kashiti?
No doonz Iyesus Krstos weeron Ik'osh údo wotowe! Eshe taa tnibotse, Ik'i nemosh keewetso wotat t meets doyon morri nemosh keewetso wotere.
Mansh Iyesus Krstosn beeyruwots and boats angshetuwo deshatsno.
Iyesus Krstosn datsetuwo kash imetu S'ayn shayri nemo, morronat k'ir dowet nemotse nas'o taan kishre.
Ash doyo maawk b́ wottsatse tuutson nemo s'eentsosh b́ falawo Ik'o k'alre, b́took na'onowere morrets meets aron morri jangosh woshat b́ meetson morro angshon ok b́ bazi.
Man b́k'aluwere meets shunon b́ woterawo no'atsitsi Shayiri shuntsok'on ananiruwotsats noats nemi tzaziy ariko bí b́s'eentsitwok'owe.
Meets shunon beyiruwotsi meets keewo, Shayiri shunok'on beyiruwotsmó Shayiri keewe bogawiri.
Meets keewu gawo k'ire b́ doweti, Shayiri gawirúwok'on wotoonmó kashonat jeenone b́imeeti.
Meets keew gawo Ik'oke shit'eek b́wottstse Ik'i nemosh bíalerawotse, kewewono maawre,
Meets keewosh kéweyirwots Ik'o geneúsho falatsne.
Itmó Ik' S'ayn shayiro ititse beyiruwe wotiyal Shayiri shúnona bako meets shunon beeratste, Krstos Shayiro deshaw ashonúwere Krstos jiraliye.
Krstos itits b́ wotiyal it meetso morri jangon k'irk b́ wotiyaloru Ik'o itn b́ káátstsotse it shayiro beyar beetke.
Iyesusi k'irotse tizts Ik' Shayiro ititse b́beyal, Iyesus Krstosi k'irotse tiztso Izar Izewer it gitsitse beyiru shayiri weeron k'iritk wotts it meetsosh kasho imetuwe.
Eshe t eshuwotso! no kashosh kup'o noosh geyife, ernmó noo beyon meets shunok'on beyo noosh geyiratse.
Meets shunok'on it beyal k'iritute, ernmó S'ayn Shayiri angon it meets fino it úd'iyal kashon beetute.
Ik' Shayiron jisheyru jamwots Ik' nanaúwotsiye.
Mansh «Niho! no nihono!» etaat it s'eegirwo na'ok'o woti Shayiro it dek'i bako shatoon beyosh aani guuts woti Shayiro de'atste.
Ik' Shayiro no Shayironton wotar Ik' nanaúwotsi nowottsok'o noosh gawituwe.
Eshe Ik' nanaúwotsi nowotiyakon bín naatetuwots noone, Krstosntonuwere naatetuwone, andowere Krstos gond bek'o kaytsuwotsi nowotiyal maniyere okoon b́ mango kayituwotsi wotituwone.
And gond bek'an shinomaants noosh be'et mangonton b́ taatseyal eegonoru talosh b́ falawok'o woshde tawituwe.
Azets jamo Ik' nanaúwots be'ewo een tewunone b́kotiri.
Azets jamo k'awunts deshawosh kewewtsere, manwere b́ took shunon b́ woterawo jangde'er b́ kotetwok'o woshts Ik' shunone.
Jangiyetsonwere azeetso b́tookon t'afi guuts wototse nas'o kesht Ik'i nana'úwotsnton s'ayinonat mang kayituwo b́wotituwok'oyiye.
Azets jamó ik wotat hambetsish b́borfetso na'a it'i kic'on detseyat kash k'as'oke b́beyiruwok'o danfone.
Ernmó gúútoke fa'o azeetso s'uziyaliye, S'ayin shayir shintso imets dek'tsuwots noworu no atsi shegr wottso Ik'o nana'ok'o woto kotfetsat nogitsitsi atson gúútoke nofa'oni,
No noworiye jangiyetsanne. Ernmó no no jangiru keewo be'etka wotiyal jangeet keewo b́woto oorituwe, be'eyiruwonere kone jangiti?
Nobe'aawu keewo nojangiyalmó k'amoon kotetuwone.
Mank'owere awuk'o Ik'o k'ono noon b́geiyitsok'o nodanaawotse S'ayin shayiro nomaawóko noon tep'etuwe, noonon kish keewo falerawo gúúton noosh Ik'o b́k'oniri.
Ash nibo shuu'at s'iliruwo Izar Izewer S'ayin shayiri asaabiyo eeg b́wottsok'o danfee, S'ayin shayiro amantsuwots jangosh Ik'o b́ k'onir Ik'i shuntsok'one.
Ik'o shuntswotsnat b́shuntsok'onowere s'eegets ashuwots Ik'o jam keewo sheengosh boosh b́k'alituwok'o danfone.
Shin b́dantsuwots b́ naayi araar b́ na'onúwere eshu ayuwotsitse k'aab b́wotituwok'o Ik'o shino wotituwe bíettsotsne.
Shino wotitune bíettsuwotsi b́s'eegi, b́s'eegtswotsnowere kááwu b́woshi, kááwu b́ woshtsuwotsnowere b́ mangiyi.
Eshe keewan jangosh eege noeteti? Ik'o noonton b́wotitka wotiyal kone noon k'efo faliti?
Ik'o b́ naay ik s'uzosh maac'o b́k'ewerawo noosha ett bíimiyakon b́ naaynton jamkeewo beenon aawuk'oneya noosh ímo b́k'azeti?
Ik'o galb'dek'tsuwotsi kone s'aamituwoni? Boon kááwwotsi woshituwo bíne.
Kone angshituwoni? Bí noshegro k'irre, k'irotse tuut Ik'o niho k'ani aaromants beedek'tso, nooshowere Ik'o k'onirwo Krstos Iyesusiye.
Krstos shunatse noon k'álo falituwo kone? Kic'eemó, gondbek'e? Gishee himó k'ak'e? Himó araats wote, t'up'ertawemó? Shike?
Hanwere «N jangosh aaw jamó noone úd'eyiri, Shukeyiru mereerwotskok'o taa weerone» Ett guut'etsok'one.
Eshe noon shuntson bín keew jamanotsida'adek'on da'atswotsiyere bogfone.
Mansh k'iro b́wotiyalor, kasho b́wotiyalor, melakiwotsi bowotiyalor, naashuwotsnor bowotiyal, andfa'o b́wotiyalor, shutsi weetuwo b́wotiyalor, kup'uwotsi bowotiyalor
Danbaan tuuka wotiyalor, dashaanowere gop'awotiyalor, kon naaro wotowa azeetso wotiyal no doonz Iyesus Krstosn nodaatsts Ik'i shunotse noon k'álosh falituwo eegonwor biaalok'owo arikon dandek'roone.
Krstosn arikoniye t keewiri, kooratse, S'ayn shayiron t nibonúwere tkorawok'o taash gawirwe.
Een shiyanonat k'ut'eraw kic'on t nibotse fa'ee,
Meetson t jag wotts tjiruwotssha err taa Krstosatse k'aleyar Ik' c'asho tiyats b́bodink'e shunfee b́teshi.
Boye Israe'el ashuwotsiye, na'ok'o wotonat mangi wuliyo nemono b́imi, aron Ik'o bo ik'itywok'ono b́kitsi, b́ jangits keewo bíimi.
Amants nihwotswere bokne, Krstos meetson b́wáá bo naarotsne, bíye jamoniyere dambe. Bíwere dúre dúrosh deeretso Izar Izeweriye. Amen!
Wotowa eree Ik' aap'tso wonere etaliye, Israe'el naar jamwots ari Israe'el ashnaliye.
Mank'o Abraham naar jamo Abraham nanaúwotsiye etaliye. Ik'o Abrahamsh «N naaro b́ keshetiye Yisak'ne» bíettsoshe,
Mansh meetson shuwetswots Ik' nanaúwotsiyaliye, ernmó naaro wotar taawetuwots Ik'o Abrahamsh b́jangitsok'on shuwetswots s'uziye.
Hanuwere Ik'o b́jangits aap'otse «Hambets naton hank'o aawon weetuwe, Sara nungush na'o shuwitwane» etke b́teshi.
Man mec'ro b́ woterawo Rbk'aa naruwotssh niho wottsosh Yisak'sh nungush nana'a maatúwotsi b maac'ro,
Ik'i marat' marat'o finon b́woterawo b́s'eegon b́woto kitsosh git nan'úwots boshuwewonat gondonowere sheengonowere bok'aloniyere shino
Ik'o Rbk'ash «Eenfo múk'efosh keewek wotituwe» bí eti.
Manúwere «Yak'obi shunre Esawunmó shit're» ett guut'etsok'one.
Eshe eege noeteti? Ik'o boga bogshirwe eronowa? B́jamon mank'o woteratse!
Ik'oniye Musesh «Bísh doosh tgeyruwosh doowituwe, bísh maac' k'ewo tgeyiruwoshowere maac'o k'ewituwe» etre.
Eshe Ik'i marat'o b́daatset ash shunonat ash finon b́woterawo Ik' dowon b́wottsatsne.
Manatse tuutson S'ayin mas'aafotse Gbs' nugúsosh «Neen tiango kitsr tshútsonowere dats jamatse b́daneetuwok'o woshosh neen naashiyire» ett aap'etso guut'ere.
Mansh eshe Ik'o b́shuntsosh maac'o k'ewefe, b́shuntsonowere k'el kúp'etso woshituwe.
Eshe «Ik'i shunts keewo k'efosh konuwor falratse, béré bí ashuwots bo shuntso bo fintsosh eegishe boon b́ b́s'aamiyiri» err taan aato falfete.
Nee ashono! Ik'onton mooshosh eegoneya nfali? Shalon dozets k'ac'o bín dooztsosh «Eegishe hank'o kaldek'at taan ndoozi?» etosh falituwa?
Eshe shal wozirwo iknaari shali tok'ootse k'ac iko mangosh, k'oshonowere ketts finosh woshde wozosh alo deshatsá?
Ik'o b́fayo kitsosho bíangonowere bek'shosh geeyat t'afiyosh k'antsuwotsi fayi k'ac'uwotsi ayoto k'amare wotiyal eendani?
Han b́ k'aluwere shin mangosh b́k'anitso sheeng b́woto dek'ets k'ac'uwotssh b́mangi ayo kitsoshe.
Sheeng b́ woto dek'ets k'ac'uwotsnmó ayhudiwots mec'rotse b́woterawon Ik'i ash woterawwotsitsnowere noon s'eegree.
Hanwere nebiyiyo Hose'n hank'o eteetsok'one, «Tiash teyawuwotsne ‹Tiashuwotsi› err s'eegetuwe, Shuneerawu ashuwotsnowere ‹Shuneeka› err s'eegetuwe,
Itiye ‹Tiashuwots itnaaliye› eteets beyokoke ‹Beyat beets Ik'o nanaúwotsi› err boon s'eegetuwe.»
Isayasuwere Israe'el jangosh hank'o eton b́ k'ááro eenshdek'tine b́keewi, «Isra'el nanaúwots taawo aats k'aritsi shiyok'o dab bíayiyaloru boyitse kashituwots múk'nee.
Doonzo b́ ja'arawo kááronat s'eenon bí angsho imetwe.»
Mank'owere Isayas «Dari jirwotssh doonzo shooko noosh oriyo b́k'azink'ere Sedom kituk'o wotiyank'one b́teshi Gemor kitukok'o wotiyank'one b́teshi» ett shin shin keewure.
Eshe eege no keewiti? Kááwi weero sha'erawu Ik'i ash woterawwots kááw woto bodaatsi, kááwo wotonwere amanar daatsetuwoniye.
Ernmó kááw woto daatsit nemo shuuts sha'at teshts Isra'elots, nemo s'eentsosh bomawutsotse kááwok boratsne.
«Eegoshe kááwok bodobok'azi?» eteyala bo kááw wottso daatsosh boge amanon b́woterawon finon b́wottsotsne, manshe t'ugwotsn bo k'is'eyi.
Manuwere «Hambe! ashuwotsi k'is'iru shútso S'iyonits beezree, Shútsanuwere ashuwotsi k'ic'de'er dikitu s'aloniye, Bín amanituwonmó jiitsratse» ett guut'etsok'one.
Ti eshuwotso! t maac'otse beyiru een tewunonat Ik'o maants t t'intsiru k'onon Israe'el ashuwots bokashituwok'owe.
Ari danon woto b́ k'aztsosha bako bo Ik'osh okooro bo detstsok'osh taa boosh gawituwe.
Ik'o ashuwotsi kááw b́ woshit weerindo bodartsotse bo took kááw weerona bosha'i bako Ik' kááw weeron sha'eratsnee.
Ash jamo imnetiyon kááwo b́ wotish nemi s'uwo Krstosiye.
Nem kotón daatset kááw woto Muse b́ guut'tso «Nemo fenats jitsiru jamo kashon beetuwe» etiruwoniye.
Ik'o ashuwotsi imnetiyon kááw b́ woshtsok'onomó hank'o ett guut'ere, «N nibon daro maants kone kesheti?» etk'aye, hanúwere Krstosi orshoshe,
Wee n nibon «Si'olits kone ot'eti?» etk'aye, hanúwere Krstosi k'irotse tizoshe.
Dabtnu hank'o ett guut'ere, «Ik' aap'tso n ganoke, dab nnononat n maac'otse,» keewanúwere no nokeewiiru imneti aap'oniye.
Iyesus doonz b́wotok'o nnonon ngawiyal, Ik'o k'irotse bín b́tiztsok'o n maac'on niamaniyal kashitune.
Asho b́ maac'on amanar kááwituwe, b́nonon b́ gawiyal kashituwe,
S'ayn mas'aafotse guut'etsok'on, «Bín amants jamo jitseratse.»
Eshe ikosh doonz wottso jamosho doonz b́wottsosh ayhudiyonat ayhudiy woteraw dagotse eegoru k'osh k'osheyo aaliye, bín k'oniru jamosh b́s'aato ayide'er imetuwe,
«Doonzo shúúts s'eegiru jamo kashituwe» eteere.
Ernmó bo amaneraniyere aawuk'oneya s'eegosh bofaliti? B́ jango booshiyaniyere aawuk'oneya bo amaniti? Nabirwo alonomó aawuk'oneya shishosh bo faliti?
Nabirwotsi wosheerawonomó aawuk'oneya nabosh bo faliti? Hanuwere, «Doo keewuman shishituwots wáá woo awuk'owe b́geneúshiti!» ett guut'etsok'one.
Ernmó Isayas, «Doonzono! no no aap'tso kone amani» ett b́ keewtsok'o, jamwots doo shishiy keewo de'atsne.
Eshe imnetiyo b́ daatset k'ebokne, k'ebetuwonúwere Ik'i aap'otsoniye.
Aab aatuna, eshe, b́ keewts keewo shiyatsno eteya? S'ayin mas'aafotse, «Bo k'aro dats jamats b́shiyeyi, Bo aap'ts aap'onuwere dats daarats b́ bodi» ett guut'etsok'on, arikon shishrne.
Israe'el ashuwots b́ aap'tso danatsno eteya? Han eterawok'o Muse shinon «Gac'ets ash ashon okoriyat itn tgoyni, T'iwitsrawu ash ashon itn tfayi» eteere.
Isayasuwere, «Taan geerawwotssh tdatseyi, ‹Ik'o aawoke?› ett Taan aatrawwotssh tbe'eyi,» ett ááwushúk'on keewure.
Israe'el ashuwotsshomó «Azazerawonat gond ashuwots tmaants boweetwok'o aawu jamo tkishuwotsi t jargi» etre.
Aab́ dab neen aatuna, Ik'o bí ashuwotsi juuwera? B́ jamon juweratse! taa ttookon Israe'el ash taane, Abraham naaro wotat Bíniyam jirots taane.
Ik'o shini b́ marat'ts ashuwotsi juweratse, S'ayn mas'aafo Eliyas jangosh eeg bíettsok'o gawatsteya? Dab Eliyas Israe'el ashuwotsi Ik' shinatse awuk'o ett b́ s'aamitsok'o danatsteya?
Manoor Eliyas «Doonzono! nebiyiwotsi úd'rne wosh t'intseyiru t'arap'ezono gaakrne, ts'uziye oori, taano úd'oshe bogeyiri» etre b́ teshi.
Ernmó Ik'o eega ettniya bísh bíaani? «Ba'ali eteets dozets ik'osh tuk'umalerawo shawat kúm ashuwotsi ttokish ooridek're» etre bísha.
And dúranatse b́wotsiyal, s'aaton marat'ere ortsuwots muk' Israe'el ashuwots fa'ane.
Marat'onwere s'aaton b́ wotiyal finonaliye etee, finon b́ wotiyal, s'aato s'aat b́ woto orerere etee.
Eahe b́ k'awuntso eebi b́wotiti? Esra'el ashuwots bogetso datsatsno, marat'etswotsmó bo geyiruwo daatsrne, oortsuwotsmó bo maac'o bokup'i.
Hanuwere «Ik'o bo nibo b́ dúngiyi, mansh eshe hambetsish b́ borfetso bo ááwo be'atse, boowazonuwere shiyatse» ett guut'etsok'one.
Dawitwere, «Bomishi maronu detset kambo, dikit gop'o wotar boon kic'ituwe! bofiniru gond fino botokats boree!
Bo ááwo b́ be'awok'o t'aluwowe, bojik'o gond bek'on jam aawo k'urowe» etre.
Aab́ aani neen aatuna, ayhudiyots bodihi aani boturawok'o wotatniya? Mank'owaliye! ernmó ayhudiyots gondo bo fintsi jangosh Ayhudi woterawwots kasho bodaatsi, han b́wotiye ayhudiyots Ayhudi woterawwotsi bo ookoritwok'o woshoshe.
Ayhudiyots gond fino dats jamosh deero datsire, bodiho Ik' ash woterawotssh deero wotere, Ayhudi jamwots bookashink'ee deero awuk'o aye b́wotiyank'oni!
And nokeewir itsh Ik' ash woterawwotsshe, Ik' ash woterawwotssh wosheetso twottsok'osh t finosh mango taash shiyeetuwe,
T meets jag wotts ayhudiwotsi okooriyoshe, mank'onowere daneraka ik ikuwotsi kashiyo falituwe etee.
Ik'o boon b́ juwoor datsatsi ash k'oshuwots Ik'onton b́ manetka wotiyal Ik'o boon b́ dek'or eeg b́wotituwok'o arefa? Haniyere k'irotse tuwok'oyi etee!
Ik naari boot'otse shintsotsi kayo S'ayinka wotiyal boot' jamo S'ayinkee b́ wotiti, mank'o mit iko b́s'ap'o S'ayina wotiyal b́ jabwotswere S'ayine bowotiti.
Worfitsi woyra eteyiru mit jaabo wotts ayhudiyots k'ut'eyar bodihitka wotiyal it boditsi woyiriy mit jaabo wotts Ik' ash woterawwots bo shegro shááto shegrshr weyiri zeyito bítse b́keshiru s'ap'ootse keshiru gaalonat deeron kaytsuwotsi itwotiyakon, b́ jaabwotsats ít'k'ayere.
It Ik' ash woterawotso jaabwotsats ít'k'ayere, it it'alomó it jaab mec'ro it wottsosh s'ap'oni itn kuriti bako it b́ s'ap'o kurirwotsi itwoterawok'o dande'ere.
Ernmó «Jabúwots tishat bodihi, taa bo beyok tikinditwok'o» etaatne b́ teshi.
It ettso aree, ernmó bo k'ut'at bojuwe amano bok'aztsosh b́ wottsotse itwere k'up'at it ned'iye itamantsoshe, eshe, shata bako hit'o itn geyiratse.
Ik'o azeewon jaab wotts ayhudiyotssh maac'o k'ewo b́ k'aziyakon itsh maac'o k'eweratse.
Eshe Ik' doowonat Ik' shatiyon aab s'iilere, b́ shatiyonu b́kitsir dihitswotsats b́ wotor b́ doo wotonu b́ kitsir itshee, hanowere b́k'alir b́ dowon k'up'ar it betka wotiyalemó b́ doo itsh wotituwe, kup'o itk'azalomó itwere k'ut'eyarniye it dihiti.
Ayhudiyots bo amaniyal yoots bobeyok aanitune, Ik'o yoots bobeyok boon aaniyosh falituwe.
It Ik' ash woterawwotsmó azeyon boditsi woyiri miti jaabo wotat teshtsuwots it beyokalo worfotsi woyiri mitats tokeyo it faliyakon hanots bo azeyon worfitsi woyiri miti jaabo wotts ayhudiyotsmó yoots bobeyok aanar tokeyo aawuk'oneya boosh b́ maaweeti!
Ti eshuwotso! «Danfone» err it'k'ayere itsh tkeewitwo ááshts keewo fa'ee, bíwrer Israe'el ashuwots k'azts woto b́ jamosh b́woterawo Ik' ash Woteraw jamwots s'eenon Ik'ok bowafetsoshe.
Eshe hank'on Israe'el asha ash jamwots kashitúne. Mansh hank'o ett guut'ere, «Kashituwo S'iyonn weetuwe, Yak'ob naar jamatse gondo wokiituwe,
Bomorro boosh t t'afiyor bonton tkindit taaro haniye.»
Israe'el ashuwots doo shishiyosh aap'etso dek'o bok'aztsotse, itjangosh it Ik' ash woterawotssh b́dooyish Ik'osh balangaro bowoti, bomarat'ewonmó nihiwots jangats tuutson Ik'o boon shunknee.
Ik'o noon marat'de'er b́ deero bí imiyakon b́ k'alts keewumansh b́gawtso woniratse.
It Ik' ash woterawwots shin Ik'osh alerawwotsiye it teshi, andomó ayhudiyots aleyo bok'aztsotse it Ik' maac' k'ewo it datsi.
It maac' k'ewo it daatstsok'on boowere maac' k'ewo bodatsituwok'o boowere and Ik'osh alerawwotsi woterne.
Ik'o b́ maac' k'ewo ash jamosh kitsosha ett ash jamwotsi ale k'azon is'k'reroshná.
Ik' gaalona, dani teleefonat danoonúwere awuk'o eene! bí angsho fal bíats boderake, b́ werindonu danerake.
«Ik' hasabiyo danetuwo kone? Bísh iztsi wotituwonmó kone?
Ik'osh gushituwonat b́ gushitsono dek'etuwo kone?»
Jam keewo b́ daatse bíyokne, jam keewo bíne b́beeti, jam keewo bíshe b́ beeyeti, dúre dúron mango bísh wotowe! Amen!
Eshe eshuwotso! Ik'o genee'úshitwo, beyar beetwonat S'ayin wosho woshde'er it atso it t'intsitwok'o maarts Ik'o shútson itn k'onirwe. Manowere t'intso itn b́ geyitso ari Ik'osh finet finoniye.
Sheengonat genee'úshitwo kim deshawonowere Ik'o shuntso fadbek'o it falitwok'o it nibi gawirwon handraar, it beyo woneewa bako datsani ark'ayere.
Aaninuwere it ik ikets Ik'o itsh b́imts imnetiyok'on tooko dashan detson asaabore bako it angoniyere danb it tookosh bogotaane err asaabk'ayere ett taash imets s'aaton keewirwe.
No ats ikatse ay kayuwots fa'ane, noatsi kay ik ikonuwere k'osh k'osh fino detsfe.
Mank'owere noo ayuwotsi wotat nobefere Krstosn ik ats noone, ik atsi kayuwotsi nowottsok'on noatsatsewo desheeknone.
Mansh Ik'o b́ s'aaton noosh b́ ímts k'osh k'osh naari deero finats jiitswone, noosh imetso Ik'o aap'ts keewa wotiyal no amantsok'on Ik' aap'tso keewwone.
Noosh imetso k'oshwotssh fina wotiyal kup'ar finone, noosh imetso daniya wotiyal sheengshde'er daniwone,
noosh imetso iza wotiyal izwone, noosh imetso tuwdi dowawotiyal nib s'eenon imone, noosh imetso ashuwotsi k'eeza wotiyal kup'ar k'eezwone, noosh imetso mihretiya wotiyal hanowere gene'on k'aluwone.
Git alber deshaw ari shunewo t'ut'k'ayere, gond keewo shid'ere, sheeng keewi shuutso sha'ore.
It ats atsewo eshuwwots shunon shunewere, it ats atsewosh mango imosh nohewere,
mawuk'ayr, Shayron aat'iruwotsi wotoore, doonzosh keewewere.
Jangiyetson gene'owere, gond bek'o k'amoore, jam aawo Ik'o k'onwere.
Amants eshuwotsi bokic'or te'úwere, ibwotsno ibíewre.
Itn gishirwotsi deerwere, derwere bako c'ashk'ayere.
Geneúwirwotsnton gene'ore, epiruwotsnton efere.
It ats atseyo ik hasabiyon ikwotar beewere, it tooko danbaan deshr bog taana eto k'ayr t'owwotsnton ik wotar beewere. It tookosh danfone etk'ayere.
Ash jami shinats sheeng wotts keewo k'aluwere bako, ashuwots itats gond keewo bok'aliyal, it aanide'er gondo boosh k'alk'ayere.
Itsh b́ faleyal ash jamonton jeenon beyosh it weeron it falitu jamo k'aluwere.
T jirwotso! fayo Ik'osh k'ayere boko it it tookon weero oorshk'ayere, «Weer weershtwonat weer worshi gushono anituwo taane etfe Doozo Ik'oni» ett guut'ere.
Mansh weer worshoniyere n balangaro b́k'ak'iyal mazuwe, b́shashuwiyal shashuwo kishwe, hank'o n k'aliyal goyinar b́ jitsituwok'o woshitune.
Mansh gond keewo sheeng keewon da'úwere boko gond keewon da'ek'ayere.
Konuworu naash wottso b́ daatsit Ik' shunon b́ wottssotse and datsk'eziruwots bo naash Ik'on b́ wottsotse ash jamo naashwotssh alewo bísh geyife.
Mansh naashuwotsi k'efitu jamo Ik' aloniye b́k'efiri, aleraw jamonuwere sezi angsheyo b́ tookats dowetuwe.
Dats k'eziruwotsi shatet gond finirwotsi bako sheeng finiruwotsiyaliye, naashuwotsi shat k'azo geefneya? Bére sheeng fino finowe, booke údo daatsitune.
Naasho neesh sheengo b́ k'alituwok'o naashiyets Ik' guutsoniye, dats k'eeziruwo shiki gorado bí'ed hank'on woto b́k'aztsotse gond fintso nwotiyal dats k'eeziruwo share, bíwere gond finiruwotsi sezosh Ik' weer wershono kitsr Ik'osh finitune.
Mansh mengst naashuwotssh alewo itsh geyife, it aletwere Ik' fay mec'ro shatoon b́ woterawo it nibo itn b́ gac'ituwosh woto geyituwe.
Ereero it imiru manshe, naashuwots finan finosh botuu Ik'osh finoshe.
Eshe danbi naashuwotssh k'alo geyituwu jamo k'aluwere, ereero bísh wotituwosh ereero, t'ilisho bísh wotituwosh t'ilisho imere, shatetwono sharere, mango bísh wotituwosho mango imere.
Kon k'awuntsonúwor itatse beek'aye, itatse beeyet k'awuntsoniye itats atseyo shúnee mec'r wotowe, ash shunetuwo nemo finats jitsre.
«Wido amk'aye, úd'́k'aye, úmp'k'aye, k'osh ashk wotts keewu jamo tewunk'aye» etiru tzaziyotsnat k'osh tzazi jamwots, «Asho ntookok'o woshde'er shune» etiru ik tzaziyotse ko'eyat bofa'oni.
Ash shuniru jamo b́ shuniru ash manats gond keewo k'alatse, mansh ash shuniruwo nem jamo finats jitsre etee.
Eshe tokrotse it tuwit sa'ato and b́bodtsok'o dande'ere, shini noamanortsoniyere bogo and no kashit aawo iki nomaants t'inre.
T'úwonu beshe b́ beshiri, aawonu t'inree, eshe t'aluwotse fineyiru finon fink'ayone, sháánon bin finet kes'i tahono tahade'one.
Weral míshon, mashon, widonat máátsonat nungushi iko ikats keshon, fayonat okooron b́ woterawo aawu shanon beyiruwu ashuwotskok'o s'ayinon sha'owone.
Eshe Doonzo Iyesus Krstosi tahade'ere bako it meets shuni shashuwo kishosh gawuk'ayre.
Ititse b́ imnetiyon maawuk wotts asho b́ keewo de'ere bako b́ took asaabiyats moosho tuuzk'ayere.
Dab ash iko konnari keewo móósh faliyit imnetiyo detsetwe, b́ imnetiyon kup'eraw ashonmó worfi maay mec'ro meetuwe.
Mansh jam keew meyiru asho mááraw asho gac'k'aye, máárawonwere meet asho ats angshk'aye, Ik'o bínowere dek're.
Bére, ash k'oshi guutso ats angshiruwan nee kone? Bí b́ need'iyal wee b́ dihiyal b́ doonzo kis'e. Dab Ik'o bín need'iyo b́ falituwotse kup'ar need'ituwe.
Mank'o aawu iko aawu ikoniyere bogo mangfe et gawiruwo beyo falituwe, ando k'oshonu aawu jamwots mango taale bako aawwotsitse bogabogo aaliye ett asaabirwe. Eshe hanan arts keewwotsatse asho ik ikon b́nibots bíamantsok'o woshuwe.
Ik aawo k'osh aawoniyere bogshde'er mangiyituwo b́ beyal han b́ k'alirwe doonzo mangosha ettniye, jam naari mishono meyiruwo doonzo mangosha etniye b́meyiri, b́ meyiru mishosh Ik'o údituwe, jam naari mishono marawo doonzo mangosha err maratse, maa b́ k'aztsotsno Ik'o údituwe.
Noyitsere ikonuworu b́ kashon wotowa b́ k'iron b́tokkaliye.
Nobeyalo doonzosha nobeeti, no k'iriyalo doonzosha no k'iriti, eshe nobeyalo, nok'iriyalo doonzok noone,
Eshe Krstos k'irt k'irotse b́ tuu kashon betuwotsnat k'irtsuwotssh doonz wotoshe.
Bére, nee n eshuwats eegoshe n angshiri? Wee ni eshuwi eegishe n gac'iri? No únets Ik' angshi jori shinats ned'ituwone.
Manwere, «Taa kashon betuwo taane etfe Ik'oni, Ash jamo b́ gurbon tshinatse tuk'umalituwe, B́ alberon taa Ik' twottsok'o gawituwe» ett guut'ere.
Eshe notook tookon no took fini jangosh Ik' shinats t'inr aatetwone.
Eshe iko ikats angshk'aye, ernmó asho b́ eshuwsh weratse kambo wee t'úgo gedk'azosh no atso korde'one.
Ik keewo kiime err asaabiru ashosh keew man kima b́ wotiti bako kon naari keewonworu b́ tookon kim b́ woterawok'o taa doonzo Iyesusn t'iwintsdek' danre.
Nee n meyiru mishi jangon ni eshush t'ugo n wotiyal shúnonaliye nbeyiri, eshe Krstos bísh b́k'irts asho n meyiru mishi jangon b́ t'afitwok'o woshk'aye.
Eshe itoke sheeng keew wotts keewo k'oshuwots bok'efetuwok'o woshk'ayere.
Ik' mengsto S'ayin shayiron datsetsetk kááwe, jeenonat gene'ona bako, móónat úshi keewaliye.
Han jangosh Krstissh guuts wotts asho Ik'o geneúshituwe, ashoknowere údeek wotituwe.
Eshe jeenwoto bín datsetuwonat no ats atseyo bín nokup'it keewon sha'owone.
Mishi jangosh Ik' fino gakk'ayone. Mish jamo s'ayine, ernmó k'osh ashosh t'ug wotitu mish móó dáree.
Eshe ni eshúsh t'úg wotk'azosh meetso maak'azo, Weyinyon dútsets biro úsh k'azo, wee kon naari t'ug wotituwo fino fin k'azo sheenge b́ wotiti.
Eshe imnetiyan itnat Ik' dagots wotowe, err n amants keewo b́k'alor b́ maac'o bín b́gac'erawu asho údekee.
B́ amaneraniyere meyiru ashonmó b́ k'aliruwo imnetiyatse tuutson wot b́ k'aztsosh bíyats angshetuwe, imnetiyon k'aleraw keewu jamo morre.
No imnetiyon kúp wottswots, mawirwots kuro kurdek'o geyife bako no took mec'ro geneúshitu woto geyiratse,
no took tookon k'osh asho b́ imnetiyon b́ kup'ituwok'o bín t'ak'amituwonat geneúshit keewo k'aluwone.
Krstos b́ tooko geneúshratse, dab «Ashuwots neen boc'ashts c'asho ti'ats b́ oot'i» etiru S'ayn mas'aafotse eteetso bí ats b́ bodi.
S'ayin mas'aafotse nodatsituwots k'amonat kup'on, noosh jángo b́beetuwok'o shin guut'ets jamo dano noosh b́ wotituwok'o guut'ere.
Ik níbon wotde'er ik noonon Ik'o nodoonz Iyesus Krstos nihi, bín it mangitwok'o, k'amikonat angi kúp'iko Ik'o Izar Izewer Krstos Iyesus shunok'on it atsatsewo ik níbetsuwotsi woto itsh ime.
<range>
Krstos Ik' mangosh itn b́ dek'tsok'o it jamets iko iko de'e.
Hanowere t keewor Ik'o shints nihuwotssh b́ jangitso b́ wotituwok'onat Ik'o arikeewets b́ wotonwere b́ danetuwok'o Krstos ayhudiyotssh guutso wotere etee.
Krstos ayhudiyots guutso b́ wottso k'osh jango Ik' ash woterawwots Ik'o b́ mhretiyosh bín bo údituwok'owe, hanuwere, «Eshe Ik' ash woterawwots dagotse neen udituwe, n shúútsosh dubon údo t'intsituwe» ett guut'etsok'one.
Aaninu «It Ik' ash woterawotso, Ik' ashuwotsnton gene'owere!» ett guut'ere.
Aaninuwere, «Ik' ash Woteraw jamwots! doonz údoore, Ash ash jamwotswere údoore!» ett guut'ere.
Ando Isiyas, «Iseyi naarotse shuwetuwo weetuwe, Ik' ash woterawwotssho jishituwo wotar tuwituwe, boowere bojangtso biyats woshdek'etune» etfe.
It jangtso S'ayin shayiri angon eenfere b́ ametuwok'o jangetso Izar Izewer bín it amanetsosh gene'únat jeenon s'eenon itsh ime.
Ti eshuwotso! doo woton s'eentsuwotsi, danon gaaltsuwotsnat it ik iketsuwots k'osho izosh falituwotsi itwottsok'o danre.
Ik ik keewwotsi itsh gawiyosh geeyat woshan Ik'o taash b́ imts s'aatok'on ááwushuk'on itsh guut're.
Deeranuwere taash b́ime Ik'o doo shishi keewo Ik'i ashwoterawwotssh shishiyosh kahniyo wotat Krstos Iyesush finoshe, Mansh Ik' ashwoteraw ashuwotssh S'ayin shayiro S'ayintsonat Ik'onowere gene'úshit wosho wotáár bot'inetuwok'o finiruwone.
Manatse tuutson Krstos Iyesun Ik'osh fino tfaltsotse it'iruwee.
Ik'i ash woterawwots bo aletwok'o woshosh Krstos ti aap'onat finatse tuutson b́ fints keewo wotiyalabako k'osho aap'osh aawo shu'atse.
Hank'owere een adits milikit finuwotsn S'ayin shayiri angon Iyerusalemnat b gúúratse tuut Elwarik'oni b́ borfetso Krstos doo shishiyo danire.
Jam aawu t tewuno k'osh asho b́ agtsats dabr ago b́woterawo Krstos shutso b́ shiyerawu beyok jamok sheeng doo shishiyi keewuman daniye.
Hanu, «Haniyere shinon b́ jangosh eegoru keewerawu ashuwots bek'etune, b́ jangosh shiyawwots t'iwitsitunee» ett guut'etsok'one.
Manshowere itmaants twarawok'o ayoto taan baziyeree.
Andomó han gúúratsi fa'a datsuwotsatse t finit beeyokuwots bo beetsotse, hank'o ay dúrosh itn s'ilosh een tewuno tdetstsotse
Ispen maants t amor man weeron itn s'ilosh gawure. Muk' aawosh itnton gene'útsat tteshiyakon twerindo ttuwosh taan falit tep'o it k'alituwok'o jangere.
Andomó Ik' jirwots tep'et gizo deshde'er Iyerusalem maants ametuwe.
Hanuwere Mek'odoniyonat Ak'yiyi datsatse fa'a Ik' jirwots Iyerusalemn beyiru tugúretsuwotssh boon tep'et gizo woshosh boshunon bogawutsotsne.
Tep'anowere bo shunon imo boosh geyik b́wottsotsne, Ik' ash woterawots ayhudiyotsnton shayiri deero kayosh b́wotiyal boowere bomeets deeron ayhudiyotsi tep'o boosh geyife.
Eshe ko'iyets gizan Iyerusalem maants de'am boosh t imiyakon it weeron waar Ispen maants t ameti.
Itok twoor Krstos deero s'eenon itsh de'er tweetuwok'o danfee.
Tieshuwotso! t jangosh Ik'o maants k'onon tmaak'oriruwo taash itdabish nodoonz Iyesus Krstosnat S'ayin shayiri shunon iti k'oniruwe.
Ik'o taash it k'onituwere Yihud datsatsi fa'a amanerawu ashuwots kishotse farr Iyeresalemitse t detsts fiinonuwere Ik'i jirwotsoke dek'eyo b́daatsituwok'owe.
Han b́wotiyakon Ik'o bíetal geneúwon itok waarr itoke kashdek'o shunfee.
Jeeniko Izar Izewer it únetsnton wotowe! Amen.
Feben Knkriy kitotse Ik' moowosh finiru nomish amanetsu b wottsok'o it dano geefe.
Bi taanat k'osh ay ashuwotsi b tep'iruwotse amants ibuwotsi ibiyo boosh b́ wotituwok'o doonzo shútson de'er bish geyit keewo jamon bin it tep'etuwok'o oona itsh etiruwe.
Iyesus Krstos fino finiruwotsnton ik wottsuwots P'rsk'lnat Ak'ilnsh jamo keewwere,
boowere t shegro k'iroshoru dab k'andek'kne boteshi, hann boon jam aawosh úditwe, t s'uzi b́ woterawo Ik' ashwoteraw krstani woto maants aants Ik' moowwotsworu it údirune.
Bo moots Ik' k'onosh kakuwets amantsuwotssh jamo t'intsuwere. Isiyi dats kayatse shini Krstosn amantsonat tshuntso Ep'enet'ossh jamo keewwere.
Itsh ayidek'at maawutsu Mariyamsh jamo t'intsuwere.
Taanton tipeyat teshts woshetswotsitsere daneets teshts ayhudiyots jaagúwots Andronik'osnat Yuniyassh jamo t'intsuwere, boowere taayere shine Krstosi bo amani.
Doonzon tshúntso Amp'ilyat'ossh jamo t'intsuwere,
Krstos finon noonton ik wottso Úrbanosnat tshúntso Ist'akussh jamo t'intsuwere.
Krstosk b́ wottsotse fadeyat bíere bísh gawetso Ap'elissh jamo t'intsuwere, Arst'obulos maa ash wottsuwotssh jamo t'intsuwere.
Ayhudiyotse t jago Herodiyonsh jamo t'intsuwere, Narsises maa ashuwotsitse Doonzon amantsuwotssh jamo t'intsuwere.
Doonzosh finon ayidek't maawirwotssh Trufaynnat Trufolsh jamo t'intsuwere. Doonzo finon ayidek'at mááwtsunat Krstosn ayidek'at tshunts Persissh jamo t'intsuwere.
Doonzosh finon ayidek't danetso Rufossh jamo t'intsuwere, taan b naayikok'o shunfu b́ indshowre jamo t'intswere.
Asnkritosnat Flegonsh, Hermesmsh, Patrobasmsh, Hermasmsh, bonton fa'a eshúwotssh jamo t'intsuwere.
Filologossh, Yulyash, Neryanat b́ mishsh jamo t'intsuwere, hank'o Olumpasnat bínton fa'a amantsuwots jamwotssh jamo t'intsuwere.
S'ayin jobon it atsatseyo jobeyar jamo aatewere. Krstosk wotts Ik' maa jamwots jamo itsh t'intsirune.
Ti eshuwotso! it dek'ts dan man k'efituwotsi wotat it dagotse k'aleyon gond bek'o dowet ashuwotsatse it atso korde'ere, boatsere wokoore!
Hank'o ashuwots botookosha bako Krstosshaliye bo finiri. Bonono shaawshdek' dáshon garaamiwots nibo boant'elciri.
Doo shishi aap'osh aleets ash it wottso ash jamokere b́ danetsotse geneúk t wotwotiyaloru, sheeng keewosh dantswotsi, gond keewoshomó maac' kúp'uwotsi it wotitwok'o geefe.
Jeeniko Izar Izewer káári Shed'ano it tufi shirots tiitsetwe. No Doonz Iyesus Krstos s'aato itnton wotowe.
T finonton ik wottso T'imotiwos jamo itsh t'intsiruwe, eshe ayhudiyotse t jag wotts Luk'iyosnat Iyason Sosip'at'roswere jamo t'intsirune.
Woshhan guut'tso taawe T'ert'iyos Doonzon jamo t'intsituwe.
Taanat hanokere fa'a jamo Ik' moowwotsi Ibiiruwo Gayiyos jamo t'intsiruwe, kitutsi gizo detsiruwo Erast'os, no eshú K'a'rt'os jamo itsh t'intsiruwe.

Taa tdaniru doo shishi keewan Iyesus Krstos jangosh beshiyeyiru woshonat yootstson aashat teshtso, andomó be'ets ari ááshts keewon Ik'onwere it imnetiyats it ned'ituwok'o iti woshosh falituwe.
Andomó arikan be'ere, dúre dúrts Ik'o tzaziyon jamwots amanar bo aletwok'o Nebiywots mas'aafi weeron ash jamwots bo danetuwok'o k'alere.
B́ s'uzn dani teleefo detsts Ik'o Izar Izewersh, Iyesus Krstosn dúre dúron údo wotowe! Amen.
Ik' shunon Iyesus Krstossh wosheets wotosh s'eegetso P'awlosnat no eshu Sostensokere.
K'orontos kitotse fa'a Ik' moosh, biyitsnowere Iyesus Krstosn S'ayin wotts S'ayin bowotish s'eegetswotssh, mank'owero bo be beyoke, bonat nonsh Doonz wottso no Doonz Iyesus Krstos shúútso s'eegiru jamwotssh.
No nihi Ik'onat Doonzo Iyesus Krstosokere s'aatonat jeenon itsh wotowe.
Iyesus Krtosnton s'aato itsh imetsosh it jangosh jam aawo Ik'o údituwe.
Jam keewon, noon keewon wotowa danon Krstosn gaalwutserte.
Krstos jangosh itsh t keewts gawo itokere kúp'ere.
Eshe no Doonz Iyesus Krstos be'ewo koton nobefere kon naari shayiri imo itsh shapratse,
No doonz Iyesus Krstos aani woor eeg eeg deshawwotsi wotar nodatsetwok'o bí s'uwosh b́ borfetsosh kup'ar it beetuewk'o woshúwe.
B́ naay no Doonz Iyesus Krstosnton ikwoto itdetsetuwok'o itn s'eegtso Ik'o amaneke.
Ti eshuwotso! «K'alewo it dagotse b́ berawok'o, it jamets shiyeyar ik níbonat ik s'iil s'iilon kup'ar beewere,» etaat no Doonz Iyesus Krstos shúútson itn k'oniruwe.
T eshuwotso! it dagotse fayo b́ beyiruwok'o K'elo'e maa ashuwotsoke shishre.
Manuwere it itok tookon «Taa P'awlosk taane, taa Ap'losk taane, taa P'et'rosk taane, taa Krstosk taane» it etiri.
Bére Krstos kayera? P'awlos itsh jiitera? Himó it gupe P'awlos shútsoneya?
Taa K'ersp'osnat Gayyosiyere okoon ititsere konnoru t gufawotse Ik'o údituwe.
Eshe «Taan P'awlos shútson guuperte» err keewosh falituwo aaliye. [
Arikee, Ist'ifanos maa ashuwotsi gupre, maniyere okoon k'osho taa t gupts asho b́ bewok'o gawratse.]
Krstos taan b́wosh doo shishi keewo t danituwok'owa bako t gupishaliye, Krstos jiito hank'on b́ oorerawok'o doo shishi keewan tdanir ashoke daatsets dani telfi noon keewok'onaliye.
B́ jiti keewo t'afit ashuwotssh darok'owe b́ taaweti, noosh kashituwotsshomó Ik' angee.
«Dani telefetswots dano t'afituwe, Dani telefetswots danono ok k'aaú bazetuwe» ett guut'ere.
Eshe dantso aawoke b́ fa'oni? Nem daniruwonu aawoke b́ fa'oni? Danosh geyiruwonu aawoke b́ fa'oni? Ik'o datsanatsi dani telefo eegoru bítse dandeshawok'o woshk'rerosha?
Datsnatsi ashuwots bo took danitelefon Ik'o danosh bo falawok'o Ik'o b́ danon boats is'k'rere, ernmó dárok'o taaweyiru no nodaniru doo shishiy keewon amanituwots bo kashituwok'o Ik' shún wotere.
Ayihudiyots adits keewo bek'oshe bo geefoni, Girik ashuwotswere danitelefe bogefoni.
Noomó Krstos noosh b́ jitetsok'oniye no daniri, Hanuwere ayhudiyotssh t'uge, Grik ashuwotssh dáree.
S'eegetswotsshomó ayhudiyotssh wotowa Grik ashuwotssh, Krstos Ik' angonat Ik' danitelefe.
Ik' dára ett gaweyiru keewo ash danitelefoniyere bogfe, Ik'o maawa ett gaweyiru keewo ash kup'oniyere bogfe.
T eshuwotso! Ik'o itn b́ s'eegor awuk'o ash it wottsok'o aab gawde'ere, ash gaawiruwok'on it dagotse aywots daanetsuwots wee kúp'uwots wee een een ashuwots aalne.
Ik'o dantelfetswotsi jitsiyosh datsanatse dartsok'o taawets ashuwotsi b́ marat'i, kúp'uwotsi jitsiyosh datsatse maawtsok'o taawetswotsi b́ marat'i,
Ik'o datsatsi ashuwotsoke fa'ane ett be'eyiru keewwotsi bo berawok'o woshosh datsanatse dash antsonat gac'ets k'awnts deshaw keewo b́ marat'i.
Hanowere b́k'al konwor asho Ik' shinatse b́ tooko dambaan b́deshawok'owe.
Itnomó Ik'o Iyesus Krstosnton ik woto it detsetwok'o b́ woshi, mansh Ik'o Iyesus Krstosn noko danitelefo bíne, noosh noko kááwo bíne, no s'ayinonat no bín nofaritwok'o b́ woshi.
Eshe mas'aafotse guut'etsok'on «It'etuwo b́ beyal Ik'on id'ee.»
Ti eshuwotso! taa itok twoor Ik' jango itsh t gawutso, keew falonat bog dan kitsonaliye.
Itnton t beyor Iyesus Krstosiyere oko dab jitats jiteyat b́ k'ironiyere k'osho eegoru tdanawok'osh k'ut'dek'atniye t teshi.
Eshe itnton t beyor maawk wotat shatonat ay k'eewone tteshi.
T noon keewonat nabo ash danitelefonat noon keew shawshats b́ woterawo Ik' shayiri angaats tep'ekee b́teshi.
Hanowere tk'altso it imnetiyo ash danitelefats b́ woterawo ik' angaats te'ek b́ wotishee.
Ernmó bo shayiri beyon katsuwotssh dantelefi aap'o keewituwone, wotowa eree nokeewitwo datsanatsi danitelefon wee s'uwatse t'afosh wotit datsan k'eeziruwots danitelefoniyaliye.
No no keewiruwonmó Ik'o yoots dúroniye shinon no mangosh b́ k'anitsonat aashat teshts Ik' danitelefoniye.
Datsni k'eziruwitsitsere danitelefo dantso konworu aaliye, danfno wotik'ee mang wotts Doonzo jirawuk'ne b́ tshi.
Wotowa eree mas'aafo, «Ash ááw be'awo, Ash waaz shiyawo, Ash nib gawawo, Ik'o b́ shúntswotssh k'anire» etfe.
Nooshmó Ik'o b́ shayiron aashts man kitsre, Ik' shayiro dashan wokts Ik'oke aashtsonoru b́ oreraniyere jam keewo p'ec'at b́ s'iili.
Ash iko jangosh b́ took shayironiyere okoon b́ gawiruwo dantso kone? mank'o Ik' shayironiyere okoon Ik' gawiruwo dantso konuworu aaliye.
Ik'oke noosh b́ imets keewo nodanish Ik' shayira bako datsanatsi shayiro de'atsone.
Eshe no shayiri keewo shayiron wotts ashuwotssh no danir ashokere daatsets danitelefon b́ woterawo Ik' shayirokere daatsets dantelefone.
Ik' shayiro deshaw meets ashonmó Ik' shayiroke imeyiru imo dek'osh falatse, bí im eenonuwere p'ec'ar b́s'ilet Ik' shayiron b́wottsotse t'iwints dek'osh falatse, hanuwere bísh darok'owe woshder b́ s'ileti.
Ik' shayir detsts jamonmó jam keewo p'ec'ar s'iilo falituwe, b́ took keewonomó konuwor p'ec'ar s'iilo falatse.
Hanu, «Doonzo gawiruwo kone danosh faliti? Bísh izosh falituwo kone?» Ett guut'etsok'one. Noomó Krstos nibo detsfone.
T eshuwotso! taa iti t daniyor meets asho Krstosats kúp'eraw na'i marmat'ok'o it wottsok'ona bako shayiretswotsk'o it wottsoshaliye.
Kúp' mish moo máá falaaw na'i marmat'ok'o it wottsotse taa itsh t maanztso ezaa bako kúp' mishaliye, andoor b́ wotiyal kúp' mish moo falrafa'ate.
It andoru meets ash itne, it ats atseyo it okoreyirwotsnat it mosheyirwotse meets ash itnosha? it finirwore k'osh ashok'owosha?
Iko «Taa P'awlosk taane» k'osho «Taa Ap'losk taane» bí etor datsanatsi ash itnosha?
wotowa bako Ap'los kone? P'awlos kone? boowere it itk'alirwok'o k'alts guutsne, botook tookon bo finir Doonzo botook tookon boosh b́ eezts finoniye,
Taa ttooki, Ap'los aatso b́ ishi, eenshtsonmó Ik'oniye.
Eshe bos'man enshtso Ik'oni bako tooktsonu aats ishirwonu eegnaliye.
Tooktso wotowa aats ishtsonu taalne, bo took tookon bofintsok'o bo k'awntso dek'etune.
No Ik'osh tohar finit guutswots noone, itmó Ik' goshonat Ik' agiru maa itne.
Ik' taash b́imts s'aatok'on maa agiru s'ekok'o agoko need'itdek'i, koshonu taa need'itsmanats bíagi, ernmó ik iko manats awuk'o bíagiruwok'o t'iwintso bísh geyife.
Ikn ned'yetsmantsere okoon konuworu k'osho ned'iyosh falatse, need'yokanwere Iyesus Krstosiye.
Ned'okanats awntson, wee ambaron wee k'awunts shaaw shúútson, mitoon, tootson wee buyon agetuwo b́beyal
ik ik asho b́ fino b́be'et angshiy aawo weetuwe, manots aaw ik ik asho b́ fino awuk'o b́ wotok'o tawon fadere be'etuwe.
Gmbi agf iko bíagtso tawon b́fadeyor mic'aniyere b́ oriyal b́ k'awntso daatsituwe.
B́ fino tawon mic'r t'afitu agtsonmó t'ut'etuwe, wotoa eree bí b́tookon tawotse beshat mic'aniyere oorts ashok'o kashituwe.
Ik' maa it wottsok'onat Ik' shayiro ititse b́ beyiruwok'o danatsteya?
Eshe asho Ik' moo b́ gakal Ik'o bín gaketuwe, Ik' mooniye S'ayine, Ik' maa S'aynwotswere itne.
Konworu b́ tooko ant'elck'aye, datsanatse danitelefetso araar be'etwo fa'e wotiyal Ik'oki arik wottso danitelefo b́datsish b́ tooko dartsok'o taawwe.
Datsatsi danitelefo Ik' shinatse dáree, hanu, «Ik'o dani telefetswotsi bogond finon detsetwe» ett guut'etsok'one.
Hank'owere, «Doonzo dani telefetsuwots asaabiyo k'awuntso b́deshawok'o danfee» ettso guut'ere.
Eshe jam keewo itk b́wottsotse konworu ashon it'k'aye.
P'awlosi wotowa, Ap'losi b́ wotowa, P'et'rosi wotowa, Datsan wotowa, kasho wotowa, k'iro wotowa, and beyiruwo wotowa, shuuts wetuwo wotowa, jámonwor itkee.
Itmó Krstos nanaúwots itne, Krstoswere Ik' na'ee.
Eshe ash jámo noon Krstos guutswotsi nowottsok'o Ik'oke aashtso kitso adaro boosh imetswotsk'o woshde noon taawwe.
Adar dek'tswotswere amanetswotsi wotar daatsewo boosh geyife.
T jangosh b́wotitka wotiyal itwoor tiyats itangshiyal wee k'osh asho tiyats b́angshiyal eegonor kic'eratse, arikon taawor dab ttookats angsho falatse.
Taa tdantsok'oyi wotiyal tnibo taan gac'eratse, hanuwere taa s'ayin twottsok'owo kitsratse, ernmó tiyats angshituwo doonzo s'uziye.
Mansh bíaawo b́ borawo, doonzo angshosh b́waftsere shino konatsor angshk'ayere, bí b́woor t'aluwotse ááshtso mist'iriyo shanomaants kishituwe, ashuwots nibotse ááshts hasabiyo kishituwe, manoor ik ikon Ik'oke bísh wotit údono daatsituwe.
Eshuwwotso! iti t'ak'amosha etaat keewanats taanat Ap'losi aridek'at tkeewi, hanowere tk'al «Guut'etsatse beshk'aye» etiru izi biitso no atse it danetuwok'wa etaatniye, mansh ash ikon it'o k'oshonowere gac'o geyiratse itsha.
Nee k'oshuwotsiyere eegneya nbogi? K'oshoke nde'aw keewo eebi fa'oni? Eshe jam keewo k'oshoke ndek'ka wotiyal de'aw ashok'o eegoshe n it'iri.?
Andere itsh geyiru keew jamo daatsrte, andere galetswotsi wotertee, no atse k'aleyat naashwtserte, arikon it naashka wotink'ere, noowere itnton toowar nonaashitwotse it naashonuwere sheenge b́wotiyank'oni,
Ik'o noon b́woshtswotsi k'iro boatsats angshr bo úd'etuwoki beewok de'amet ashuwotsitse shutstsuwotsi noon b́wooshtsok'o arefee, manatse tuutso dats jamatse melakiwotsnat ashuwots shinatse miis'i mit wotatniye nobe'eyiri,
Noo Krstos jangosha etaat dogwotsi woterone, itmó Krstosn ayidek'at dantsuwotsi wotwutserte, mank'owere noo mawtswotsi woterone, itmó kup'uwotsi woterte, it mangiyeyirwotsi woterte, noomó keteyeyiruwotsi woterone.
And b́ wotiyaloru and sa'atansh b́ borfetso nok'ak'iri, no shashúwiri, no aratsiri, no jot'eyiri beyoko t'út'at hake bako nojawriri.
No kishon finat ango nomaawiri, noon bo c'ashor noderiri, noon bo gishor no k'amiri,
noon boc'ashonat noshútso bot'afiyor maac' nefon boosh no aaniri, andish b́ borfetso datsanatse juwetsok'onat datsatse fokets kímo woterone.
Taa han itsh tguut'ir shuneets tnana'úwotsk'o woshdek'at izosh gawatni bako iti jiitsiyo geyatniyaliyee.
Krstosn jishiru ayuwotsi it detsalor nih ayuwotsi deshatste, taayere itn Iyesus Krstos doo shishiyon shuure.
Mansh tjafro sha'ar taan it arituwok'o iti k'oniruwe.
Hanatse tuutson shuneetsonat amanets doonzon t naayi wottso T'imotiyosi itsh woshere, b́ be beyokenowere Ik'i maa mooke t daniyirwok'o bí taa Krstosn t daatsts handr beyon bín it jishetuwo itsh gawituwe.
Ernmó ititse ik ikuwots taa itn s'iilo twarawok'o boosh bí arere kofangon s'eenwtserne.
Ernmó doonzon tooh karn aawotse itok weetuwe, manoor kofangirwanots bo noon keew s'uzi b́woterawo bokúp' kúp'onor dano geefe.
Ik'i mengsto noon keewi kis' b́ woterawo Ik'i kúp'e.
It geyirwo eebi? Sezi gumbo de'er it maants twoo geeftee? Himo shunonat tooko dashan detsi shayiron twoone it geyi?
Ititse jitsits widi fino b́beyok'o keeweyiruwe, han naari widi fino dab Ik'i ash woterawwotsoke k'alekaliye, manuwere b́ nih máátsu máátsok'o woshdek't beyiruwo fa'ee eteefe.
Eshe, hank'o jitsits keewo ititse b́ befere eegoshe bognone etaat it míshiri? Maniyere dab keewanatse tuutso shiyano itsh geyiratsa? Han naari fino fints asho ititse kishuwere.
Taa meetson dab itnton woto tk'azalor shayiron itntoniye tfa'oni, ar itnton tbeyiruk'o wotde'er han naari fino k'alts ashaats Doonzo Iyesus shúútson angshuwere,
It kakwewor taawere nodoonz Iyesus angon it dagotse shayiron tdaatsetuwotse,
Morron s'eents ashaan meetso b́ gáhituwok'o Shed'anosh imo itsh geyiyank'ee. Han it k'alitwere doonzo Iyesus angshosh b́weyi aawots ashaan kashu bkashituwok'wee.
Eshe it it'o shengaliye, boot' shash múk'naú boot' jamo b́ shashituwok'o danatsteya?
And it wotts jamok'o boot' shasho bítse deshaw handr boot'ok'o it wotish boot'i nato ok juuk'rore, nofazigi mereer wottso Krstos shukeere,
Mansh gondonat gondon s'eents boot'i shashon b́woterawo boot' shasho bítse deshaw kaawonat ari tushon nobaaliyo mangiwone.
Haniyere shin itsh tguut'ts woshatse gobetswotsnton ik wotk'ayere etreb́teshi.
Han tietoorowere b́ jamon datsanatsi gobetsuwotsatse wee jaalets ashuwotsatse wee úmp'etswotsatse wee woteraw Ik'o ik'iyrwotston iko wotk'ayere etaliye, mank'o b́wotink'ere datsuatse kesho itsh geyife etee.
Taayere itsh tguut' krstiyaniyotsi etefere wido sha'iruwotsnton, k'awntiruwotsnton, Woteraw Ik'o ik'iruwotsnton, wee ash shúúts t'afiruwotsnton, wee mashiruwotsnton, wee biik'iruwotsnton ik wotk'ayere etniye. Hanotsk'o ashuwotsnton towaar maak'ayere.
Krstiyaniwots mabariyoniyere úre fa'a ashuwotsats angshosh kone taa? Krstiyaniwots mabariyatse fa'úwotsatsnmó itwoor angsho faliyalkitneya?
Úratse fa'a ashuwots jango angshituwo Ik'oniye, eshe mas'aafo bíetiruwok'on «Gond asho ititse kishuwere.»
Ititsere iko bí eshu amantsonton b́ fayeyal b́ keewman amantsuwots angshon bísh bo s'iiletwok'o b́ k'aloniyere s'amiyosh Ik' ash woteraw angshiruwots shinats daamosh ááweya b́ shúk'eti?
Ik' ashuwots datsatsi ashaats bo angshituwok'o danatsteya? eshe, datsanatse angshiruwots it wotor keew muk'anats angshosh maawituteya?
Melakiwotsats dab it angshitwok'o danatsteya? eshe, datsanatsi keewwotsats bogshde aawuk'oneya angsho nomaawiti?
Eshe it took tookon it fayeyal krstyaniwots ik mabariyoniyere úratsi gac'ets ashuwots shinats bokeew man aawuk'oneya it t'intsituteya?
Hano tíetir it jitsituwok'owa etaatniye, wotowa ére eshuwotsitsere angsh falitu dants eenasho datseyalkeya?
Eshe, ik krstiyaniyo k'osh krstiyaniyo s'amir Ik' ashwoterawwotsok angshi moots daamo geyiyituwa?
Eshe it took tookon s'amiyeyar mooshewo b́tookon itsh it took keetiye, maniyere iti dadewo k'aneratsa? mank'o iti dirshewo k'aneratsa?
Itmó it eshuwotsi wotts krstiyaaniwotsnoor dadaat itdirshiri.
Eshe weergondetswots Ik'i mengsto bonaarawok'o danftooshna? Keewhan jangatsno daand k'ayere, gusiyetswots, wee woteraw Ik'o ik'iruwots, wee gobetsuwots, wee gad'ayirwots,
Wee úmp'etswots, wee jaaletswots, wee máshetsuwots, wee ash shúúts t'afifuwots, wee biik'tswots Ik'i mengsto naaratsno.
Ititsnor ik ikuwots mank'o itne b́teshi, andmó Doonzo Iyesus Krstos shútsonat noko Izar Izewer shayiron morrotse mash bazrte, Ik'osh gaalets S'ayin ashuwotsi wotat, kááwerte.
«Jam keewo taash baziyeratse,» ernmó jamkeewo taash t'ak'amituwe etaliye, jam keewo taash baziyeratse, wotowa ére keew jamosh guuts wotarr kéweratse,
«Misho maac'osha, maac'onwere mishooshe,» bere Ik'o, mishonowere, maac'onowere t'afituwe, ernmó no atso Doonzo Iyesussh, Doonzo Iyesuswere no atsosh b́wottsotse noatso widosh wosho geyiratse.
Ik'o Doonzo Iyesusi k'irotse tuuzre, nonowere bíangon k'irotse tuuzituwe.
It atso Krstos atsi k'at' b́ wottsok'o danatsteya? Eshe Krstos aatsi kayo de'er gobets maatsu aatsi kayo b́ wotituwok'o wosho taash geyifa? B́ jamon woteratse!
Máátsok gobo amr binton k'etuwo bínton ik atso bo wotituwok'o danatsteya? «Gituwots ik atse bo wotiti» ett guut'ere.
Doonzo Iyesusnton ik wotit ashonmó bínton shayiron ik wotituwe.
Mansh widatse wokoore, asho b́finiru k'osh morr jamo b́took atsoniyere okoone b́ finiri wid amiru ashonmó b́ took aatsatse morro b́finiri,
It atso Ik'oke it dek'tsonat ititse beyiru S'ayin shayirosh Ik' maa b́ wotok'o danatsteya? Eshe it Ik'k itna bako it tokik itnaliye.
Bíwere itn k'awuntson keewere, mansh it aatson Ik'o mangiwere.
Taash guut'at it attso, asho máátsonton gonkewo b́k'azink'ere shege.
Ernmó widatse wokoosh nungush ik iko b́ took máátso de'e, mááts ik ikunu b took kenihosh máátso amiye.
Keniho b́máátsush k'alo bín geyitu de'eyi niwo bísh bazik'aye, mank'o máátsu bkenihsh k'alo bish geyit de'eyi niwo bísh bazik'ayiye.
Máátsu bi atsatse alo deshatsane, biatsatse alo detstso b kenihiye. Mank'owere keniho bíatsatse alo deshatse, bí atsatse alo detstsu máátsuniye.
Kup'ar Ik' k'onosh it gitets ik wotde manorush b́wotiyala bako k'aleyon iko ikosh de'eyi niwo bazik'aye. Manatse tuutson it tooko kordek'o maawr it eree shed'ano it ats fadewo b́doorawok'o aani towaar wotoore.
Han itsh tietir izook'owa bako tzaziyok'owaliye.
Ash jamo tikok'o máátso b́de'aawo b́beyink'ere shunfee b́teshi, ernmó Ik'o ik ikosh k'osh k'osh imo imre, iko ik naari imo, k'oshnuwere k'osh imo detsfe.
De'erawwotsnat bokenih k'irts máátswotssh tietetuwo hank'oyiye, bode'erawo tikok'o wotarr bobeyink'ere sheenge.
Ernmó meetsi tewnon mis'oniyere de'ewo b́k'antsotse botoko kordek'o bomawiyal de'ewne.
De'etsuwotsshmó t'imet tzaziyo haniye, tzaziyanwere Doonzoka bako tikaliye, dek'ets máátsu bkenihatse fakshek'ayiye.
B faksheeyalowere máátso amaniyere bíyal beewiye, wee bkenihnton maneewiye, mank'owere keniho b́máátsu fakshk'aye.
K'oshuwotsshmó doonzo b́woterawo taa ttookon t etiruwo hank'owiye, krstiyani ash iko krstiyani woteraw máátsu b́detsal err towaar beyo bgeyiyal fakshk'aye.
Krstiyani wotts máátsu krstiyani woteraw kenihodetsfawotiyal binton towaar beyo b́geyiyal keshk'ayiye.
Krstiyani woteraw keniho krstiyan wotts b́máátsu atse tuutson Ik'i jir wotituwe, krstiyani woteraw máátsunwere krtiyani wotts kenihoatse tuutson Ik'i jir wotituwane, mank'o wotob́k'azink'ere it nana'úwots Ik'i ashuwotsi wotofalrawnk'nee, mank'oon it beyalmó it nana'úwots Ik'i ashuwotsiye.
Krstiyani woterawo fakshewo b́geyiyal fakshewe, mank'onmó krstiyaniwo mantstso kenih wotowa máátso eegi naari keewon detseratse. Ik'o noon b́s'eeg jeenon nobetuwok'owe.
Nee krstiyani máátsune, krstiyani woterawo nkenihi daneraka nworitka wotiyal eege ndani? Neewere krstiyani nungushono, krstiyani woteraw nmáátsu nworitka wotiyal eege ndani?
Ik iko Doonzo b́ imts imok'onat b́ s'eegeori b́teshtsok'on beewe, Ik'i moowwotssh ti imtso bín bojisheetuwo haniye.
Asho konuwor wotowa gofo bíamiyak s'eegeka wotiyal gofo amawok'o wotosh gawuk'aye, gofo bíamawo s'eegeka wotiyalo gofamo geek'aye.
Gof amonu gof amk'azonuwere k'awuntso deshatse, Ik'o tzaziyo korde'er finats jitsoniye k'awtsetsoni.
Mansh asho ik ikon Ik'o bín b́ s'eegor b́teshtsok'on beewe.
Ik'o neen b́ s'eegor guutse nteshi? Nwotiyalor eegor woteratse, mansh kic'k'aye, nas' keshi goo ndatsitka wotiyal goo man neesh beshk'aye.
Guuts wotat b́befere Doonzon s'eegets asho Doonzon nas' keshke, mank'owere nas'o wotat b́befere s'eegets asho Krstossh guutse.
Ik'o k'awuntson iti b́kewutsotse ashuwots guutso wotk'ayere.
Mansh tíeeshwotso asho ik ikon b́ seegeyori b́teshtsok'on Ik'onton mank'oon beewe.
De'eraw ashuwots jangosh Doonzoke tdek'ts tzaziyo deshatse, ernmó doonzo mhretyon amanek twottsotse ttook asaabiyo hanats dabr tt'intsitwoniye.
And nobeyiru gizeyo kic'its gize b́wottsotse de'eraniye bíyal beyo sheeng arefee taasha,
B́woteferowere máátso dek'ri wotiyal faksho geek'aye, máátso de'atsne wotiyal dek'osh geek'aye.
Ernmó nee máátso ndek'al niats morro wotituwe etaliye, mank'owere baarna'a iku máátso bíamal morro bi ats wotituwe etaliye, wotowa ére de'eyiru ashuwotsi datsanatsi beyi kic'o ayide boon daatsituwe, ttewunonuwere kic'anitse itkashitwok'owe.
Ti eshuwotso! taa itsh tietirwo hank'oyiye, dúronúwo k'awnwtsere, haniyak eshe mááts detstswots mááts deshawok'o wotaarr beewne. Mááts detstswots deshawok'o wotarr beewne.
Shiyanirwonwere shiyaanerawwotsk'o, geneeúwirwots geneeúwerawwotskok'o wotde'er beewunee, k'ac' keewirwots, k'ac' iko deshawwotsk'ok'o woshde'er boatso taawunee.
Datsanatsi gaalon kis' keshiru jamwots bín kis' keyawok'o wotde'er beewunee, andi be'eyiru datsan beshitke.
Mansh konnari hasabiyon it kic'eraawon it beyo shunfee, mááts de'awu asho doonzo b́geneeúshit keewo b́geyiruwotse bíasabiyo b́ t'iwintsit doonzosh s'iilit finatse.
Mááts dek'ts asho bíasabiruwo datsan keewonat b́máátsú bín b́geneeúshit keewe.
Manatse tuutson bíasabiyo gitok kaywutsere etee. Mank'o mááts amaaw máátsu wee baarnaú bmeetsonat bshayiron S'ayinr doonzok woto bgeyituwotse bi asaabiyo b́t'iwintsit doonzo s'ilits finatse, mááts amts máátsunmó bkenihi máác'o k'eezosh bgeyiruwotse bgawir datsatsi keewe.
Taa han itsh tietiru kamboots kindr it kic'ituwok'owa etaatniyaliye itsh b́ sheengetuwok'owa etaatniye, t tewunonuwere it niwon beyarr it asaabiyo b́ bad'erawo nibi s'eenon doonzosh itfinituwok'owe.
Ik asho b́ wid'tsu dek' k'azosh b́ k'ut'iyakon mank'o b́ k'alo na'a mansh sheeng wot b́ k'azok'o bísh b́shiyeyal, maniyere okoon bin dek'o b́ geyiyal, b́ deek'onu ar bísh bíariyal b́ tewuntsok'on b́ dek'al morro woteratse, eshe dee'ewune.
Ernmó ik asho b́ nibo b́ kúp'iyal, b́ dek'etuwok'o bín woshit keewo aali wotiyal, b́ tewuno kordeketuwe wotiyal, b́ wid'tsu dek' k'azosh b́ k'ut'iyal sheenge b́ k'ali.
Eshe mááts dek'etuwo sheenge b́k'ali, mááts de'awonmó bogshdek't sheenge b́ k'ali.
Máátsu b kenihi kashon b́ befetsosh de'eyi nemon tipekiye, b kenihi b́ k'iriyalomó b shúntsosh amoosh falfane, bi amet asho amants woto geyife.
T s'ilok'onomó máátso amaniyere biyal b beyink'e k'anefe, geene'arniye b beeti, taa Ik' shayiro t detstsok'o arefee.
Woteraw ik'osh shukeets meetsi janga wotiyalo arikee «No jametswor dano detsfone» b́woteferor dano ashe bogtane etee b́dofoni, shunonmó age bíagfoni.
«Dano detsfe» ett gawiru asho fa'ewotiyal bísh dan geyiitowok'o andoor danafa'ee.
Ik' shunts ashonmó Ik'oke daneke b́wotiti.
Mansh woteraw ik'osh shukeets meetso meyi jango b́wotiyalo, woteraw Ik'o kasho deshaw b́wottsosh Ik' ikoniyere okoniye k'osho Izar Izewer bíaalok'owo danfone.
Dab Izar Izeweri b́woterawo Izar izewerotsi ett s'eegeyirwots ayuwots Izar izewerotsnat ay doonzuwots daronat datsatse fa'ane eteyalor,
Noko Izar Izewermó jam keewo aztsonat noowere bíko no wottsuwots Ik'o niho b́s'uziye, mank'owere jamkeewo bín azetsonat noowere bín nobeyirwo Doonz iko Iyesus Krstos s'uziye.
Ernmó han dan jametswotsiyaliye, ik ikuwots han b́borfetsosh woteraw Ik'o ik'iyo bo doyo wosh bodek'tsotse meestso bomeyir woteraw ik'osh shuketsok'o woshdek'tniye, mansh bo asaabiyo maawk b́wottsosh bokiimiri.
B́wotiyalor Ik'ok noon t'intsituwo mooniyaliye, moonok'azalor noosh shapit keewo aaliye, nomaalor noosh oot'et keew aaliye.
Wotowa ére nas' it keshtsan imnetiyon kup'eraw ashuwotssh t'ug b́ woterawok'o it atso korde'ere.
«Dano detsfe» err woshosh shúketso wosh shukeyiruwoke nmaafere b́ imnetiyon kúp'eraw asho neen b́ bek'al n fintsan ashman woshosh shuketso b́ meetuwok'o bíango n kúp'iri etosha?
Eshe nee «Dank taane» err Krstos bísh b́ k'irtsonat b́ imnetiyon kúp'eraw krstyaniyo t'afituwe etee.
Hank'on amants it eshuwotsi dadar bo nib maawtso gaawiyon Krstosi it dadiri.
Eshe misho t eshu amantsosh t'ug b́ wotitka wotiyal t eshush t'ug wot k'azosh b́ jamon meetso maaratse.
Taa nas' keshk taanosha? Taa wosheets taanalneya? Taa doonzo Iyesusi be'atsta? Itwere doonzon t fini oot' itnalneya?
Doonzon wosheets t wottsok'o kitsit mahatabo it itwottsotse k'oshuwotssh dab wosheets woto tk'azal itshere arikon wosh na'a taane.
«Wosheets woti mebtiyo deshatsne» err keewituwotssh ti aanitwo haniye,
No mishonat úshon daatsi mebtiyo deshatsnowa?
K'osh wosheetskok'o doonzon eshúwotsk'o P'et'rosotsk'o krstiyani máátsu de'e gúrosh mebtiyo deshatsnowa?
Wee finar beyo b́ geyit taanat Barnabas s'uzsheya?
Demozalo b́ took gizon kes'fo kone? Woyiniyo tohr b́ shuwo maarawo kone? Gizi s'eeno jinr bíezo úyawo kone?
Han t keewir ash asaabiyok'oneya? Nemonu hank'o eratsa?
«Mááy sirbiru minz beero b́ noono tipk'aye» ett nemotse guut'ere, eshe Ik'o hank'o bíet minz beruwotssh shiyanatneya?
Ik'o han bíet noosh shiyanatniyosha? Gosh goshiruwo jángát b́ goshiruwok'o, mááy bútsirwo jángát b́ bútsiruwotse, hank'on jamo b́ bano b́ daatsituwok'o, han arikon b́ guut'e no jangoshe.
Noo shayiri keewo itsh no shookori wotiyal it meets deero itoke no k'es'al een keeweya b́ wotiti?
K'oshwots keewan itoke daatso boosh geyife wotiyal eshe no haniyere bogo daatso aawuk'oneya noosh geyiyo b́ k'azeti? Nooyere mebtiyann t'ak'ameratsone, no Krstosko doo shishiyosh t'ug b́woterawok'o jam keewo k'ama nok'amri bako mebtiyan t'ak'ameratsone.
Ik' mootse finiruwots bo misho Ik' mootsne bodatsituwok'o wosh t'inetseyiru t'arap'ezoke finirwitsu wosh manatse kayide'er bometwok'o danatsteya?
Mank'o doo shishiyo daniruwotsu bometuwo fin manatse bo daatsituwok'o Ik'o azazere.
Taamó mebtiyanotsitsere ikunoru t'ak'ameratse, hanowre t guut' t mebtiyan eegishe taash koteyo b́ k'azi? Etaatniyaliye, asho bín t ít'iruwo datsmec'ron b́ oriyoniyere k'iro taash k'anefe.
Doo shishiyo daniyo taash geyik b́ wottsotse t it'et keewo aaliye dab doo shishiyan daniyo tk'azal indowe taana!
Doo shishi keew angnon b́ woterawo t shunon tdaniruwosh k'awutso detsfe, angnona t finiri wotiyalomó taash imetsmani ti fini bako k'osh tk'alts keewo fa'ee etaliye.
Eshe t maawirwosh t k'awuntso eebi? T maawi k'awntso doo shishwo daniyir daats taash geyituwo t de'aawo doo shishi fino damozalo hank'on t finoniye.
Taa konshor guuts twoterawo nas' ash taane, wotowa ére t faltsok'on aywotsi kashiyir boon t'akamosha etaat jamosh guutso wotere.
Ayhudiyotston t wotor ayhudiyotsi kashiyosh ayhudiyotsk'o twoti, taa nemi shirots woto t k'azalor dab́ nemi shirotstsuwotsi kashiyosha etaat nemi shirotse beyiru ashuwotsk'o t woti.
Taa Ik' nemo detstsonat Krstos nemi shirots t wotiyaloru dab́ nem deshaw Ik' ash woterawotsi kashiyosha etaat nem deshaw ashok'o twoti.
Bo imnetiyon maawtswotsi kashiyosha etaat maawtswotskok'o maawk t woti, t faltsok'on muk'uwotsi kashiyosh jamonton jam keewo t woti.
Jaman t k'alir dooshishiko deero kayosh dooshiyosha etaatniye.
Wos'i nokorewor jametso b́wos'fook'o boyitsnowere ik s'uzo shlmatiyo b́dek'fook'o danatsteya? Mansh itwoor shlmatiyo dek'osh woc'ere.
Wos'on noheyiru jamwots maawfetsr anaanshr dano woshfne, bo mank'o bomaawir beshituwo t'afitwonat andish wotitu akliliyo daatsoshe, noomó nomaawir t'afraawonat dúre dúrik wotts akliliyo daatsoshe.
Taamó am b́ bodooko danawu ashokok'o datsmec'ro woc'atse, jongo kisho t'umde'er jot'iruwok'o datsmec'ro shóótetk taanaliye.
Mansh k'oshuwotsi nohewo maants s'eetk'riyakon taa t tookon nohemanitse úr wotaarr tdaatserawok'o tiatso korde'er taash bíazazetuwok'o woshituwe.
Tieshuwotso! Nonihots daawno bo abaatse wotdek't boon b́ jishfere b́teshok'o jametswots aatsk'ar biro bokimtsok'o itsh gawiyo geefe.
Musenton ikwotoshat daawnanat aats k'aranits bogupeyi.
Únetswotsu ik naari shayiri mishman máárne, bo únetswere Shayiri úshman úshrnee,
Únetswotswor iknaari shayiri úshe boúshi, bo úshtsonwere boon shoyidek't sha'efetst teshts shayiri s'almanitse t'úúp'ke b́tesh, s'almanuwere b́tookon Krstosiye b́teshi.
Man b́woteferor ayuwotsn Ik'o genee'úweratse, mansh bo duuno woruwots juweyat b́oori.
Bo gond keewo botewntsok'o noowere gond keewo notewunrawok'o jaman noosh ats kotiyosh ariyetso wotere.
«Ashuwots móónat úshosh beebodek'i, weeralonowere duubosh botuwi» ett bo jangosh guut'etsok'on, bo woteraw Ik'o bo ik'itsok'o it were bokok'o woteraw ik'uwotsi Ik'i k'ayere.
Boyitsere ik ikuwots widi morro bofintsok'o noowere widi morro finonowa? Bo han bok'altsotse boyitse hiye keez kum ashuwots ik aawon k'irrne.
Boyitsi ik ikuwots fadt dawunzoon shaas'eyat bok'irtsok'o noowere Krstosi fadk'ayone.
Boyitse ik ikuwots mumundat úd'iru melakiyon bot'aftsok'o itwere mumund k'ayere.
Keew jaman boats b́bod noosh no ats kotiyosh ariyeyi, guut'ewwere dúri s'uwaatse fa'úwotssh noosh dano b́wotishe.
Eshe need'iruwok'o ariru asho b́ dihrawok'o bí atso korde'e.
Ashaats bodiru fadewoniyere k'osh fadewo itats boratse, Ik'o amaneke, it angoniyere bog wotts fadewo it ats b́ bodetuwok'o eekeratse, it fadeworo bín it k'amit ango imr fademanitse it keshet weero itsh k'anitwe.
Mansh eshe shuneetswotso! woteraw ik'uwotsi ik'iyatse wokoore.
Hanowre itsh t'iwintsirwotsi itwottsotsne, hansh taa tkeewirwo it itokon aab angshuwere.
Noo Ik'o udat nokayirwo deerets úshi wanc'o Krstos s'atsonton ik woto detsfoshna? Notitsiru mishonwere Krstos meetsenton ik woto detsfoshna?
Meeyiru mishman ik b́wottsotse noowere ikánatse kayiruwotsi nowottsotse aywotsi nowotiyalor ik ats noone.
Aab Israe'el ashaashwots bok'altso s'iilere, tiiniru wosho meyiruwots wosht'intseyiru t'arap'ezonton ikwoto deshatsnowa boteshi?
Eshe hank'o t etor woshosh t'intsets meetso wotk keewa eteya tieti? Himó woteraw Ik'o wotk keewa etya tieti?
Mank'owiyaliye! Ik' ash woterawwots wosho bot'ntsir Ik'osh b́ woterawo fo'erawwotsshe, eshe it fo'erawwotsnton ik woto itdetsetuwok'o geeratse,
Doonzo úshi wanc'o úyifetsr aani fo'erawwots úshi wanc'o úsho falatste, doonzo mishi marats kayefetsr fo'erawwots mishi maratse kayiruwotsi woto falatste,
Eshe hank'o k'alr doonzo okoriwonowa? No bíyere bogo kúp'efnwa?
Jam keewo baziyekaliye, ernmó jam keewo t'ak'amitkaliye, jam keewo baziyekaliye, ernmó jam keewo agetkaliye.
Asho ik ikon k'oshuwotssh b́ sheengetwok'owa bako b́ took t'k'miyo geek'aye.
It nibots tuwiru amank'azo okjuk'rar gawuyatse kemeyiru meetso eega eega iterawon moore.
«Datsunat biitse fa'a jamo Doonzoke.»
Krstiyani woteraw asho iti móósh b́s'eegal móósh iti b́s'eegtsmanok itametka wotiyal itsh t'inetu mish jamo it tookotse tuwit amank'azjamo okjuk'rar eega eega iterawon moore.
Ernmó ash iko «Meetsan woteraw ik'osh shukeeke» bíetal ash man han b́ keewtsonat nibo b́dantsotse meetsman maak'ayere.
Niba ti etorowere asho niboni eta bako it niboniyaliye tietiriye. Bére s'ayin twoto k'osh ash nibats bíangshiir eegoshe?
Taa Ik'o údefetśr tmáal Ik'o bín túdiru keewatse tuutson eegoshe taan k'ooreti?
Eshe it moor wotowa it úshor wotowa jamkeewo it k'alor jamkeewo Ik' mangosh k'alwere.
Ayhudiwotsi wotowá, Ik' ash woterawwotsi wotowá, Ik'i moonor b́wotiyal, kon shoor t'ug wotk'ayere.
Taa jametsuwots bokashituwok'o jametswotssh b́shengisha bako ttookosh b́sheengetuwok'o tgeerawotse, ash jamo tk'aliru k'alon tgene'úshiruwok'o itwoor mank'o k'aluwere.
Taa Krstosi tiartsok'o itwere taan arore.
Jam aawo taan it gawirwonat itsh t imts dano kúp'idek'at dets itdek'tsotse, itn údiruwe.
Ernmó nungush jami tooko Krstosi, mááts tooko nungusho, Krstos tokonwere Ik'o niho b́wottsok'o it danetwok'o shunfee.
Tooko p'urdek't Ik' k'oniruwo wee bek'i aap'o keewiru nungush jamo b́ tookoniye b́ketiyiri.
Mank'owere btooko p'ur bde'awon Ik' k'oniru wee bek'i aap'o keewiru máátsu b tookoniye bketiri, btooko p'ureraw máátsu bs'ageetsok'owe b́taaweti.
Máátsu b tooko p'ureratsane wotiyal b took s'iiro k'ut'ewiye, ernmó btook s'iiro k'ut'ewo wee s'ageyo bin ketit keewa wotiyal b tooko p'urowiye.
Nungusho Ik'o ariyetsonat Ik' mango bín b́ be'etk b́ wottsotse b́ tooko p'uro geyiratse, máátsunmó nungushi mangiye.
Máátsuni nungushatse daatseyi bako nungusho máátsatse daatseratse.
Mank'were máátsu nungushosha bi azeeyi bako nungusho máátsush azeratse
Hanatse tutsonat melakiwots shinatse alishirootse b́fa'ok'o kitsitwo, p'uro b tookats gerde'iye.
Doonzoke no detsts beyon máátsu nungushalo beratsane, nungushonu máátsalo beeratse.
Máátsu nungushatse b datetsok'o nungushonu b́ shuwet máátsatsne, ernmó nungusha wotowa mááts wotowa k'osh jamkeewonu Ik'okne b́ daatseti.
Aab it tookon anghsuwere, máátsu btooko b p'urerawo Ik'o k'ono bish wotituwa?
Nungusho b́ took s'iiro b́genziyal bísh keeti mit b́ wotok'o hank'on azeyon danekosha?
Máátsunmó bish took s'iiro ime btooko bín ipbdek'etuwok'o b́wottsotse btook s'iiro bgeenziyal bish bmangee.
Han jangatse moosh geyiru asho fa'ewotiyal noon wotowa Ik'i maa k'oshuwots wotowa hank'o doyo deshatsone.
It ko'ewor it k'aliruwo gonda bako sheeng keew b́woterawotse and itsh ti imiru dananatse iti úderatse.
Jamoniyere shino ikwotdek'at it kakuwewor it dagotse k'osh k'oshewo b́beyo shishre, t shishts keewonwere badooko arik b́wottsok'o amaniruwe.
Ar keewetsuwots konotsi bowottsok'o galeyar bodanetwok'o ititse k'osh k'oshewo b́beyo jinatse.
Ikok it kakuwewor it meeyir doonzo kooc'i mishaliye.
It móór iko iko b́ korááwo bíyaailye b́meyiri, mank'oon iko b́ k'ak'efere iko mashe b́mashiri.
Eshe it meetuwoknat it úshet moo deshatsteya? Himó Ik' moone it gac'iri? Himó eegoru bo meetu deshawwotsne it jiitsiri? Eshe eege itsh tieteti? Keewansh iten údota? B́ jamon úderatse!
Doonzoke t dek'tsonat itsh tbeshits dano haniye, doonzo besheyat b́ imewots t'ú manots misho k'aúb́dek'i,
Ik'o b́ údiyakon tiitsdek't, «[nahere móóre,] han itsh wotituwo tiaatsoniye, han taan bín itgawitwo wosh de'ere» bíeti
Mank'o kooc' mishoniyre il úshi wanc'o k'aaúdek't «Úshi wanc'an t s'atson finet handr taaroniye, jam aawo han itúshor bín taan gawosh wosh de'ere» bí eti.
Mishan itmooronat úshi wanc'an it úshor jam aawo doonzo b́ wafetsosh b́ k'iro keewitute.
Konuworu asho bísh wot geyirawo doonzo tusho b́ móónat doonzo úshi wanc'an b́ úshal doonzo atsonat s'atso k'awunts bí ats wotituwe.
Eshe konworu asho tushan b́ mooniyere shinonat wanc'an b́ úshoneyere shino b́ tooko shú s'iilo bísh geyife.
Asho konworu doonzo atso eeg b́ wotok'o galde'er b́ dananiyere doonzo tusho b́ maal doonzo úshi wanc'o b́ úshal b́ tookats angshe b́ doweti.
It dagotsere ayuwots bomawutsonat boshodu ik ikuwotsu bok'iriye han jangatsne.
Noo notokats angshrone wotink'e no ats angsherawunk'ee b́teshi.
Ernmó il datsunton noats angsherawok'o and angshiru doonzo noon b́ seziri.
Eshe t eshuwotso! Doonzo kooc' mishosh it ko'eyor it ats atseyo korewere.
It ko'ewo angshosh b́ woterawok'o ititse k'ak'ts asho b́ beyal b́ meyitse moowe. Oorts keewosh taa manok twoor dabr bín jiishetwo itsh imetuwe.
Ti eshuwotso! ando S'ayin shayiro b́imet imuwotsi it dano geefe.
Ik'i ash woterawwotsi it teshor it danaw keewwotsn jisheyat noon keew falraw woteraw ik'uwots maants iti daamefok'o danfte.
Mansh Ik'i shayiron jisheyar Iyesusi c'ashetuwo konwor aaliye, mank'owere S'ayin shayiron jisheyarni bako «Iyesus doonze!» etetuwo konworu bí aalok'o itsh keewituwe.
K'osh k'osh S'ayin shayiri imuwots fa'ane, S'ayin shayironmó ike.
K'osh k'osh finuwots fa'ane, doonzonmó ike.
K'osh k'osh fini naaruwots fa'ane, ernmó jamo b́jamon finituwo ik Ik'oniye.
No ik iketsitse S'ayin shayiro be'eyat b́ fiinirye jametsi t'k'miyoshe.
S'ayin shayiro ik ashosh dani teleefi aap'o imetuwe, k'osh ashoshowere shayirman dani aap'o bí imeti,
Ik shayirman ikosh imnetiyo bí imeti, k'oshoshmó shodets kashiyit imo bí imeti,
Ikosho Ik'oke bek'on keewo, ikoshowere Shayirwotsi galde dano, ikosho k'osh naari noon keewo, k'oshoshowere imets k'osh noonon keewtso bits falo bí imeti,
Wotowa'ere jamán k'alituwo ik shayirmaniye, S'ayin shayiro b́ shunok'o ik ik ashosh k'osh k'osh imo b́ imeti.
Ash iko ayi atsi kayuwotsi detsfe, bí atsi kaywots ayi bowotefere bobeyir ik ash manatse. Hank'o Krstos ayi atsi kaywotsi detsts ik atsi kayok'owiye.
