Ayhudi nowotiyalo Grik ash nowotiyalo, guutswotsi nowotiyalo, S'ayinwotsi nowotiyalor, ik ats wotosh ik shayiri S'ayinon guuperoone, noúnetswor shayir ikanitse úshrone.
Ik atso b́fiine ay atsi kaywotsatsna bako ik atsi kayo s'uzatsnaliye!
Tufo «Taa kish woto tk'aztsotse atsi kay taanaliye!» bíetal eshe hank'o bíettsosh atsi kay b́woto oorituwa?
Waazonuwere «Taa ááw woto tk'aztsotse atsi kay taanaliye» bíetal, eshe, hank'o bíettsosh atsi kay b́woto oorituwa?
Ats iko b́ jamon ááw b́wotink'ere eegneya shisho b́faliyank'oni? Ats iko b́ jamon waaz b́ wotink'ere eegneya shink'o b́faliti?
Andmó Ik'o b́ shunok'o ik ik atsi kayo atsotse bísh wotit beyokok b́beyoko deshde'er b́datseetuwok'o woshre.
Boúnetswor ik kayo s'uzi bowotink'ere ats jamo eewkneya b́ datseeyank'oni?
Andomó ay atsi kaywots bobeyalor atso ik s'uzee.
Aawo kishosh «Nee taash geyiratsne!» etosh falratse, tookonuwere tufosh «Nee taash geyiratsne!» etosh falratse,
Dab́nuwor bítsi maawkwotsi araat be'eyiru atsi kaywots iki bogshdek't geyiknee.
Mangi muk' detstswotsi araat noosh be'eyiru atsi kayuwots iki bog mango boosh imetuwone, bek'osh jitsik araat noosh be'eyiru atsi kaywotssh iki bog mango imaat boon nokotiriye,
Bek'osh sheengiru atsi kaywotsmó jaman boosh geyiratse, Ik'onmó s'ilosh jitsitu araat be'eyiru atsi kayuwotssh bog mango bo detsetwok'o woshdek'́t atsi kayuwotsi gonkire.
Hanowere b́k'al atsi kaywots dagotse k'osh k'osheyalo bo ats atseyo bogawetuwok'owe.
Ik atsi kayo b́ kic'iyal k'osh atsi kaywotsuwere jamon bíntoniye bo kic'iti, ik atsi kayonu mango b́ daatsor k'osh atsi kaywotswere bínton ikn bo geneúwiti.
It Krstos atsi kayi itne, it ik ikon bíatsi kay itne.
Mansh Ik'o ik ik asho Ik' mootse k'osh k'osh fino bodetsetuwok'o woshre, hank'on shino woshetswotsi, gitlo nebiyatiyotsi, kezlon danirwotsi naashire. Dabtnuwere adits finituwotsi, dabt shodtso kashiyo boosh imetswotsi, ashuwotsi t'ep'o boosh imetswotsi, jiishiruwotsnat k'osh k'osh noonon keewiru ashuwotsi woshre.
Jamwots wosheetswtsneya? Jamwots nebiyatiyotsneya? Jamwots danirwotsneya? Jamwots adits finirwotsneya?
Jamwots shodts kashiyo boosh imeknowa? Jamwots handr noonon keewo falfnowa? Jamwots handr noonon keewetso biitso falfnowa?
Eshe ayidek't bogf imo daatsosh gewoore. Dab and jamoniyere bog weerindo itsh kitsuna.
Taa ashuwots noon keewon wee melakiwots handr noonon keewo falr shuno deshatse wotiyal kuhiru biri wee cicilru bilbilyo twotoniye.
Bek'on keewi imo tdetsalor aashts jamo tdanalor, danjamo tdetsalor, guro beyokere k'osh beyok beshit imnetiyi jamo t detsal shuno deshatse wotiyal taash eegor k'aatse.
T detsts jamo t'owwotssh t kayiyal, dab tiatso b́ ooriraniyere bín it'osha err, beshide'er ti imal, shuno t t'ut'al eegoru taash k'alatse.
Shuno k'ame b́ k'amefoni, shuno sheenge b́ k'alfoni, shuno okoorrake, shuno bog taana erake, shuno id'ake,
Shuno niwalo finerake, shuno b́ took jang mec'ro geerake, shuno nibo k'unake, shuno bín dadeyaloru dadman dadok'o taawakee,
Shuno ar wotts keewatsa b́ geneúiti bako kááw woterawonton geneúwerakee,
Shuno jamo falituwe, jamono amanituwe, b́ jangituwere jamoniye, jam keewon kúp'e b́wotiti.
Shuno b́ jamon dihiratse, bek'on keewo imets imo beshituwe handr noonon keew falo beshituwe, dan wotiyalowere beshituwe.
No danon wotowa bek'on no keewitwo k'atsoniye.
Ernmó s'een wottso b́woor k'atso ooritke.
Na'a t wotor na'ok'owa t keewufo, na'ok'owa t gawfo, nana'ok'owa t maramarefni, gan asho t wotoromó nana'i doy jamo k'aztk'iri.
And mestawut shuwa shuwa etir mastawit gondotse s'ilirwotskok'o noone, bíyormó shin shinaatsne nobek'eti, and tdanir k'atsoniye, bíyoromó Ik'o taan b́ dantsok'osh s'een dano detsetwe.
Eshe imnetiyo, jángo, shuno, keezanots oorar betknee, ernmó hanotsitsere bogetuwo shune.
Eshe shuno daatsosh gewoore, S'ayin shayiri imuwotsitse dab bitsnor bek'on keewo kup'arr gewoore.
Andr noonon noon keewitwo Ik'osha bako ashoshaliye b́keewiri, ááshk wotts keewo S'ayin shayiri angon b́ keewirwosh b́ keewirman danetuwo aaliye.
Bek'on keewitwonmó k'osho agosh, kup'iyonat atskup'iyosha ashuwotssh keewituwe.
Andr noon keewon keewit asho b́ took mec'roniye bíagiriye, bek'on keewirwonmó Ik' moo agetwe.
No jamets andr noon keewon it keewo shunfee b́ teshi, bogshde'er t shunetuwonmó bek'on it keewink'ere, Ik' maa ashuwotsi agosh andr noon keewon keewetso biitsetuwo bí alitka wotiyal, andr noon keewiru ashoniyere bek'on keewiru asho bogfe.
Eshe t eshuwotso! itok twoor andr noonon keewon keewufere t weyi wotink'ere eebi itsh t k'aliyank'oni? Bogo itsh t k'alitiye Ik'oke ááshtso kitson wee danon wee bek'on keewon wee dano itsh deshde'er twaale.
Turarok'onat T'imbok'o kash deshaw duubi k'ac'uwots k'osh jááwi k'ááro bo t'ut'al bo imiru duubi k'ááro awuk'o b́ wotok'o aawuk'oneya b́ daneti?
Ezbedo daneraw k'ááron b́ fugeyal, kes'osh kone k'aniti?
Mank'owere it be'ets andr noonon keewetsman it keewor it dants noon keewon keewo it k'azal it keewirwo kone danosh faliti? Jongosh keewirwok'owe it wotiti.
Datsanatsere ay naari noon keewwots fa'ane bits deshaw noon keewo aaliye.
Taash keeweyiru noon keewi biitso danatse wotiyal keewiru ash mansh ibee t wotiti, bíwere taash ibee b́ wotiti.
It S'ayin shayiri imuwotsi kup'shdek'at it geyiruwosh, bogshde'er geyo itn b́geyiyit Ik' maa ashuwots bín bokup'it imuwots boayituwok'owe.
Andr noon keewiru asho b́ keewirwo biitso b́ falituwok'o Ik'o k'onuwe.
Andr noon keewon Ik'o t k'oniyal t shayirona Ik'o tk'oniri bako t níbo shuwalke b́ wotiti.
Bére eeg t k'ale taan b́ geyiyiti? T shayiron Ik'o k'onituwe, t nibon dab Ik'o k'onituwe, t shayirono Ik'osh dúbetuwe, t nibon Ik'osh dúbetuwe
Hank'o woto b́ k'azal nee shayiron Ik'o n údor, nee ni etiruwo danawu asho n údonat ni Ik' k'onosh «Amen» eto aawuk'oneya b́ faliti?
Arikon nee nt'iintstso údon Ik'o k'ono sheengetskee, ernmó ash k'osho bín kup'eratse.
Taa it úneetsiyere bogo handr noonon keewirwo twottsosh Ik'o údirwe.
Ernmó k'oshuwotsi daniyosha err Ik' mootse tats kum aap'uwotsi handr noonon keewoniye úts aap'uwotsi ttookon keewo shunfee.
T eshuwwotso! gond keewosh nana'i marmat'ok'o wotoore bako it asaabiyon nan'i marmat'uwotskok'o wotk'ayere, maniyere it asaabiyon katstswotsi wotoore.
Manuwere, «Handr noonon keewiru ashuwotsnat Bo noon keew keewo daneraw ashuwots noonon ash ashaanotssh keewitwe, Mank'o b́wotiyalor taan k'ewatsne etfe Doonzo Ik'oni» ett nemoots guut'ere.
Hansh andr noon keew keewon keewo milikit b́wotit amaneraw ashuwotssh bako amaniru ashuwotsshaliye, bek'on keewets keewo keewonmó milikit b́wotit amaniru ashuwotssha bako amaneraw ashuwotsshaliye.
Krstiyaniwots bokakuwewor Ik' maa ashuwots andr noon keew keewon b́ keewor danawwots wee amaneraw ashuwots bowaal keewirwotssh «Ashaanots geeniya bowutsi» etaalknowa?
Ernmó ik iko bek'on bo keewiyal amanerawo wee danaw asho b́waal b́shishts keew jamon bísh shiyeetuwe, wee jamon bíyats angshituwe.
B́ nibots ááshts keewo keer be'etuwe, b́ baronowere gup' gup'dek't «Arikon Ik'o itdagootse!» eton Ik'osh b́sagaditi.
Eshuwwotso! eshe eeg k'alo geyifa? Ik' k'onosh it kakuwewor ititse iko Ik'osh duubo detsfe, k'oshonu daniyo detsfe, k'oshonu ááshts keewo kish kitso detsfe, iko ando andr noonon keewo detsfe, ikonu keewetsman biitso detsfe. Eshe, jaman krstiyaniwotsi agetk woto bíngeyife.
Andr noon keewwotsi keewirwots bobeyal git bor wee bí ayiyal keez wotde'er keewne, bo bokeewirwono k'osh asho biishe.
Keewetsman biitsiru asho bíaalitka wotiyalmó andr noonon keewirwo kakweetsmanotsitse s'k eree, b́tookonat Ik'osh keewwe.
Bek'on keewitu gito wee keez wotar keewitunee, k'oshuwotsmó keewetsman k'ewude t'iwintsde s'iilne.
Ko'eyat beyirwotsitse k'osh asho ik jago b́ bek'al, shini keewiru man s'k err beewe.
Ik ikuwots bo danetuwok'onat bo kup'ituwok'o it jamets taron Ik' wosho keewo falfte.
Nebiyiwots bek'i shayiro nebiyiyotssh keewetuwe.
Jeeni Ik'o Izar Izeweri bako fayi Ik'o Izar Izeweriyaliye. S'ayin Ik'i maa ash jamotse k'alefok'o,
máátswots Ik' maa ashuwotsitse s'k erne. Nemonmó bí etir bo boaletwok'owa bako bo alititwok'o eekeratse.
Ik ik keewo danosh bo geyiyal bo kenih keniho bo meyitse aatune, Ik' k'onosh ko'eyor máátsuwots bo keewo jiitsike.
Beree Ik' aap'o b́ waa itokneya? Himó Ik' aap'o b́ waa itok mec'ree?
«Taa nebiyi taane wee taa Shayiron imetso detsfe» eteet asho b́ beyal t guut'tsan doonzo tzaziyo b́ wotok'o dande'e.
Han danawo b́ beyal bíwere danek'aye.
Eshe t eshuwotso! bek'on keewosh kup'ar gewoore, andr noon keewono bazik'ayere.
Ernmó jam keewo niwonat matson wotowe.
Eshe ando t eshuwotso! itsh tdanits doo shishi aap'o itsh gawiwo geefe, doo shishy aap'onwere it dek'tsonat kup'dek'at bíyats it needirwoniye.
Taa itsh tdaniitso doo shishi aap'o kup'ide'er desh it dek'ink'ere bín kashiyank'te, maniyere okoonmó it amantso datsmec'roone.
Taa t dek'ts shintso jamoniyere bogo itsh beshire, itsh tbeshits keewonwere S'ayin mas'aafotse guut'etsok'on Krstos no morrosh k'irre,
duukere, S'ayin mas'aafotse guut'etsok'onowere keezl aawots k'irotse tuure etke.
Bí P'et'rossh be'ere, ilowere tatse git woshetswotssh be'ere,
Úts bal ashuwotsiyere bogts b́shuuts shoydek't sha'iruwotssh iknoto be'ere, boyitse ayuwots andish b́borfetsosh fa'ane, ik ikuwotsmó k'irrne.
Maniye hakonowere Yak'obsh be'ere, wosheets jamwotssho be'ere.
Jami s'uwaatsnowere shabetsok'o wottsosh taash ando be'ere.
Taa Ik'i moo gishtso twottsotse wosheets jamwotsitse dashonat wosheka err s'eegeyo taash geyirawo taane.
Ernmó taa and twottso wotat tdaatseyir Ik'i s'aatonee, taashowere imets s'aato shuwalon ooreratse, dabnuwor k'oshuwotsiyere bogo finon mawure, erenmó han k'alirwo taanton fa'a Ik'i s'aatoni bako taanaliye.
Eshe taan wotowa boon wotowa nodaniyrwo haniye, itwere itamantso haniye.
Krstos k'irotse b́ tuutsk'owa no daniyiri wotiyalmó ititsere ik ikuwots aawk'oneya k'irots tuwo aaliye boetiri?
K'irotse tuwo aali wotiyal Krstos k'irotse tuuratse etee,
Krstos k'irotse tuuratse wotiyal no daniruwoni wotowa it imnetiyo k'awuntso deshatse etee,
Ik'o Krstosi k'irotse tizre etaat daniruwots kootets Ik'i gawwotsi woterone etee, eshe k'irts ashuwots k'irotse tuwatsno wotiyal Ik'o Krstosi k'irotse tuzatse etee.
K'irts ashuwots k'irotse tuwatsno wotiyal Krstos k'irotse tuwatse etee.
Krstos k'irotse tuuratse wotiyal it imnetiyo k'awuntso deshatse etee, andoru morrotsa it beyiri etee,
Krstosn amanat k'irtswots t'afrnee etee,
Krstosi nojangir datsanatsi be mec'rosha wotiyal ash jamoniyere bogo noosh shiyanetk nowotoniye.
Ernmó Krstos k'irtswotssh k'irotse tuwon k'aabo wotat arikon k'irotse tuure.
K'iro b́ waa ik asho atse tuutson b́ wottsok'o k'irotse tuwonu b́ weet ik asho atse tuutsone.
Adam atse tuutson ash jamo b́k'iriruowok'o mank'o Krstos atse tuutson ash jamo kasho daatsituwe.
Man b́wotituwere ik ikosh b́ tar tarone, Krstos k'irotse tuwooke shintsoniye, ilowere Krstos b́woor bík wottsuwots k'irotse tuwitune.
Maniyere hakowere bíalguronat alona ang jamo t'afir mengsto Ik'o Nihosh beshide b́ ímet aawo dúri s'uwoniye b́ wotiti.
Ik'o b́ balangar jamwotsi bí ali shirots b́ woshfetsosh Krstos b́ naasho geyiyituwe.
Da'eyar s'uwatse t'afitu t'elato k'ironiye.
«Ik'o jam keewo bí ali shirots woshk'rere» ettso guut'ere, maniye daneke, ernmó «Jam keewo bí ali shirots wotere» bíetor jam keewo bí ali shirots woshts Ik'o nihono dabaatse
Jam keewo Krstos ali shirots b́ wotiyakon Ik'o niho jámo b́jámon b́ wotituwok'o naayo b́ tookon jám keewo bí ali shirots woshtso Ik'o niho shirots wotitwe.
Eshe k'irts ashuwots tuwatsno wotiyal k'irts ashuwots jangosh guupeyiru jamwots eebi bo'ot'oni? k'irts ashuwots b́ jamon k'irotse tuuratsno wotiyal ashuwots boshegro eegosha etniya bo gupeyiri?
Noo nowotiyaloru aaw aawon t'up' er tawootse nobeyir eegoshe?
T eshuwotso! taa aaw aawuon k'iro taan b́ datsiri, hanowere t keewir doonzo Iyesus Krstos jangosh itatse t detsts it'o arik b́wottsotsne.
Ash asaabiyok'on taa Efesonn dini s'ootswotsnton t kaare eeg orshoshe? K'irtswots k'irotse tuuratsno wotiyal «Yaats nok'iritwotse woore moone, úyone» eteetsok'oyiye.
Dáshek'ayere, «Woteraw tooho sheeng doyoniye bí awashifoni.»
It nibo maants aanoore, morro fink'ayere, ititsere ik ikuwots Ik' danawwots fa'ane. Hano ti etiri it jitsitwok'wa etaatniye.
Asho iko «K'irts ashuwots aawk'oneya botuwit? k'irotse bo tuwor bodetset atso awuk'one?» err aato falitwe,
Nee dogono n shokiru mááyo b́ k'irrawo boc'r beyo falatse,
Nee n shokor Geshi shooko wee k'osh mááyi shooko s'uzi n shooketi bako ili bos'et miti gindoniyaliye.
Ik'onmó shook mansh b́ shuntsok'o miti gindo b́ imeti, ik ik shookosh k'osh k'osh miti gindo b́ imeti.
Meets jamo ik naaraliye, ash meetso ik naare, gizi meetso k'osh naare, Kafuwots meetso k'osh naare, Mus' meets k'osh naare.
Mank'o daritsi atso fa'ee, datsatsi atsonu fa'ee, ernmó daratsi atsi mango ik naare, datsatsi atsi mangonu k'osh naare.
Aawi mango ik naare, Ashitsi mangonuwere k'osh naare, K'enuwots mangonu k'osh naare, ik k'eeno k'osh k'eenoniyere k'osh mango detsfe.
K'irotse tuwit ashuwots jango haniye bíari, t'afitu k'irts atso wotat shooketso k'irawu beetk atso wotar tuwituwe.
Ketoon shooketso mangon tuwitwe, maawon shooketso kúp'on tuwituwe,
Meetsi ats wotat shooketso shayiri atso wotar tuwituwe. Meetsi atso b́ beyok' shayiri atsonuwere fa'ee.
Mansh, «Shints asho Adam kashets azeetso b́ woti» ett guut'ere, iltso Adam Krstosmó kash imet shayiro b́ woti.
Ernmó shintso b́ waa meetsone bako shayironaliye, shayiron wottso b́waa meetson wottsoniyere ile.
Shints asho Adam bí azee shawatse b́ wottsosh datsatsike, gitl ashonmó b́waa daratsnee.
Datsats wottswots datsatse azeets ashok'one, daaratse wottsuwots daaratse waats ashok'one.
Datsatsi asho aro noartsok'o daratsi asho aronowere aritwone.
Eshuwotso! itsh tkeewirwo haniye, meetsonat s'atson Ik'i mengsto naaratse, mank'owere k'irr t'afit atso t'afrawu kashets atso naaratse.
Eshe! mist'iri iko itsh keewirwe. Noo noúnetswor k'irratsone. Ernmó no únets wonetuwone.
Nowoneetwonwere s'uwatse ezbedo fugewor ááwi k'iluowok'o iknotone. Ezbedo fugetuwe, k'irts ashuwotswere t'afraw kashetswotsi wotar tuwitune, noowere wonetuwone,
T'afituhan t'afrawo k'irituhanwere k'irrawo tahdek'o bísh geyituwe.
T'afituwaan t'afrawo k'iritwanwere k'irrawo tah b́dek'or «K'iro da'ewon k'oot'ewtsere!» ett guut'etso s'eenetwe.
Mank'owere, «K'irono! bín nkoshetuwo aawoke b́fa'oni? K'irono! ash bín n t'afit ango ewuke?» etetuwe.
K'iro bín b́koshet ango morre, morri angonuwere neme.
Ernmó nodoonz Iyesus Krstos weeron da'o noosh imetuwosh Ik'osh údo wotowe!
Eshe mansha shuneets eshuwotso! kup'ar need'ore, ik keewonor shek'ek'ayere, doonzo finosh it shaatso datsmec'r b́woterawok'o dande'er, it eed'irawo jam aawo doonzo fino finosh kup'ore.
Amantsuwotssh giz kishi jango Gelatitsi Ik' moosh t imts bín bojisheeyirwok'on it were mank'o k'alwere.
Taa twoor giz kisherawok'o ik ik gawiyotsi sanbat eenots ititsi ik iko b́datsiruwok'on kishde'er beezwe.
Taa itok twoor, amoosh falitúne it etts ashuwots it kishts gizo de'er Iyerusalem maants boametuwok'o bín bodeenet dabdabeyonton boon woshituwe.
Taa tiamo b́ geyitka wotiyalo, taanton ametúne.
Mek'odoniiweeron amoosh t etirwotse manweeron t beshoor iki it weeron weetwe.
Tiametu jamok tweerosh taash wotit tep'o taash it woshituwok'o daneraka itok teshetwe, daneraka jooshonor itnton beshiyosh falituwe,
And tbeshor iki b́weeron itn s'iilo geeratse, doonzontoh b́wotiyal múk'i geenzts gizeyosh itnton teshosh geyirwe.
Ernmó P'ent'ek'ost'eyi bali aawo b́borfetsosh Efesonitse teshetwe.
Ayi eenonat shuu detsts fin fengesho taash k'eshewutsere, k'efirwotsu aynee.
T'imotiwos itok b́woor shatalon itnton b́beetuwok'o bín tewu'ere, bíwere tikok'o doonzo fino finiruwe.
Mansh konwor bín b́gac'eraawok'owa, bí eshwwotsnton t maants b́weetuwok'o tkotirwotse tiyok jeenon aanar b́weetwok'o b́weerosh bín geyitwon bín tewu'ere.
No eshu Ap'los k'osh eshwwotsnton it b́ s'iiletwok'o kup'shdek'at k'onre b́teshi, bímó and it maants wosh eekeratse, bísh b́k'anoor weetwe.
Maaw k'ayere, it amantsok'on kup'arr need'ore, kup'ore, aawo shuu'ere.
It k'aliru jamo shunon k'aluwere.
Ti eshwotso! Ist'ifanos maa ashuwots Akayiy datsatse amants shintswotsi bowottsok'onat amantsuwotssh finoshowere botoko beshidek't boimtsok'owo danfte.
Hanotsk'o ashuwotsnat bontonwere finon maawiru jamwotssh it aletwok'o kup'idek'at it baterawok'o gawirwe.
Ist'ifanosna, Ferdonat's Akayik'oswere t maants bo waatsotse gene'owere, it tiyoke daatsewo itk'aztsotse bo it shegro taash shaptso s'eentsrne.
Bo t shayironat it shayiron kashirne, mansh hanotsk'o ashuwotsi dande'ere.
Isiyon fa'a Ik'i moowwots jamo itsh t'intsirune, Ak'ilnat K'irisp'iln, bomootse kakuweyiru krstiyani jamwotswere bo nibon jamo doonzo shúútson itsh t'intsirúne.
Hanoke fa'a krstiyani jamwots jamo itsh t'intsirune, S'ayints joobewon jamó it atsatsewosh aatewere.
Taa P'awlos jamáán t kishon itsh guut're.
Doonzo shunawo b́beyal c'ashek wotowe! No doonzo wowe!
No doonz Iyesus s'aato itnton wotowe.
T shuno Iyesus Krstosn it únetsnton wotowe.
Ik' ettsok'on Iyesus Krstossh wosheets wottso P'awlosnat no eshuu T'imotiyosoke. K'orontos kitotse fa'a Ik' moonat Akayiyin fa'a Krstiyani wotts ash jamwotssh.
No nihi Ik'oke, no doonz Iyesus Krstosoknowere s'aatonat jeenon itsh wotowe.
Maarts nihonat kup' jam imet Izar Izewer, no doonz Iyesus Krstos nihi Ik'osh údo wotowe,
Noo Ik'oke nodatsiru kúp'iyon gond bek'otse beyiru jamwotsi kúp'sho no falituwok'o Ik'o noon no gond bek' jamotse kúp'shitwe.
Krstos gond bek'o ayidek'at no kayidek'tsok'on hank'o Krstosn kúp'eyo ayide'er datsituwone.
Noo gondo nobek'or it kúp'eyonat kashon daatsitute, no nokúp'iri itwere itkup'twok'owe. Kup'han b́datsewe no ats bodets gond bek'i naari k'amoon it itned'tsoshe.
Noo gond bek'o it kayok'o mank'o no kúp'ono it kayituwok'o no dantsosh itatsere nodetsts jángo kúp'e.
T eshuwotso! Isiyi datskayotse no beyor no'ats bodts gond bek'o it danetuwok'o geefone, no'ats bodts gond bek'onuwere kurosh nofalitwoniyere bogo no'ats dihit b́ teshtsotse kashon beyosh nojangtso dab k'ut'dek're b́ teshi.
Mank'o k'iro no'ats angshetsok'owe noosh shiyeyat b́ teshi, jaman no'ats b́ boduwere no amaniruwo k'irts tizitu Ik'ona bako no took angon b́ woterawok'o nibn no dek'ishe.
Mansha bí noon hank'o een k'irosh betsit t'úp'er tawatse kashire, kashitwe, dabnwere b́ kashitwok'o bíne nojágiti.
It noosh Ik' k'onon it tep'o geyituwe, ayi ashuwots Ik' k'onatse tuutson noosh imets Ik' s'aatosh aywots udo t'intsitune.
No it'et keewo haniye, hanwere ar b́ wotok'o no nibo gawitwe, k'osh ashuwotsnat bítsnooru itnton nobeets beyo Ik'oke nodek'ts S'ayinonat kááwatse tuutsone, han b́ wotuwere Ik' s'aatone b́ teshi bako ash dani telefonaliye.
Nababar t'iwintso it falit keewoniyere okoon k'osho eegoru guud'atsone,
no jangosh k'atso it dantsok'o mank'o s'eenon it danetwok'o amanitwe, manshowere doonzo Iyesus b́ weet aawor no itn noit'etuwok'o itwere noon it'etuute.
Keewann arik twottsosh gitoto it t'ak'ametuwok'owa etaat shin shino iti s'ilosh geeyatniye tteshi,
Itn s'ilosh tietwere Mk'odoniy datso maants it weeron t beshoronat bíyokere aanar twore b́ teshi, hank'onowere Yhud datso maantsan t sha'or taan it tep'etuwk'o gawatniye t teshi.
Hanowere t gawor t k'aliru danaw hake baka etirwok'o arefta itsha? Han t gawirwo iknon «ee, etonat iya'a» etaat ash gawirwok'o hake baka eton t k'altsok'o arefta itsha?
Ik'o amanek b́ wottsotse no nokeewirwo, «ee wee iya'a» etiru hake baka eton keeweyiru aap'ok'oyiyaliye.
Taanat Silasn T'imotiyosu itsh nonabtso Ik' na'o Iyesus K'rstosi «ee wee iya'a» etonaliye b́teshi, ernmó ee eto bín wotere.
Ik'o noosh b́ jangits jamo, «ee» etiruwo Krstosne, mansh Ik' mangosh Krstosn «Amen» no etiri.
Noo itnton Krstosats no kúp'ituwok'o woshtso Ik'oniye, noon galdek' futtso bíne,
Bík nowotok'o kitsit mahatabon no'ats gedtsona shino maants noosh b́ imet gaalosh no níbots S'ayin shayiro agitok'o woshdek't imtso bíne.
Taa K'orontos maants aanat woo t k'azitsi jango itn tshiyanirawok'o itsh maac'o keewatniye, hansh Ik'o gawosh s'eegetwe,
It it imnetiyon kúp' it wottsotse it itgeneúitwok'o itnton finituwone boko it imnetiyon iti azazeratsone.
Eshe iti tshiyanirawok'o gawat iti s'iilo it maants ando aanar twarawok'o k'ut'dek'niye tteshi.
Dab iti tshiyaaniyalor ityere t shiyanitswotsiyere oko taan geneeúshituwo kone?
Mank'o itsh t guut'uwere itok twoor taan geneúsho boon geyit ashuwots taan boshiyanirawok'o geeyatniye, t geneúwo it únets geneúwo b́wottsok'o amanirwe.
Shiyani eenonat nibi kic'on, ay aac'uwonowere wotdek'at itsh tguut' ayidek'at iti tshuntsok'o itdanetwok'owa etni bako iti shiyaaniyosha etaatniyaliye.
Ash shiyanitso konwor fa'e wotiyal b́shiyaniyi taan b́woterawo b́ naando k'ees'iyo wot k'aya bako k'osh weeron ititse ayuwotsnoor shiyaanire.
Han naari ashosh ititse ayuwots bíats boangshts fayo bísh bodfe.
Mansha ashaan weeralon shiyaanotse b́kindrawok'o dab maniyere bísh orowa err bín it kup'iyo itsh geyife.
Mank'owere bín it shuntsok'o aaniyi arikon it kiitsituwok'owo iti k'onirwe.
Wosh ekeewnowere itsh tguut' fadeyar jam keewon aletswotsi it woto danoosha etaatniye.
It bísh oorowe it eteet ashosh taawere oorowe etetuwe, bísh oorowe ti eteet naando b́beyalor taa Krstos shinatse oorowe tietet itsha erniye.
Man t k'alirwere shed'ani gond fino nodantsotse shed'ano noon b́ darirawk'owa etaatniye.
Maniyere hakon Krstos doo shishiyo daniyosh T'iro'ad maants ti amor doonzo fini fengsho taash k'eshree,
Ernmó t eshúwi Titoyi daatso t k'aztsotse t shayiro kash de'atse, mansh manoki krstiyaniwotsi jamiyat Mek'odoniyo maants ti ami.
Ernmó jam aawo Krstos da'oon noon jishirwonat sheeng sháák' detsts shituwok'o Krstossh no detsts dano jam beyok nobetsitwok'o woshtso Izar Izewersh údo wotowe!
No kashitwotssh wotowa t'afitwotssh wotowa Krstosn Ik'osh sheeng sháák'o detsts it'anok'o noone.
Ikosh k'iro maants jishit k'iri sháák' noone, k'oshosh kasho maants jishit kashi sháák' noone, beré finansh bodts wotituwo kone?
Noo Ik' aap'tso jaak k'ac' kemiru ayuwotsk'o noonaliye, ernmó Ik'oke wosheets kááw woshetswotsk'o wotar Krstosn Ik' shinatse keewituwone.
Ando aani notooko údo tuuwwonoowa? Himo ik ikuwots bok'aliruwok'o itsh wee itoke noon tep'osh guut'etso noosh geyiyifek'úna?
Ash jamo b́ dantswotsnat b́ nababirwotsn nonibots guut'ts dabdabewwots itne.
It no finon daatsets Krstos dabdabewotsi it wottsok'o daneke, woshanuwere b́ guut'e beyat beyiru Ik' shayirona bako k'elemiyonaliye, manuwere ash nibatsa bako gashets shúts tabtabats gut'ekaliye.
Hanowere no etir Krstos weeron Ik'atse nodetsts imnetiyoshe.
Ik keewonwor nowooke b́wottsok'o gawosh flratsone, manwere eegoshe nonotokon bodknoonaliye, ernmó noon bodtswotsi woshtso Ik'oniye.
Handr taarosh finirwotsi nowotitwok'o noon falitso bíne, hanuwere fidelon guut'ets nemon b́woteraniyere S'ayin shayiri tep'one, fidelon guut'ets nemo ud'itkee, S'ayin shayironmó kash imetke.
Nemo fideliyon gashdek't guut'e shúts tabtabatse b́ teshi, nemo imeyori shááno k'aawe'efe bíamiri wotiyaloru Israe'el ashuwots Muse shiitso t'iwints de s'iilo falatsno boteshi, eshe k'ir dowet nemo hank'o mangon b́ be'eyal
bére, S'ayin Shayiri weeron daatset fino bog mango deetsalkeya?
Ashuwotsats morr doots fino hank'o mango b́ detsiyakon ashuwots bín kááw bowotit fino aawuk'oneya bog mango b́ t'ut'eti?
Ilts mango ayidek't bog b́wottsatse tuutson beshts mango eegoru b́ berawok'o tawetwe.
Ili t'afitwonworu hank'o mango b́ detsiyakon, dúre dúrosh kúp'ar beet keewonmó aawuk'oneya bog mango b t'ut'eti!
Hank'o jangetso nodetstsosh ááwu shúk'on keewitwone.
Muse múk'efere amiru b́ shiits golo b́ t'affetsosh Israe'el ashuwots bo be'awok'o b́ shiitso b́ ipefoni b́ teshi, nooyere Musek'o noonaliye.
Bo nibo arikon dúnguwtsere, andish b́ borfetso nat taari mas'aafo bo nababor bonibo manoori ipetsmann ipetsok'one b́fa'oni. Ipman ipalon b́wotit Krstos s'uzn b́ wottsotsne.
Hambetsish b́ borfetsosh nemi mas'fo nababeyi taawo bonibo ipeyirumann ipeke.
Ernmó asho doonzo maants bíaanor «Ipeyiruman k'ayb́tuwiti.»
Doonzo shayire, doonzo shiyiri beyokonowere s'ayin kesho fa'ee.
Noo noúnets iperaw shiits wotar doonzo mango mestawtotse bek'eyirwok'o bek'irwone, Shayir wottso doonzo aro aroosh mangoniyere mango maants wonetuwone.
Ik'o b́ mhretwon bísh finet finan noosh b́imtsotse maac'o k'ut'r shuuts aaneratsone.
Aashtsonat jitsik wotts keewo juuk'rerone, nemi gondon fineratsone, Ik'i aap'ono kooton woniratsone, dab iki ariko sháánatse nokitsiri, notook jangoshmo ash jami nibots Ik'i shinatse ariko keewitwone.
No danits doo shishi aap'o dab ááshka wotiyal bíáásh t'afitwotsshee.
Datsani keewiru shed'ano amaneraw ashuwots níbo deekk'rere, mannowere Ik'i aron be'eetso Krstos b́mangi dooshishiyon boosh b́sháánits shááno bobea'awok'o b́woshi.
Noo nodaniyirwo Iyesus Krstos doonz b́wotonat noowere notookon Iyesus jangosh it guuts nowottsok'oni bako notooko nabratsone.
«Shááno t'aluwotse shááne!» ett keewts Ik'o Krstos aron goliruwo Ik'i mango dani shááno noosh b́ imetwok'o b́ shááno nonibots b́ sháánetwok'o woshre.
Ernmó jamoniyere bogts angaan Ik'oka bako nok b́woterawotse mangts keewan shali k'ac'ok'o wotdek'at detsdek'rone.
B́ kaat kaaton gond bek'o noats bodiruwe, ernmó da'eratsone, ayoto daandirwonee, ernmó maac'o k'ut'ratsone.
Giishefoone, ernmó noon shuntswotsi t'ud' danaknone, togeere dihfoone erenmó k'irraknoone,
Iyesus kasho no atsotse b́be'etuwok'o Iyesus ats bodts k'iro noatsatsowere jam aawo kurdek'aatniye nogúúriri.
Iyesus kasho noats k'irituwanitse b́be'etuwok'o no kashetswots Iyesus jangosh jam aawo beshat noimeyiri.
Mansh k'iro noyitse, kasho ityitse b́ finiri.
Wotowa eré «Taa amanere, manshe tkeewiri» ett guut'etsok'on, noowere imneti ikman shayiro nodetstsotsene no amaniri, manshowerowe keewirwone.
Doonzo Iyesusi k'irotse tiztso Izar Izewer nonowere Iyesusnton b́ tizituwok'onat itntonwere noon b́ shinats b́ t'intsituwok'o danfone.
Jaman it t'k'imiyosh wotts s'aato s'eent b́ ooyefetsosh ay ashuwotssh b́ bodtsi taawon Ik' mangosh wotit údo bí ayituwok'owe.
Mansh no maac'o k'ut'ratsone, úratsi noaro b́ t'afiyaloru gitsitsi no atso aawu aawon handr wotituwe
Keet wotts gond bek' andish nodek'irwan s'uu deshaw ayidek't een wotts dúre dúri mango noosh daatsituwe.
Noo nokotirwo be'eraw keewoni bako be'eyirwoniyaliye, be'eyirwo andkee, be'erawonmó dúre dúrikoniye.
And gofok'o wotts datsatsi nomeetso b́gahor ash kishon b́ woterawo Ik'on ageets dúre dúri beyoko darotse nodetstsok'o danfone.
Andi beshit gofanitse nobeyor kashe no k'ushiri.
Mansh no meets datsatsan b́k'alewor araats wotaarr datseratsone.
Arikon k'iritwo kashots b́k'ot'etwok'o tahdek'osha bako noatse giinbazeyo no shunaawotse noo daritsi atso han abaats dabde'er tahdek'o geefone, mansh datsatsi dunkaniyotse fa'uwots noo noats b́mangre kasho nok'as'iri.
Keewansh noon k'anitso Ik'oniye, maniyere bog keewo noosh b́ imetu jamosh agito b́ wotish b́ shayiro noosh imtso bíne.
Datsatse no atson no befetsosh doonzo'atse no woktsok'o no danaloru jam aawo bín amanetuwone.
No nobeyir amanona bako keewwotsi bek'onaliye.
No beewok wotts meetsanitsere k'aleyar doonzonton wotoshe no tewniri, mansh amanon beetuwone.
No meetsanton nowotiyal wee bíyatse no k'aleyal no k'os'ó doonzo geneúshe.
Datsatsi beyon nok'altso gond wotowa doo keewosh ik iko b́ finok'o b́ k'auntso dek'osh noúnets Krstos angshi jori shinats t'ino noosh geyife.
Doonzo shato eeg b́wottsok'o no dantsosh, ashuwotssh sheenga err bodek'etwok'o woshitwone, no eeg nowotok'o Ik'o danfee, itwere it nibotse eeg nowotok'o it danetuwok'o jangirwe.
Nibotse beyiruwon b́ woterawo be'eyiruwon it'iruwotssh aaniyo it falituwok'o noon it it'etuwok'o itsh gowo imetuwone bako aani no itsh notooko úderatsone.
Geetsuwotsi no wotiyalowere Ik'osha etaatniye nogeyi, nibetsuwotsi woterone wotiyalowere itsha etaatniye nibetsuwotsi nowoti.
Manjangosh Krstos shuno noon detsetwe. Iko jametsosh b́k'irre jametsotswotswere bok'iro dandek'roone.
Kashon fa'a jamwots boosh k'irtsonat k'irotse tuutsosh bobeetuwok'owa bako haniyak botookosha err boberawok'o Krstos jametswotsshowere k'irre.
Haniyere okoon noo asho konnor meetsi s'iil s'iilon s'iilatsone, haniyere shin Krstosnor nos'iil ash jamikok'o meetsi s'iil s'iilona wotiyal shinomaants han k'alratsone.
Mansh eshe asho konuwor wotowa Krstos jiro b́wotiyal handr azeeke, nattso beshwtseree, jamonu handr wotwtsere.
Jamhan b́wotuwere noon b́ tookonton Krstosn manitsonat maniyi fino noosh imts Ik'one.
Hanuwere Ik'o Krstosn datsatsi ashjamo b́tookonton maniree etee, bo naandonowere boats taawratse, nooshowere asho doonzonton nomaniyish bí aap'o noosh imre.
Ik'o ashuwotsi noweeron b́ s'egetwotse Krstos shegro wotat wosherone, mansh «Ik'onton manewere!» err Krstos shútson itn k'onitwone
Noo Krstosn Ik' kááw fino kayituwotsi nowotitwok'o Ik'o morr deshawo Krstosi no morrosh wosho b́wotitwok'o b́ k'ali.
Ik'onton tohaat finirwotsi nowottsotse itdek'ts s'aato datsmec'ron oorik'r k'ayere etaat itn k'oniruwe.
Ik'o, «Taash wotts aawots nkeewo k'ebre! Kashiyi aawotsowere neen tep'ree!» bí etirwotse «Eshe hambe! wotts aawo andee, kashi aawonwere andee.»
No fino k'efeerawok'o ik keewon konshor t'ugo woteratsone.
Maniyere gond bek'ona, ono bek'ono, k'ic'onowere k'amefetsr Ik'osh finirwotskok'o notooko jam weeron t'intsituwone.
Ik'osh fintsuwotsi nowoto nokitsitwere jot'ewon, tipewon, noats tuuzeyiru dimbiron, finon maawon, tokr t'ut'onat s'oomiyonee,
Mank'owere s'ayinon, danon, k'amoon, doowoton, S'ayin shayiron jisheewonat bíats daro bítse aalts shunon,
ari aap'onat Ik' angone. Bín da'osh wotowa noatse k'arbazosh kes'i kac' wotts kááw fino no k'anonat giri kishon deshdek'etwone.
Mangosh wee ketosh, k'orewosh wee údewosh k'an dek'k noone, aretswotsi nowotefere, dirshtswotsi eteyi.
Danetswotsi wotefetsat danerawwotskok'o nowoti, k'irrne etefere hamb kashetswotsi wotat nodatseyri, no jot'eyaloru úd'eratsone,
Shiyano noats b́ bodaloru jam aawo geneúituwone, tuguretswotsi wotefetsat ayuwotsi gaaletso nowoshiri, eegoru deshawwots wotefetsat, jam keewo detsfone.
It K'orotosn beyiru ashuwotso! hamb, itsh kish dek'at keewurone, no nibonowere gawintsdek'at itsh k'eshrone.
Itna itshuno noosh baziyi bako no itsh bayatsone.
Niho b́nana'úwotssh b́keewfok'o tkeewre, noo nonibo gawunon k'eshde'er nogitsotse shisheyirwo itsh kish nokitstsok'o itwere mank'o noosh k'aluwere.
Woteraw finon, amaneraw ashuwotsnton ikn s'andek'ayere, kááwonat morron awuk'o k'alrniya ikwoto bofaliti? Sháánonat t'aluwon towaar beyo aawk'oneya bofaliti?
Krstosnat Diyablosn aawuk'oneya ik woto bofaliti? Amantsonat amanerawonmó aawuk'oneya kod'ewo bofaliti?
Ik'i maa S'ayino woteraw dozets ik'uwotsnton eeg ikwote b́detsi? Ik'onwere, «T beyokonowere tiashuwots taalots woshituwe, Bontonwere beetwe, Taa boosh boko Izar Izeweri wotituwe, Bowere ti ashuwotsi wotitúne» ett b́ keewtsok'on no beyat beyiru Ik'osh S'ayin Ik' maa noone.
Manats dabt doonzo hank'o etre, «Bo dagotse galeyar keere, Kim wotts keewo t'awik'ayere, Taawere iti dek'etuwe,
Taawere itnihi wotituwe, Itwere t nungush nana'úwotsnat mááts nanaúwotsi wotitute, Etre jam faltso Izar Izeweri.»
Tmashotso! jam keewo jangit noosh imetsotse atsonat shayiron kimshit kon naari keewatse notooko s'ayitsuwone, Ik' shatoon S'ayin nowoto s'een b́ wotituwok'o woshwone.
It nibon noon de'ere, no konnoru daderatsone, konatsor gondo fineratsone, dirshon konatsno ik jago geeratsone.
Hano t etir itats angshoshaliye. Haniye shini itsh tkeewtsok'o it no nibots itne, eshe kashon wotowa k'iron jam aawo itatse k'aleratsone.
Itatse tdetsts imnetiyo eene, itatse tdetsts it'o eene, kup'wtsere, nokic' jamon ayide geneúituwe.
Mek'edoniyots nobodiyakon ay kaaton gondbek'a no atsats bodi bako kash dek'o iknotonor daatsratsone, úratse fayo gitsotsnowere shate nodetsi.
Ernmó juweetswotsi kup'shit Ik'o Izar Izewer Tito b́woon noon kup'shre.
Nokup'uwere b́ waats mec'rosh b́woterawo it bín it kup'shtso noshishtsotsne, t jangosh it detsts mirac'o, shiyanonat tjangosh it kic'irwok'o noosh b́keewre iki tgeneúwi.
Haniyere shin itsh t guut'ts wosho itn shiyaanik b́wotiyalor dab woshman tguut'tsotse goyineraatse, goyinere wotiyalowere tgoyin twoshon múk'na'a gizewosh itn tshiyanitsotsne.
Andmó gene'owere, tgene'útsonuwere eegoshe itn tshiyanitsosh b́woterawon it shiyantsatse tuutson naandrone etaat itwonetsotsne, eshe it shiyano Ik'o ettsok'o b́wottsotse no itn eegor daderatsone etee.
Ik'o ettsok'on wotts shiyano woro maants jishituwo naandre eton daatset wonewo b́daatsitwotse goyino dooratse, datsatsi shiyanonmó k'ire b́doweti.
It shiyaanan Ik' ettsok'on b́wottsok'owo awuk'o kup'de fino, awuk'o wotts aniyidek'o, awuk'o kááron fayo, awuk'o shato, awuk'o mirac'o, awuk'o okooro, awuk'o sezonowere b́dootsok'owo nibnde'er t'iwintsde s'iilere. Ando it jam keewon s'ayin it wottsok'o gawon gawirute.
Itsh t guut'alor taa itsh tguut' no jangosh itdetsts kup'ar fino Ik'o shinatse itsh shaanr b́daneetwok'owa etaatni bako morro bín dadets ashosha etaatniyaliye.
Jamanatse tuutson noo kup'erone, no nokup'tsoniyere bogo ando Tito b́daatsts geneúwon iki ayidek'at geneeúweroone, manu eegishe b́shayirosh kashdek'o itdatsitsoshe.
It atse t detsts it'onowere Titosh keewre b́teshi, itwere taan jitsiratste, jam aawo itsh arikeewono itsh keewufoone b́teshi, hanuwere it jango Titosh nokeewtso itn it'o arbwotoon be'ere.
It únetswor azazeyirwotsi itwottsotsnat shatoonat k'ewon bín itdek'tsok'owo Tito b́gawor itsh b́detsts shuno ayidek't eeno wotere.
Taawere jam weeron itn it'o tfaltsotse iki bogshdek' geneúwere.
T eshuwotso! Ik'o Mek'odonin fa'a Ik' maa moowwotssh bí imts s'aato itsh daniyo shunfone.
Bowere ay gond bek'on faderne, b́woteferoru bogen'úo ayidek't eene, ayidek't tugurtswotsi bo wotiyaloru dab een teudo woshrne.
Bo faltsok'onat bofaltsoniyere bogo bo shunon bo imtsok'o taa boosh gawitwe,
Yhud datsatse beyiru Kirstiyaniwots ash tep'i gowo boosh baziyerawok'o kup'idek't noon bok'oni.
Bowere bo k'oltso no nokotirwoniyere boge, shin shin botoko doonzosh boimi, manats dabtnu Ik' shunok'on botoko noosh imrne.
Finan shin shinon fintso Titoyi b́ wottsotse andoor bo teudi finan s'uwaats de'am b́ betsitwok'o bín k'onitwe
It imnetiyon, noon keew keewon, danon, kup'on, nooke dan itdek'ts shunon jam keewono bogfte, tewd dooyi finannowere it bogetwok'o wotowe.
Eshe, tietir azazonaliye, ernmó k'oshuwots imon kup' woto it kup' wotonton no nohir it shuno ar b́ woto shu'ar s'iilosha etaatniye.
It no doonz Iyesus Krstos s'aato danfte bí eegoru dab gaaletsk b́ wotiyaloru bí tugurets wotat it galetswotsi it wotituwok'o itsha ett tugretsk b́ woti.
Han jagosh itsh sheeng araat be'ets izo itsh imetwe, beshts dúron im mec'r b́ woterawo han k'alosh shini geetswots itne b́ teshi.
Eshe imosh it detsts shúno finats jitsit s'uwo maants b́ bodetwok'o it faltsok'on it gawts man and k'aluwere.
Imosh sheeng shun detstso b́ beyal ashman tewdi doon b́ detstso b́ imala boko bíangalon b́ímíshaliye.
Hanowere ti etir it únets taalo it wotitwok'owa bako it imon it kic'efere k'oshwots bín kash bodek'isha etaatniyaliye
It it kic'or bogizo it kic'ats b́ jinetwok'o and it gizo bok'ic'ats jinee, hank'on it dagotse manuts woto beetwe.
Hanwere, «Ayi ko'itswotssh oreratse, múk' ko'itswotsshowere shapratse» ett guut'etsok'one.
Taa itsh t shiyanirwok'o Titowere itsh b́ nibon b́ shiyanituwok'o woshts Ik'o údewe.
Tito it maants b́weet b́ took shunon tuut gene'ona bako no nok'onts mec'roshaliye.
Doo shishiy nabon Ik'maa jamooke údetso eshúwo bínton woshitwone.
Haniyere dambon eshuwan no sheeng finan doonzo mangosh nofinorat finosh nodetsts sheeng shuno nokitsor noonton amt nofiinman b́ tep'etwok'o Ik'i moowwots n marat'etsoniye.
Tewdi doon imets gizan nok'eezor noshútso b́ t'afrawok'o no atso kordek'etwone.
Noo nogeyiru keewo doonzo shinatse s'uz b́woterawo ashuwots shinatse kááw wotts keewo k'ale.
Ayoto ay weeron fadere kup'at fintso wotat daatsetso no'eshuwi Titowi bonton woshitwone, bí itatse b́detsts imnetiyo een b́wottsotse and finann iti tep'osh b́detsts kup'at fino awurtsooniyere boge.
Tito jango dano b́geyitka wotiyal itn tep'osh taanton finirwo, fini weeron ttohe, bínton tohaat weyiru k'oshwots jango b́wotiyalowere bo Ik'i moowwotsatse naashuwots, Krstos mangosh need'tswotsiye.
Mansh it shúno boosh kitswere, hank'on it shunonat itatse nodetsts it'o k'awtsalko b́ woterawok'o Ik'i maa jamwotssh kitsitute.
Yhuditse fa'a krstiyaniwotssh kisheet gizi jango itsh guut'o taan geyiratse,
«Akayiy dats ashuwots natstsoon tuut tep'osh k'andek'kne» etaat mek'edoniitsi ashuwotsoke it jangosh ti ít'ir it kup'ar it finitwok'o t dantsoshe, it kup'at itfiintsonwere k'oshwotsnoor tuuzere.
Keewanatse itatse no detsts it'o dats mec'ro wotar b́oorerawok'o eeshwanotsi woshiirwe, itwere ari taa haniyere shin ti ettsok'o k'ande'er korere.
Mek'edoni dats ashuwots taanton itok waarr itk'ande'aawo bodatsiyal itats noit'tsatse tuutson jiitsitwone, itmó ayde'erniye itjiitsiti.
Mansha imetuwone it etts tewud doon it imiruwo it k'aniyitwok'o itsh bogawitwok'owa etaat eshwaanots taayere shino itok boweetwok'o wosho b́ geyiko b́wottsok'o daatsre, mank'oon taa twoor tewudi dowon it imetuwo k'anke b́wotiti, itwere it imet angnon b́woterawo shunon b́wottsok'owoniye b́kitsiti.
«Múk'shde shooketwo muk'e b́kakuwiti, ay shooktso aye b́ ko'iyiti» ett keewetso gawde'ere.
Eshe Ik'o b́shunfo geneúwon imet asho b́wottsotse asho ik ikon b́nibotse imosh b́geetso shunr ima bako shiyaanefetsr wee b́maac'otse aalo imk'aye.
Jam aawo jamkeewon it tooko falr shengfiinats jinosh itfalitwok'o ayide b́ deero itsh imo falfe.
«Hanwere t'owwotssh tewdi dowon imre, B́ kááw finonwere dúre dúrosh beetuwe» et t guut'etsok'one.
Shooko shooktsosh, moowosh misho imirwo Izar Izewer it shooket shooko ayde'er imetwe, it kááwi shuwonowere itsh ayituwe.
It tewdi doo noweeron boosh b́bodiru ash jamwots Ik'o bo úditwok'o jam aawo it imetwok'o Ik'o jam keewon iti deritwe.
It kaliru tewdi finan krstiyaniyots kic'otse kishoniyere bogo ashuwots Ik'osh ay udo bot'intsitwok'o woshitwe.
It tewdi dowi finann Krstos doo shishiyo dek'at bísh azazetswotsi itwottsok'onat, bonat k'oshwotsnsh tewdi doo kitsosh b́ wottsotse jametswots Ik'o úditúne.
It atse fa'a s'eent kud'ts Ik'i s'aatatse tuutson itjangosh Ik'o k'onfetsr itn gawitune.
Ash noon keewon keewosh falerawo bí imtsosh Ik'o údeek wotowe.
Taa P'awlos it shinats twotor ááwu nefe eteyiri, itokere tworomó ááwu shúk'e eteyiri, Krstos doowootonat maac'nefon iti k'onirwe,
Meets ettsok'on no sha'irwok'o woshdek't taawiru ik ik ashuwots shinatse ááw shuuk'on keewo t geeyiyaloru itok twoor ááw shuk'on t keewitwok'o k'alk'ayere.
Dab datsanatse no beyaloru nokaarit datsatsi kaaraliye.
No kes' k'ac'onwere ááshet gop'o gaak faliyit Ik' ang detstswoni bako datsanatsi kes' k'ac'wotsiliye.
Ik'o danosh t'ug wotar tuwit mooshonat míshon gaaketwone, asaabi jamono k'aa'uder Krstossh bíaletwok'o woshitwone.
It aleyo s'een b́wotor konnari alek'azono sezosh k'andek'tswotsi wotitwone.
It its'iilirwo úratse bek'eyiru keewo s'uziye, asho konwor wotowa Krstosk taane ett bíatso amanirwo aanide'er t'iwintswe, noowere bíkok'o Krstosk nowottsok'o dande'e.
Doonzo noosh b́imts alon ayide'er ti it'alor bín jitseratse, alan noosh ime iti agosha bako gaakoshaliye.
T woshon itn t shatiyirwok'o ark'ye itsha.
Ik ikuwots «P'awlos woshwots mangtswotsnat kup'knee, bí b́tookon noonton b́wotormó maawke, b́ noon keew keewonwere k'awntsalke» etiirunee.
Man etiru ashuwots noo wokoon wotdek'at nowoshtswotsitse noguut'irwonat t karnonowere itnton wotdek'at nofiiniruwi dagotse k'osh k'osho b́beerawok'owo dande'ene.
B́ wotefere botoko údiru ash ik ikwotsnton no tooko nohiwosh wee notooko nuutsir s'iilosh ááwo shu'atsone, bomó botoko botookonton botatstsonat botookonowere botookonton bonohitsotse t'iwints dek'knaliye.
Noomó dab itok no borfetso Ik'o noosh b́ imts fini gúúron it'etuwoone bako tatsoniyere dambo id'atsone.
It beyruwere nofiiniru gúúrots b́wottsotse Krstos dooshishiyo daniyoh itok nowoor gúúrmaniyere besheratsone.
Mansha Ik'o noosh b́beezts gúúroniyere beshar k'oshwots finon weeralo id'atsone, maniyeremó it imnetiyo b́daboor Ik'o noosh b́beezts gúúrotse noon it mangitwok'o tewnirwone.
Eshe k'osh ashi fini gúúrots kindr shin fiinets finon noid'awo itiyere oke fa'a datswotsatse bíko doo shishi aap'o shishiyosh falfone.
Ernmó «It'etwo doonzon id'ee.»
Asho údewosh b́bodet doonzo bín b́údora bako b́tooko b́tookon b́údoraliye.
Taa muk'i dog t wottsotse taash it k'amitwok'o jangirwe, oona! taash k'amde'ere.
Baarna'a s'eenu ikukok'o iti kenih iko Krstossh twid'tsotse, Ik'i okooron okoorirwe.
Dawunzo Hewaani weeri gondon b́ sheelitsok'o daneraka it asaabiyonwere awaashwtsar Krstossh itdetsts okooronat s'ayinon wottso it amanewo k'ayk'ritute etaat shatirwe.
Ik asho itok waar no nó nabtso b́woterawo k'osh Iyesusi itsh b́nabiyal wee it itdek'ts shayiro b́woteraniyere k'osh shayiro itdek'al, wee it dek'ts doo shishiyo b́ woterawo k'osh doo shishiyo it dek'al, s'k etaatni it dek'i etee.
Ernmó taa een een woshetswotsiyere jam keewon tdashtsok'o areratse.
Noon keewon dantso woto tk'azaloru dab dano taash shapatse, hanowere ayoto ay weeron kishdek' itsh danirone.
Taa Ik'i doo shushiyo itsh k'awntsalon tnabonat itn dambaan tizosh t tooko dashan t detso morrok'oweya b́ taaweyiri?
Itsh finosh k'osh Ik' moowwotsoke tep'o dek'at boon biik're.
Itnton tbeyor taash wotit keewo b shapor, Mek'odoniyon waats t eshwots taash geyits jam keewon botep'irwotse konatsoru kuro woteratse, andish b́ borfetsosh itats jam keewon kuro woteratse, shino maantsisho kuro woteratse.
Krstos arikeewo t gitsotse b́ beyirwtse hanatse tuutson t id'awok'o woshitwo Akayiyi datsatse konworu aaliye.
B́ jango eebi? Itn shuno tk'ztsosheya? Itn tshuntsok'o Ik'o danfee.
K'osh wosheets manots, «No bonk'o finirwone» err boit'et weero t'ut'iyosh and tk'alirwok'o shino maantsoru dab k'alituwe.
Hank'o ashaanots Krstossh woshetswotsi aroosh botook wonawoniru kootets woshetswotsnat ash ant'elcef finetswotsiye.
Hanwere adiyit keewaliye, shed'anonworu dab shááno melakiwotsi aroosh b́ tooko b́woniti.
Mansh eshe shed'anosh finirwots kááwosh finirwotsi aroosh bo tooko bowoniyal noon adiratse, s'uwatse bo fini k'awntso daatsitune.
«Asho konwor dartso twottsok'o bísh ark'aye» err aani keewituwe. Dartsi twotiyaloru dab múk'i t it'etwok'o dartsok'o woshde'er taan taawwore.
Hank'o it'on tkeewor t keewirwo doonzo shunok'o b́ woterawo dartsok'o wotatniye.
Aywots meets keewon bo it'iruwosh taawor it'etuwe.
It t'iwintsirwotsi it wottsok'on dartswots jangosh gene'on k'amitute.
Hank'o konworu guutsok'o itn b́ woshiyal, konworu itko b́maal, iti b́finiyal, iti b́gac'iyal, it malalats b́ jabiyal k'amitute.
Taan jitsitka wotiyaloru dab keewanotsi finosh kup'uwotsi wotnok'azo itsh kitsitwe. Ernmó konwor it'osh ááwo b́ shúk'ol taaworu bíkok'o ááwo shúk'twe, hanowere ti etir and dartsok'o wotatniye.
Bo Ibrawi ashnowa? Taawere Ibrawi ash taane, bo Israe'el ashnowa? Taawere Israe'el ash taane, bo Abraham naarnowa? Taawere Abraham naar taane.
Bo Krstos guutsnowa? Taawere boyere bogo Krstossh guuts taane, hanowere ti etor geyetsok'o wotatniye t keewiri, boyere bogo ayoto finon mawure, ayoto tipere, ayoto jot'ere, ayoto k'iri t'up'er tawats bodre,
Útsoti shaashe jeed'iyoto ayhudiwots k'ac'eyon jot'ere,
Keezoto gúmbon jot'ere, iknoto shútson k'is'ere, keezoto markabotse t'up'er tawo tiyats bodre, ik t'úwonat ik aawon aats k'aratse t teshi,
T sha'i ayon foki s'eenonat aats di'on, biik'irwotsn bik'ewo ti'ats bodre, Ayhudi jirwotsnat Ik' ash woterawotsokere t'up'er tawo tiyats bodre, Kitonat worwotse aats k'aratsnowere t'up'er tawo tiyats bodre, mank'o kootets amantsuwotsoke t'up'ertawo tiyats bodre.
Ayo finonat maawo detsfe b́ teshi, ayoto tokro t t'utfoni, k'ak'efe, shashwefe, ayoto mish t'ut'o tiyats bodre, ak'onat araats woto tiyats bodre.
K'osh jam keewo t taawoniyere Ik'i moowwotsosh aawu aawon shiyanat t kic'efoni.
Maawrawo kone, taawor mááwratsta? ash iko morron b́ dihor taawer nib t k'únaw aawo egore?
It'o b́ geyitka wotink'e taa bín ti it'etwo taa maaw ash twoto kitsit keewwotsne,
Dúre dúrosh údeek wottso no doonz Iyesus nihi Ik'o t koorawok'o danfee.
Demask'o kitotse tbeyor nugúso Aretasiyere dashe dats k'eeziruwo taan detso geeyat kitutse bín keshet weero kotirwotsn b́ kotifere b́ teshi.
Wotowa bako ashuwots kas'i tungushi fúri weeron ooshon taan oorsh bok'rere b́ kishotse k'az t keshi.
Dab it'otse daatset keewo b́ t'ut'aloru it'etwe, ernmo and doonzoke tdaatsts bek'onat be'etson keewo shunfee.
Krstosk wotts ik asho danfee, ashaan tatse awd natoniyere shinon keezl darok b́ borfetso b́ dek'eyi, b́ dek'ewewere b́ meetsontoni wotowa b́ meeston wot b́k'zo danatse, Ik'o danfee.
Ernmó ashaan Geneto maants b́ dek'etsok'o danfone, b́ meetson wotowá wotb́k'azon danatsone, Ik'o danfee,
Bíwere Geneto maants dek'eyat ash noon keewon keewosh falerawonat asho keewo b́ falaaw keewo b́ shishi.
Hank'o ashonn it'etuwe, t tokoshomó maawuk t wotoniyere okoon k'osh bín ti it'et keewo aaliye.
Eshe, taa ariko tkeewirwosh it'o tgeyiyalor dartsi woteratse, ernmó konwor tiatse b́bek'irwonat tiyoke b́k'ebirwoniyere bogshde'er taan b́s'iilawok'owa etaat it'atse tiatso kotdek'irwe.
Taash be'ets een een keewanotsatse tuutson t id'awok'o t meetso angitsok'o koshet weesho taash imeyi, hanuwere shed'ani melakiyo wotat taan túúzit onobek'shr ti id'awok'o taan b́woshiti.
Taan weeshiru keewan tiatse b́ k'aawu'etwok'o doonzo keezoto t k'oni.
Ernmó «Ti ango s'eenon b́fiinit n maaw manits b́wottsotse ts'aato neesh bodfe» taash bíeti, mansh Krstos ango tiats b́wotitwok'o jamoniyre bogo maawk twoton geneúfetsr it'o shunfee
Ango t daatsit maawk t wotor b́ wottsotse Krstos jangosh t maawor, t c'ashewor, gondo tbek'or, t gishewor, tkic'oro geneútwe.
Doogok'o keewre! eshe hank'o tkeewitwok'o taan k'altswots itne, taan údiyank'wots itna b́teshi, taa daneraw ash twotiyalor dab een eenne eteets woshetswotsiyere eegonor dasheraatse.
Ari wosheetso twoto kitsiru keewwots itnton tbewor k'amoon t k'alts fiinwotsiye, milikitanotsnat adits keewanotswere adiknee.
It ats kuro wot tk'azoniyere okoon k'osh Ik'i moowwotsiyere iti t dashiyi eegneya? Hanuwere naandok'o b́taawetka wotiyal taash oorowe erere!
Itok wosh k'andek' ttuwiyakon han keezloniye, taa itats kuro woto geeratse, taa tgeyir itna bako it gizoniyaliye. Bo nana'osh giz kakuwo b́s'ili ind nihwotsi bako nanaúwots indnihwotssh gizo ko'irakne.
Itsha err dab t gizonat t tookon beshide'er t imink'e ayideniye t geneuti, eshe taa itn ayidek'at t shunfere it taan it shunir hank'o múk'sh dek'atneya?
Ekewin wotowa hann wotowa taa itsh kuro woteratse, weeri gondonat ant'elcon iti tdetstsok'oye itsh bíari.?
T woshts ashuwotsitsere ikon dab kis'o keshrta?
Tito it maants b́ weetwok'o t k'oni, no eshu manowere bínton t woshi, eshe, Tito itoke t'k'miyo datsra? Taanat bín itsh nofin ik shayiron woteratsa? No sha sha'onwere ik woteratsa?
It únets andish b́ borfetsosh it gawir noo it shinatse notook jangosha etaat aninodek'irwok'o woshdek'aatni k'úna? Noo Krstosn wotdek'at nokeewirwo Ik'o shinaatsne, shuneetswotso! no jaman nokeewir iti kup'iyosha etaatniye.
Taa manmaants t woor daneraka it wotish t geyirwok'o it woterawon, taawere it itgeyirwok'o twoterawo gonketwonek'úna etaat shatirwe, mank'o itoke kaareyo, okooro, fayo, tookshuntsi woto, ash shúúts t'afiyo, óóno, bogtaana etonat dimbron beetúne etaat shatirwee.
Aani aanar itok twoor tiko Izar Izewer daneraka taan itshinatse ketitwe etaat shatirwe, haniyere shin bofints morratse tuutson kiimo, wido, shiraats jintsi wotatse tuutson naandrone eraaw ashuwots jangatse shiyanots kindiftak'úna etaat shatirwe.
Eshe, itok twoor han keezloniye taasha, awror b́wotiyal jam keewo arik b́ wotit wee git wee keez gawwotsne.
Gitlts s'iilo twoor itnton tteshor it tooko kor itdek'etwok'o keewatniye t teshi, andoor aaniy haniyere shin morro fintswotsnat k'oshwotsshor boatso korbodek'etwok'o keewitwe, and taa itok aanar twoor konshor maac'o k'eweratse,
It t gitsotse beyat keewirwo Krstosi b́wottsok'o dandek'oshe itgeyiri, itoke beyrwo b́kúp'a bako b́maawoniyaliye.
Bí mask'aliyats jiteyat b́k'ir maawona wotiyalor and Ik'i angon kashone b́ beyiri, noowere bíkok'o maawtswotsi woterone, itnton nodetsts gonkewok'onmó bínton Ik'i angon beetuwone.
It amantsatse it kúp'tsok'o sheengsh danosh it tooko t'iwintsde'er s'iilere, it atsono fads'iilere, Iyesus Krstos itgitsots b́wottsok'owo t'iwintsde'atsteya? Mank'o wotob́k'zal fadewor dihrte etee,
Noo fadewor nodihrawok'o dan itdek'etwok'owe nojangiri.
Gond keewo itk'alrawok'o Ik'o k'onirwone, Ik'o nok'onirwere no took faltswotsi wotat be'erani no'ooriyal it úni aawo sheeng wotts keewo it finitwok'owa bako tooko nofalo kitsoshaliye.
Noo ari keewosha nofinri bako ari keewo k'efitwo eegor k'alo falatsonee.
Noo maawtswotsi nowotere it kúp'uwotsi it wottsosh gene'úwirwone, no Ik'o nok'onir it s'eenwotsi it wotitwok'owe.
Woshan itoke wokdek' befetsat tguut'ir manatse tuutsone, hank'on itok twoor doonzo taash b́ imts alon itn kic'iratse, doonzo alo taash b́ im itn tiagisha bako iti gaakoshaliye.
Eshe ti eshúwotso! jamon beewere! it bebeyo manutside'ere, t izonowere beewere, it ats atseyosh ikwotore, jeenon beewere, shunonat jeeniko Izar Izewer itnton wotituwe.
S'ayin wotts jobon jobeyar jamo aatewere.
Amants jamwots jamo itsh t'intsirune.
Ashuwotsoke wee ash weeron b́ woterawo Iyesus Krstosnat bín k'irotse tizts Ik'o nihon wosheetso wotat wosheetso taa P'awlosoke,
Tiyoke fa'a eshú jamwotsoke Gelati Ik'i moowwotssh wosheetso.
No nihi Ik'okere, no doonz Iyesus Krstos s'aatonat jeenon itsh wotowe.
Gond dúranitse noon kashiyosh noko Izar Izewernat no nihi bí eektsosh Krstos no morrosh b́ tooko beshidek't b́ imi.
Dúre dúrosh b́ borfetso Ik'osh mango wotowe! Amen.
Krstos s'aaton itn s'eegtso Izar Izeweratse káári it k'aletsonat k'osh doo shishiyo maants it aantsok'o taane bí adiri.
Hanowere ti etir itn dandirwotsnat Krstos doo shishiyonowere k'uriyosh geyiru ik ik ashuwots bobetsosha bako doo shishiyoniyere shinoor ik s'uzee.
Wotowa eree noon wotowá, daratsi melakiyo wotowa, no nonabtsonton gáwet k'osh doo shishiyo itsh nabitwo c'ashek wotowe!
Haniyere shini t ettsok'o andoru aani eteetwe, it it dek'tsonton ik woteraw doo shishiyo konworu itsh b́ nabiyal c'ashek wotowe!
Bére, taa t geyir asho taan b́ úditwok'owemó? Ik'o taan b́ úditwok'owe? Himó ashuwotsi geneúshosh t geetsok'oweya bí ariri? Ashuwotsi geneúshosh t geyiyal Krstossh guutso woterawnk'e b́ teshi.
Ti eshwwotso! taa itsh tnaabts doo shishiyo ashoke daatsek b́woterawok'o it danetwok'o geefe.
Doo shishiyanowere Iyesus Krstosi taash bek'shi bako konoknoor de'atse, wee asho konwor taash daniratse.
Joots ayhudiwots imnetiyots tteshor aawk'o tbefok'o shishrte, Ik' moowwotsi weeralo gishefetsat t'afi bazoshe tnokorefooni.
Ayhudiwots imnetiyo kotósh tdúron teshts t jir Ayhudi jamwotsiyere bogfe b́teshi, nih nihwots niwosho okoori eeno detsfe b́teshi.
Ernmó tind maac'otse tbeefere Ik'o taan galbdek'i, b́s'aatonowere taan s'eeg b́dek'i.
Ik'i ash woterawots b́ naay jangosh doo shishiyi aap'o t shishitwok'o Ik'o b́ naayi taash kitsosh b́geyor taa kontonwor shiyeratse,
Taayere shin teshts woshetswotsi gonkeyono Iyerusalem maants amatse, ernmó shin Araawi datsomants k'az tiami, ando aaninwere Demask'o maantse k'az tiaani.
Maniyehakowere keez natoniye hakon Keefi eteefo P'et'rosnton daneyosh Iyerusalem maants ti ami, manoknowere bínton tatse úúts aawo tteshi.
Doonzo eshu Yak'obi tbek'i bako wosheets k'oshwotsitse konnor be'atse.
Itsh tguut'irwan kooto b́ woterawok'o Ik' shinatse itsh katsidek' danirwe.
Maniyere hakon Soriyi datsonat Kilk'i datso maants tiami.
Yhud Datsatse fa'a Krstos Ik'i moowwots t shiitso bek' danakne boteshi.
Bo boshishtsonu «Bali noon giishat teshts asho bali t'afiyosh b́geyiru imnetiyo and b́nabiri» etirwoniye.
Ti atse tuutsonowere Ik'o boúdi.
Tatse awd natoniyere hakon Bernabasnton Iyerusalem maants aanat tiami, Titonowere taanton dek'at amree b́teshi.
Man maants tiamwere Ik'o taash kitst b́bek'shtsok'onee. Haniyere shin t fintso wotowa and t fintso dats mec'r wotar b́datserawok'owa etaat Ik'i ash woterawwotssh tnabiru doo shishiyo een een wotts jishirwotssh bo aal aalshe t daniyi.
Taanton fa'o Tito Grik dats ash b́wotiyalor gofo bíametwok'o kic'iyeeratse.
Ernmó nodagots ááshon mut'at kindts ik ik kootets eshwots gofo bíametwok'o geeyatniye boteshi, ashaanots k'ororosh noyits mut'at bokind Krstos Iyesusn nodetsts s'ayin no keshtso bi'ide'er guutsmots noon aaniyo geeyatniye.
Noomó doo shishiyi arikeewo itoke kup'arr b́beetwok'wa etaat dab múk' sa'atoshor ekewotssh da'eratsone.
Ik'o ash ááwo s'iilr b́bogabogshrawotse, jisht teshts ashaanots koni bowotiyalor bojangosh taa kic'eratse, bo taa t keewiru doo shishiy aap'ats handr keewo eegor dabraatsne.
Ik'o P'et'rossh ayhudiwotssh doo shishi adaro b́ imetsok'on taashor doo shishi adaro Ik'i ash woterawwotssh t shishiyitwok'o b́wooshtsok'o bo t'iwintsdek'rnee,
Mansh eshe P'et'rosi ayhudiwotssh wosheetso wotar b́finitwok'o woshtso Izar Izewer taanor Ik' ash woterawwotssh wosheetso wotar t finitwok'o woshre.
Irok'o araat be'eyiru jishirwots Yak'obnat P'et'rosu, Yohanswere Ik'i s'aaton k'osh wotts fini gowan taash b́ imtsok'o bodantsosh taanat Bernabasnton ik bowoti milikit wottso bok'ani kisho noosh imrne, shiyeyat no Ik' ash woterawwotsok no ametuwok'o boowere Ayihudiyots maants bo ametuwok'o bok'ali.
S'uznmó bo dagotse fa'a tuguretswotsi no baterawok'o noosh oona etrne, hanwere arikon k'alosh t geef keewoniye.
P'et'ros Soriyotse fa'a Ans'okiyo maants b́ woor dart b́ teshtsotse b́ shinatsere bín t k'efi,
Yak'ob b́ woshts ik ik ashuwots Ans'okiyo maants bowaafetsere shin Ik' ash woteraw ashuwotsitsere amantsuwotsnton towaat mááfetsetni b́ teshi, bo boweyiyakonomó, «Ik' ash woteraw jirwotsitsere amantsuwots gof amo boosh geyife» etiru jirwotsn shatt shuutso maants aanat Ik' ash woterawwotsatse b́ galeyi.
K'osh ayhudi jir wotts Krstiyaniwotswor ayhudi woterawwotsnton mish móó gond b́wottsok'o aridek't P'et'roskok'o bok'ali, Barnabasworu dab b́ oreraniyere be'eyi darman maants getseyatniye b́ teshi.
Bo k'altsan doo shishi arikeewonton ik wotob́k'azo t bek'tsok'on P'et'rossh, «Nee ayhudi wotefetsat ayhudi nemok'on b́ woterawo Ik' ash woterawwots nemok'one n beefoni. Eshe, Ik' ash woterawwots ayhudoyots nemok'on bobetwok'o eegishe angnon n k'aliri?» etaat jami shinatse bín t k'efi.
Arikon no noshuweyon Ayhudi noona bako morretsk wotts Ik' ash woterawwotsnonaliye.
Ernmó asho kááw b́ wotit Krstos Iyesusi amanona bako nemo s'eentson b́ woterawok'o danfone, noowere nem s'eentson b́woterawo Krstosi amanon kááw nowotitwok'o Krstos Iyesusi amanerone, konwor asho nemo s'eentsr kááw woteratse.
Krstosi amanon kááw wotosh nogeyor no notookon morretswotsi wotar nodatsetka wotiyal eshe, morro no finitwok'o woshirwo Krstosiye eteya? mank'owiyaliye!
Taa ttookon t gáákts nemi niwok'owa aani tfiniri wotiyal taa t tookon nemosh alerawo twotok'oniye t kitsiri etee.
Ik'osh t beetwok'owa etaat k'irok'o k'aleyon nematse k'alere. Taa Krstosnton jitetsok'o t taawetsotse
haniyere okoon Krstosi t gitsotse beeti bako taa t tookon beetk tanliye, and t meets atson t beyir taan shuntsonat taash b́ tooko beshidek't imts Ik' na'o amanon daatsets kashone.
Ik' s'aato k'awntsalo oriratse, asho kááw b́ wotit nemo s'eentson b́wotiyal Krstos b́ k'ir datsmec'ra etee.
It dárts Gelati dats ashuwotso! kone iten teziyik'ri? Iyesus Krstos it shinatse jitats jiteyat b́teshtsok'on itsh sháánidek't keewere b́teshi.
Itoke danosh tgeyirwo han s'uziye, arikon it S'ayin shayiro it dek' nemo s'eentsoneyamó? Doo shishiyosh aap'etso shishat amanoneya?
It Ik' shayiron dek' tuwat andmo meetson ishoshe it geyiri, eshe hanok'o dark itne.
Doo shishi jangosh it dek'ts gond bek' jamo k'awtsalo wotat orere eteya? Han k'alrte wotiyal arikon k'awtsalko orere etee.
Ik'o b́ shayiro itsh bí imirwonat itokere adit fino b́ finir nemok'o it finirwoshemó? Doo shishiyosh aap'etso shishat it amanirwoshe?
Hanwere «Abrahamiye Ik'o b́ amani, manwere kááw wotat bísh b́ taaweyi» ett guut'etsok'one.
Eshe amanirwots Abraham nanaúwotsi bowotok'o dande'ere.
Ik'o Ik' ash woterawwotsi imnetiyon kááw b́ woshitwok'o S'ayin mas'aafo shino be'er «Ash jamwots neen deretúne» ett Abrahamsh shin doo shishi aap'o keewere.
Eshe amaniru jamwots amantso Abrahamnton deretune.
«Nemi mas'afotsere guut'ets tzaziyi jamon kúp'ar berawonat finats jitsraw jamo c'asheke» ett guut'etsotse «Nemo finats jiitson kááwwotsi wotitwone» etirwots c'ashekne.
«Kááw ashonmó imnetiyon kasho daatsitwe» ett guut'etsosh nemi fin s'eentson asho konwor Ik' shinatse kááw b́ woterawok'o daneke.
Nemo imnetiyats ned'iyekaliyee, mank'owere «Asho nemon beyo b́ falit nemi tzazi jamwotsi finats b́ jitsiyale» ett guut'ere.
«Mitats jitere k'iritu jamo c'asheke» ett guut'etsotse Krstos noosh c'ashets ash wotat nemi dowet c'ashmanitse noon b́ kishi.
Hanwere b́ wot Ik'o Abrahamsh b́ imts deero Iyesus Krstos weeron Ik' ash woterawwotsok b́ bodetwok'onat noowere Ik'o itesh imetwe bí etts Shayiri s'ayino imnetiyon nodek'ishe.
T eshwotso! aab keewan ashoke daneets keewonton ik woshde'er s'iilone, ash iko b́ kindts taaro kááwar b́ ned'iyakon konwor oriyosh wee dabosh falatse.
Ik'o Abrahamnat b́ naarosh jangiyets aap'wotsi b́ im hank'one, jangiyon aap'etso aywotssh b́ wottsok'o woshdek't «Nnaarwotssha» eraatse, ernmó ikosh b́ wottsok'o «Nnaarosha» etfe, «Nnaara» etetsanwere Krstosiye.
Eshe taa ti etirwo haniye, awd bale shaash natoniyere il imets nemo shino Ik'okere s'ayntsdek't imets taaro gaahr jangiyets aap'man t'afiyo falratse.
Ik keewo naatet nemok'ona wotink'ere jangit imets aap'i weeron b́ woto orere b́ teshi, ernmó Ik'o naato Abrahamsh bí'im jangit b́ aap'tsoshe.
Eshe, nemo ime eegoshe? Nemo dabee Abrahamsh jangiyon imets naaro b́ wafetsosh nomrratse tuutsone, nemo melakiyo weeron beshat dagi taalotsi ash ikosh imere.
Ernmó dagtalotse bede'er manit asho git jirosha bako ik jiro s'uzosh fineratse, Ik'onmó ike.
Eshe nemo Ik' jangits keewo k'efitwa? B́ jamon k'eferatse! kasho daatsit nemo imere wotink'e kááw woto nemi weerone b́ datseyak'oni b́ teshi.
Ernmó Iyesusi amanon daatset jangets keewo amantsuwotssh imetwok'o S'ayin mas'aafo b́ etirwok'o dats jamu morrosh kéweyat morron tipetsu woterane.
Imnetiyo b́ waftsere shinon nemosh tipetswotsiye noteshi, hanwere imnetiyo b́ be'efetsosh nemo noon kotdek't detsdek'tniye b́ teshi.
Hank'on, imnetiyon kááw no wotitwok'o Krstos b́ wááfetsosh nemo noon ditsirwo wotatniye b́ teshi.
Andomó imnetiyo b́ waatsosh nemi ditsi shirots nowoto orere.
Iyesus Krstosi amanon it jametswor Ik' nanaúwotsi woterte,
Gúpeyon Krstosnton ik wotts it únetswots Krstosi tahok'o tahadek'rte.
It jametswor Krstos Iyesusn ik it wottsotse ayhudiyonat Girikiyon, gútsonat guuts woterawon, núngushonat máátson dagotse eegoru k'osh k'osheyo aaliye.
Eshe Krstosk it wotiyakon Abraham naar itne, jangiyets aap'mank'on naatetwots itne.
Andoor tietirwo haniye, naatetwo na'i marmat'o wotar b́ daatsewor dets jamosh doonzo b́wotiyalor guutsoniyere eegonor k'osheratse.
Ernmó b́nih bísh b́gedts aawo b́borfetsosh ditsirwotsnat maanzirwots shirootse b́ wotiti.
Mank'owere no shayiri keewon nana'i marmat'wotsk'o noteshor datsan niwoosh keewetswotsi wotat gutswotsiye noteshi.
Ernmó eteets dúro b́bodtsok'on Ik'o b́naayi noosh b́woshi, bíwere nemi shirots wotat máátsatse b́shuweyi.
Hano b́k'al Mesee nemi shirotse teshtswotsi aani kewdek'onat noonowere Ik' nana'úwotskok'o noon woshoshe.
Ik' nana'úwotsi it wottsosh Ik'o «Nihono!» ett s'eegiru naayo shayiro no nibots b́woshi.
Mansh eshe haniyak na'a neena bako guuts neenaliye, na'a nwotiyalo Ik'atse tuutson naatetwots neene.
Haniye shin Ik'o it dartsatse tuutson bo doyon izar izewerotsi woterawwotssh guutso wotatni it kéweefoni.
Andmó Ik'o danrte, dabnwor Ik'o itn danre, bere, ekeewots maawtswotsnat k'awntsal datsanatsi nemwotsok awk'oniya it aani? Aawuk'oneya ún aani aanat bo guutswotsi wotosh itgeyiri?
K'osh k'osh aawwotsnat shashwotsn woriwoti kaywotsitsnat natwotsitse it atso kotosh k'osh wotts mango it imiri.
It dagotse finon t maawts maaw jamo k'awntsalo oritwe etniye t shatiri.
T eshwotso! taa itkok'o t wottsosh itwere tikok'o wotoore etaatniye t k'oniri, it taan eegoru daderatste.
Shini doo shishiyi aap'o itsh nabosh gowo t daats t shodtsatse tuutson b́wotok'o danfte.
T shodo dab itsh fadee b́ wotiyaliru taan gac'eratste wee taan wic'atste, dab melakiyo it dek'iruwok'owe woshdek'at taan it dek'i, Krstos Iyesusi dek'iruwok'o woshat taan it dek'i.
Haniyere shini it detsts geneú jamo aawoke b́fa'oni? B́ faleyal it ááwwotsi dab kishde'er it imetwok'o taa t tookon gaw wotitwe.
Eshe, and ariko itsh t keewtsosheya it balangaro wotat t daatseyi?
K'osh ashuwots it jangosh kic'atniye boshiyaniri, ernmó han bok'alir sheengoshaliye, bo geyirwo it noatse it k'aletwok'owonat boosh kúp'ar it shiyanitwok'owe.
Sheeng k'os'osh kúp'o jam gizewon shenge, ernmó it kúp'an taa itnton t beyor s'uzosh wotk'aye.
T nana'otso! Krstos it atse sháánon b́ be'efetsosh aani it jangosh na'it'i shambatse t fa'oni.
Itsh eeg k'alo taash b́ geyituwok'o itdartsotse dandeyatniye t kic'i, it dagotetsere datseyar k'osh k'osh noon keewon tkeewink'ere aawk'owe t shuni.
It nemosh keewetswotsi wotar beyo geyirwots aab taash keewwere, nemo bíetirwo shiyatsteya?
S'ayin mas'aafwotsitse «Abraham git nana'úwotsi detsfe b́teshi, iko b́shwee gonuwatse wotat k'oshonu b́shwee mááts gon woteraawwatsna b́teshi» ett guut'ere.
Gonu naay b́shuwe meets niwok'on b́wotefere gon woteraw naay b́shuwemó bísh jangit aap'etsok'one b́teshi.
Shints taarets taaretsnwere Sin guratstsu b wotor gutsmosh wotit nana'o shuwiruniye, biwere Agariye.
Agaar Araawi datsatse fa'a Sin guro ariyetsuniye bteshi, mansh eshe andtsu Iyerusalemntoniye biariri, bi bnanaúwotsnton guutsmotse fa'úniye.
Dambe darotsik wottsu Iyerusalemmó goniyaliye, biye no indiye.
«Nee nana'a shuraawne gene'úwowe! Nee shuwosh id'r danaawne ‹ílll› eree, Kenih detsts máátsuniyere K'azk'rets máátsu ay nana'o detsfane» ett guut'ere.
Tieshwotso! itwere Yisaak'kok'o jangiyets aap'i nana'úwots itne.
Ernmó manoor meetson shuwetso Shayiron shuweetsman b́gishtsok'o hambetsoor mank'oyiye.
Ernmó S'ayin mas'aafo bíetirwo eebi? S'ayin mas'aafo «Mááts gonu bshuts na'o gon woteraw máátsu bshutsonton towaar b́naarawotse gonu bnaaynton okaan kishwe» etfe.
Mansh eshe tieeshwotso, noo s'ayinu nana'úwots noone bako gonu nanaúwots noonaliye.
Krstos nas'o noon b́kish nas'on nobeyishe. Mansh eshe kup'arr need'ore, aaninwere guutsmi k'ambariyots tipek'ayere.
Hambe! taa P'awlos itsh tietetwo haniye, gofo it amal Krstos itsh eegor k'alratse,
Gof ametu jamo «Nem jam s'eentso bín geyife» err aani bísh keewitwe,
It nem koton kááw wotosh geyiru jamwots Krstosatse k'alewtserte, b́ s'aatotsnowere keshrtee.
Noomó Ik' shayiron kááwi wotosh jángiyetso imnetiyone nokotiri.
Iyesus Krstosn beetwosh shunon finitwo imnetiya boko gof amaa wee amk'azo eegoru oot'o imatse.
It sha'a sha'o sheenge b́ teshi, eshe and arkeewosh it alerawok'o itn bazitso kone?
Hank'o izan itn s'eegts Ik'oke waakaliye.
Manwere boot' shash muk'ú boot' jamo b shashitwoshe.
Ernmó haniyere k'osho it gawirwo it deshawok'osh arikon wotde'er doonzats amanittwe, konworu it took s'adiitwo b́ beyal angsho dek'etwe.
Tí eshwotso! taa andish b́ borfetsosh t nabirwo, «Kashosh gof amo geyife» etirwe wotiyal andish b́ borfetsosh eegishe t gisheyiri? Hank'o b́ wotitka wotiyal Krstos mask'aliyo ashuwotssh t'ug woterawnk'e b́ teshi.
Eshe hanots iti dandiru ashaanots bogeyiyal gof amo s'uzi b́ woterawo boatso gato bowoshink'ere shúnfe.
Tí eshwotso! it nas'o keshtswotsi it wotish s'egerte, ernmó iko k'oshosh shunon finowa bako nas'o it keshaan meets tewno s'eentsosh wotk'aye.
Nem jamo «K'osh asho n tokok'o woshde'er shune» eteets aap' ikon s'eenetwe.
Ernmó it atsatseyo shac'eyatni it meeyeyiri wotiyal it atsatseyo it s'uweerawok'oo it atso korde'ere.
Eshe haniyak shayiron jisheyar it betka wotiyal, meets tewno s'eentsk'ayere.
Meets tewno shayiri tewnontotoniye b́ wed'eyiri, shayiri tewnonu meets tewnontoniye b́wed'eyri, mansh meetsonat shayiron boats atsewo bo wed'eyiri, eshe it geyirwo k'alo falratste.
Shayirona it jiisheyiri wotink'eremó nemosh keweyirwotsi woterawnk'te.
Meetsi finwots daneknee, boowere wido, kiimwoto, shiraats jintsi woto,
Woteraw ik'wotsi ik'iyo, atetsi woto, balangar woto, mooshewo, fayo, okooro, b́took shuno, k'aleyo, weeri gondo,
ash een shit'o, másho, weral t'oola, hanotsi artswotsiye, haniyere shin itatso korde'ere tiettsok'on andoor aaniyi it atso korde'ere etirwe, hanotsk'o wotts keewwotsi finit ashuwots Ik'i mengtstu naaratsne.
S'ayin shayiri shuwonmó shuno, geneúwo, jeeno, k'amo, sheengo, doowo, amanetso woto,
Dingato woto, b́took keewoniye. Hanotsk'o keewwotsi k'efit nemo aaliye,
Krstos Iyesusk wotts ashuwots meetso b́gusiyontonat b́tewnonton mesk'eliyats jitk'rerne.
Shayirona nobeeyiri wotiyal shayiron jishewone.
Iko k'osho gondosh tuuzr noatsatsewo okoorefetsr datsmec'ro it'k'ayone.
Ti eshwotso! ash iko morro finar b́daatsetka wotiyal shayiri ash wottswots it han naari asho maac' nefon káátswere, ernmó neewere man naari fadewots ndihrawok'o ntooko korde'e.
Ititsi ik ikets k'oshoko kuri mango kurde'e, mank'oon Krstos nemo s'eentsitute.
Asho konwor k'oshwotsiyere b́k'ants keewo b́deshawo «Taa k'oshwotsiyere bogfe» err biasabiyal b́ tookoniye b́ ant'elciri.
Asho ik ikon b́took fino shu'arr fadbe'e, maniyere il b́ tooko k'oshwotsnton nohiyo b́woterawon b́ tooku s'uz bín b́ it'et keewo daatsitwe.
Ik ik asho b́ took kuro kurdek'o bísh geyife.
Doo shishyi aap'tso daniru asho bín daniyirwonton sheeng keew jamó kayde'e.
It tooko ant'elck'ayere, asho b́k'es'et b́ shooktso b́wottsotse Ik'ats kasho faleratse.
B́ meetso gene'úshosh shookirwo b́meetsatse k'iro k'es'etwe, shayiro geneúshosh shooketwo shayiratse dúre dúri kasho k'es'etwe.
Maac'o k'ut'dek'o no k'azetka wotiyal b́dúro b́bodor mááy katso nokakwitwotse sheeng fino finosh maawk'ayone.
And wotts aawo nodetstsotse ash jamwotssh bítsnor amaniru ashuwotssh sheeng keewo k'alwone.
Aawk'o een een fidalwotsn han t kíshoon t guut'tsok'o s'iilere!
Gofo itametwok'o iti kic'irwots úratse sheeng araar be'ewo geyiru ashuwotsiye. Han k'alirwotswere Krstos mask'aliyatse tuutson gishewo boats b́boraawok'owa ettniye.
Boohe it meetsats it'osha ettni gofo itametwok'owo bogeyiri bako gof amtswotswor dab botokish nemo koratsne.
Nodoonz Iyesus Krstos mask'aliyoniyere okoon k'oshon it'o tiatse wokowe, jit hanatse tuutson datso tiatse k'alewtsere, taawere datsatse k'alewtsere.
Mansh gof amonu gof amk'azonu eegor k'alratse, k'alitwoniyere azeets handro wotoniye.
Memeri shuutso shoyiru jamwotsnat Ik'i jir wotts Isra'el ashuwotssh jeenonat mhretiyon wotowe.
Ti atsatse fa'a jot'eetsi shoro Iyesusk twottsok'o b́kitsirwotse haniyak konúwor taan kic'ik'aye.
Ti eshwotso! nodoonz Iyesus Krstos s'aato it shayironton wotowe! Amen.
Ik' shunon Iyesus Krstossh woshek wottso P'awlosoke, Iyesus Krstosn amanek wottswots, Efesonitse beyiru S'ayinwotssh.
No nihi Ik'onat nodoonz Iyesus Krstosokere s'aatonat jeenon itsh wotowe.
Darotse fa'a shayiri deer jamo Krstosn noon deertso no doonz Iyesus Krstos nihi Ik'o údewe.
S'ayinonat eeg eego deshawwotsi wotaarr b́ shinatse nodaatsetwok'o datsu b́ azeftsere Krstos weeron noon gal b́dek'i.
Ik'o b́ geetso sheeng keew b́ wottsotse Iyesus Krstos finon b́ nanaúwotskok'o no wotish bale noon marat'b́dek'i.
Hanowere b́ k'al b́shune na'o weeron beenon noosh b́ imts mang wotts s'aato b́ úditwok'owe.
Ik' s'aati s'eenatse tuutson b́ naay s'atson keeweyat no morrosh orowa eto daatsrone.
B́ s'aatono ayidek't noosh kuut're, danonat dani teleefonowere,
Ik'o b́ shuntso Krstos weeron bali b́ k'úmtsok'on ááshat teshts b́shunman no danetwok'o woshre.
Dúri s'uwi aawo b́ bodor Ik'o finats b́ jitsts b́ k'úmtsman daronat datsatse beyiru azeets jamwots ko'ide'er ik s'uzo Krstos shirots bo wotitwok'o b́ woshiti.
Jam keewo b́ took shunok'on finiru Ik'o bali b́ k'úmtsok'on Krstos weeron b́ jirwotsi no wotitwok'o noon marat'b́dek'i.
Man b́wotwere Krstosi jángon shintswotsi wottswots noo Ik'o b́mangosh no úditwok'owe.
It it kashosh doo shishi aap' wottso ari aap'o it shishor Krstosi it amani, mank'o bí itsh imosh jangit b́ teshts S'ayin shayri matabo itats togk'rere.
Shayiranwere b́ mango údosh b́ wotitwok'o Ik'o bík wotts jamwotsi b́ kashifetsosh nodaatsit naatosh dets nodek'tsoniye.
Eshe doonzo Iyesusatse it detsts imnetiyonat S'ayin jamwotssh it detsts shuno shishat,
itn Ik' k'onon gawfetsat it jangosh Ik'osh údo t'intso need'iratse.
Mango bísh wotitwo no doonz Iyesus Krstos nihi Ik'o ayide'er it danetwok'o dani teleefonat bek'i shayiro itsh b́ imetwok'o Ik'o k'onitwe.
Aaw naari jangosh it s'egetsok'onat S'ayinwots bo naatet mang wotts ristiyo aawk'o ayi b́ wotok'o it danetwok'o it nibi ááwo b́ sháánetwok'o Ik'o k'onitwe.
Tatsdeshaw bí angi eeno noosh amanirúwotssh aawk'o een b́ wotok'o it danetwok'o Ik'o k'onitwe,
Bí anigi eenano finats b́jiitsi k'irotse tuzdek't darotse b́ k'ano maants b́ beeztso Krstosne.
Ik'o niho Krstosi darotse b́ k'ano maants b́ beez aaw naari alguroniyre, aloniyere, naashoniyere, angoniyere, doonzwottsonat shúúts jamoniyere damb aaninwere datsan s'uzats b́ woterawo weet datswatsnorniye.
Jam keewo b́ aali shirots woshdek't bísh b́keewiyi, Ik' maatsnowere jamoniyere damb b́ wotitwok'o tooko bín b́ woshi.
Ik' moowniye bí atsuniye, jamó b́ jamon s'eentsitwo bín s'eenon kiitsitwaniye.
It it daadonat it morri jangosh it shayiri beyon k'irk itne it teshi,
Manoor datsanatsi gond sha'ok'owa it sha'efoni, aaninwere jongatse fa'a shayiri angwotsi keewirwosha it alefoni, bíwere and azazeraw ashuwotsatse finiru kim shayironiye.
Nó jametswere haniye shinon bo dagotse no meets shunok'onat no maac' gawirwo shoydek'at sha'at no meets tewnok'o beyaatniye no teshi, k'oshwotskok'o no azeewon Ik' fayi shirotsne noteshi.
Ernmó Ik' maac' k'ewo ay b́ wottsonat noosh b́ detsts shuno een b́ wottsatse tuutson,
No morron k'irk nowotiyaloru Ik'o Krstosnton kashetswotsi no wotitwok'o woshre, it kashwere b́ s'aatone.
Ik'o Iyesus Krstosnton k'irotse tuuzt daritsi beyokoke bínton noon b́beezi.
Han b́k'alwere Krstos Iyesusn noosh k'eshdek't b́kiitsts doowonat bínton nutsiyetwo deshawo s'aati gaalo weet dúrwotsitse noosh kitsosha etniye.
It it kash imneti weeron wotts s'aatone, manwere Ik' ima bako itokikaliye.
Konwor asho b́ id'aawok'owa, kashiyit s'aato b́daatse finonaliye,
Noo Ik'o bal b́k'anits sheengo finefetsr nobetuwok'o Krstos Iyesus weeron aaniyi azeets Ik'i aztswots noone.
Mansh eshe, bal it shwewon Ik'i ash woterawwotsi it teshtsok'o, Ayhdiwots ash kishon gofo boamtsosh it'fetst itsh gof amawwotsi ett boc'ashfok'o,
it Israe'el ashuwotsnton gonke deshawwots, Ik'o bí ashuwotssh b́jangitswtsats need'iyets aap'i taarwotssho ib wottswots, datsanatsnowere it jangiru ik keewalonat Ik'alon beyirwots, manorowere Krstosatse wokat it teshtsok'o gawde'ere.
Andmó it haniyere shin wokat teshtswots Krstos Iyesusn wotdek'at b́s'atson t'inrte.
Noon k'ált teshtso fayi girgido b́meetson gáákt Ayhdiwotsnat Ik'i ash woterawwotsn ik woshtso nojeeno Krstosiye.
Git jirmanotsitse bínton ikwotitwo ik handr asho azosh Muse nemi tzaziyonat b́ niwwotsi gaakt jeeno b́woshi.
Mask'aliyatse k'irtnwere s'aaleyar beyo k'aaúbazre, gitetswtsnowere ik atso woshdek't Ik'onton maniree.
Waatnwere, wokat teshtswotssh itnat karnt teshts ayhudiwotsshowere jeen dooshiy aap'o nabre.
Bíyatse tuutson no gitetswor ik shayiron jisheyr nihok t'inetwone.
Mansh eshe it S'ayinwotsnton ik datsi ashuwotsnat Ik'i maa ashuwots itna bako haniyere okoon ibonat ashdatsi ashuwots itnaliye.
Woshetswotsnat nebiywotsn need'itsats agerte, ageyiru maamansh tungúshatse shutswotse kaatsde detset shúts kup'o Iyesus Krstosiye.
Maa eenmanu b́ jamon bín ikok desheyarr doonzo S'ayin Ik' moo wotarr eenetwe.
Ik'o b́ shayiron bíts b́ beet moo wotosh itwere Krstosn tohaar ageetute.
Itsh Ik' ash wotserawwotssha etaatni taa P'awlos Krstos Iyesussh tipetso t woti.
Itsh t sheengshitwok'o Ik'o b́ s'aaton fini gowo taash b́ imtsok'o arikon shishrte.
Bal k'awnon itsh t guut'etsok'o Ik'o ááshts man taash k'eshdek't kitsre.
Itsh t guut'tsan it nababor Krstosko ááshts keewo taa t t'iwintstsok'o danosh falfte.
Ááshts keewanwere Ik' shayiron S'ayin woshetswotsnat nebiyiwotssh and b́ be'etsok'on beshts dúrwotsatse teshts ashuwotssh be'eratse.
Manwere b́ kitsir Ik' ash woterawwots ayhudiyotsnton b́ rstiyo naatetuwotsnat ik atsi kaywotsi wotar Ik'o b́ imts jangosh dooshishi weeron Krstos Iyesusnton kayitwotsi bo wottsoniye.
Ik'o b́ angi finon taash b́ imts s'aaton taawere doo shishiyansh finru guutso wotere.
Taa S'ayin wotts jamwotsiyere t múk'iyaloru dab́ daar deshaw Krstos gaalo manwere doo shishiyo Ik' ash woterawwotssh t shishiish Ik' s'aato taash b́ imi.
Mank'o beshts dur jamwotsatse jam azts Ik'on ááshat teshts Ik'o b́ beeztso eeg b́ wotok'o jamosh t kitsitwok'o s'aato taash imere.
Manwere b́ wot and dúranatse Ik' maa weeron daaratse fa'a alirwotsnat naashwotsn Ik' dan teleefo bí ar arok'on bo danetwok'owe.
Ik'o no doonz Krstos Iyesusn han findek't b́s'eents dúre dúrosh b́ k'úmtsok'one.
Krstosk no wottsonat bín no amantsosh Ik' shinatse ááwu shúk'onat imneityon t'inosh falfone.
Taa it jangosh t dek'iru gond bek'o it mangoshee b́ wotiti, mansh t gond bek'i jangatse tuutson it ango b́neferawok'owa etaat itn k'onirwe.
Eshe Ik'o Niho shinats t gubron tuk'umalde'k'aat Ik'o t k'onir han jangoshe.
Daronat datsatse fa'a ik ik maa asho koni b́ wottsok'o b́ daatsit Ik'okne.
Ik'o it gitsitsi atso kúp'shit ango b́ shayiri weeron b́ mangi gaalon b́ imetwok'o Ik'o k'onitwe.
Mank'owere Krstos imnetiyon it nibots b́ betwok'onat itwere s'ap'ar shunon kúp' it wotitwok'o Ik'o k'onitwe.
Ando aani Krstos shuno b́ gaawnonat b́ genzon, danmban b́ tuwonat dashan b́ gop'on, awúk'o b́ wotok'o S'ayin jamwotsnton s'eenon t'iwintso falr,
ash danoniyere bog wotts Krstos shuno it danetwok'o Ik'o b́ s'een jamon s'eenosh it bodetwok'o Ik'o k'onitwe.
Eshe mansh noyitse finirwo bí'angi weeron nok'onirwonat nogawirwoniyere danmb ayide'er bogshde k'alo falitwo Ik'o Izar Izewer,
bísh Ik'i moonat Krstos Iyesusn dúr jamon dúre dúrosh mango wotowe!, Amen.
Eshe doonzosh t fintsosh tipeets wottso taa, it s'eegets s'eegosh geyik wotts beewon it beetwok'o itn k'onirwe.
Shunon it took tookon k'amefetsr tooko dashan detson maac' nefonat faleyon beewere,.
Jeenon it atsatseyo deshede'er Ik' shayirotse daatseyiru ik woto kotosh kúp'owere.
It s'eegeyor ik jángosh it s'eegetsok'o ik atsonat ik shayiro fa'ee.
Aaninuwere doonz iko, imneti ikonat gup iko fa'ee.
Dabnwere jamoniyere damb wottso, jamotse wotde finitwo, jamotse beetwo, jamosh nih wottso ik Ik'o Izar Izewer fa'ee.
Ernmó Krstos imosh bí ettsok'o bodtso no took tookosh s'aati imo noosh imere.
Mansh S'ayin mas'afotsere, «Damb b́keshor mus'o mus'dek'tni bí'ami, Ashuwotsshowere imuwotsi b́ imi» eteetsok'owiye.
Beree «Dambaan b́ keshi» etiru aap'an shini shin datso maants, datsotsnoru ayidek't dashan wotts beyok b́ ot'tsoni bako k'osho eebi b́ kitsiri?
Dashan ot'tsanwere bí jamo s'eenosh dar jamoniyere damb keshtsoniye.
Bíwere ik ikwotsi wosheetso, ik ikwotsi bek'etswotsi, ik ikwotsi doo shishiyo nabitwotsi, ik ikwotsi amantsuwotsi jinetwotsi, ik ikwots danitwotsi bowotitwok'o imuwotsi boosh b́ imi.
Hanowere b́ k'al amantswotsi kirstani finosh k'anir Krstos ats wotts Ik' moowu bi agetuwok'owe.
Ando Ik' na'o danon imnetiyon daatseyiru ik wotok bodroone, Krstos s'ayinonat s'een b́ wottsok'o noowere ik wotde s'een asho no wotitwok'owe.
Haniyere okoon ashuwots gondonat ant'elcosh k'andek'ts dani jongonat aats fundon hake bako gifnide'er daamet nanaúwotskok'o woteratsone.
Dab maniyere aro shunon keewfetsr jam keewon took wottso Krstos maants eenetwone.
K'osh k'osh atsi kaywots bodesh Krstosne, ats jamonwere ikok b́ deshee shas'wotsne, eshe ik ik atsi kayo bísh eteets fin sheengshde'er b́ finor ats jamo bí eneti, shunonowere b́ kup'iti.
Haniyakon, k'awntsalkeew gawirw Ik' ash woterawwotskok'o beek'ayere etaat doonzo shútson it tooko kor it dek'etwok'o itsh keewre,
Bo asaabiyo t'aluwtskee, bodaronat bo k'elikúp'i jangosh Ik'o boosh bí imts beyatse k'alernee.
Jitso bot'ut'tsosh kim jamo k'alosh bo tewnirwotse botoko meets tewunosh beshidek't imrne.
Itmó Krstos jango hank'owaliye it dani,
Arikon b́ jango shishrte, aronwere Iyesusitse b́ fa'ok'o bín danrte,
Mansh antelchde'er morro maants jishit Woteraw tewno shini bín it beyiru nat wotts it azeets doyo okaan juu bayere.
It nibonat asaabiyon b́ jamon handr wotowe,
Arik wotts kááwonat S'ayinon Ik' arok'on azeetso handr atso tahade'ere.
Eshe kooto keewk'ayere, no jamets ik atsi kaywotsi no wottsotse no ats atsewo ari keewo keewwone.
Fayore! it fayonomo morro fink'ayere, it fayetsok'on it befere aawo ilk'aye.
Dablossh b́ kindit fúro imk'ayere.
Ump'irwo haniyak úmp'k'aye, dab kic'tswotssh b́ imish gizo b́ daatsitwok'o b́ kishon sheeng fino finowe.
B́ jamon it nonotse woteraw keewo keshk'aye, maniyere dab shishetwotsi geneúshitwonat kup'shosh wotitu keewo ashuwotssh keewwere.
It kashts aawo b́ kiitstwok'o wotitwo it ats jot'ets Ik' S'ayin Shayiro shiyanik'ayere.
S'aam woto, nib k'úno, fayo, kúúho, c'ashonat kon naari gond jamo it atsere okaan wokowe.
Maniyere it ats atseyosh doowwotsnat maac' nefwotsn, shiyanitwotsnat imetwotsi wotoore, Ik'o Krstosn it morro itsh orowe bí ettsok'o it were it atsatsewosh orowe erre.
Haniyere okoon shuneets nanaúotskok'o itwere Ik' shuuts sha'irwotsi wotoore,
Krstos noon b́ shuntsok'onat Ik'o geneúshit sheeng sháák' detsts imonat wosho woshdek't b́ kasho noosh beshidek't b́ imtsok'o itwere shunon beewere,.
Han naari keewan Krstiyaniyosh b́ geyirawotse wido wee kon naari kiimo wee jaalo itokere shishek'aye.
Maniyere dab Ik'osh udo t'intswere bako iritwonat dárts ash keewo, wee aatsni keewu keewo itesh woteratse, hank'o keewan itsh geyiratse.
Gobetso b́ witiyal, kon naari kim fin finiruwo b́ wotiyal, wee woteraw Ik'o ik'iyok'o wotts jaalo b́ wotiyal, Krstosnat Ik' mengstotse bano b́ dashawok'o dande'ere.
Keewanotsatse tuutson aleraw ashuwotsats Ik' fayo b́ wetwotse konwor woteraw keewon itn ant'elck'aye.
Mansh aleraw ashuwotsnton ik wotk'ayere,
Yoots it t'alwwotsiye it teshi, andomo doonzok it wotsosh sháán itne mansh sháánon beyiru ashuwotskok'o sha'ore.
Doo jamo, kááwonat ari shuwo b́ daatset shááanokne.
Mansh doonzo geneúshit keewo eeg b́ wotok'o p'ec'ar s'iilere.
Shuu deshaw t'alwi finonton ik wotk'ayere maniyere shááno maants kishde'er kitswere.
T'alwotse beyiru ashuwots ááshon bok'aliru keewo keewonwor dab jiitsike.
Jam keewo shááno maants b́ woor eeg b́ arok'o shiratsne b́ be'eti.
Shiratse be'eyiru jamo shááne, mansh, «Nee tokrirwono tuuwe! k'irtswotsitse galeyar tuuwe! Krstoswere neesh c'eeshitwe» eteere.
Eshe aawk'o it beyirwok'o t'iwintsde'ere dan teleef danetswotsk'owa bako danteleef deshawwotskok'o beek'ayere.
Dúran gond b́ wottsotse itsh imets aawo b́ besheraniyere bín finore.
Mansh doonzo shuno eeg b́ wotok'o t'iwintswere bako dartswotsi wotk'ayere.
T'afiyo maants itn b́ dametwotse woyiniyon dutsets bíron mashk'ayere, maniyere S'ayin Shayiron s'eenere.
Duubonat udon, Shayiri jááwonowere it ats atsewo keewewere, it maac'otse kishde jááwar duwr doonzo udoore.
Jam keewosh no doonzo Iyesus Krstos shútson jam aawo Ik'o Niho udoore.
Krstos mangosha err ititsere iko ikosh alewee.
Máátswotso! doonzo Iyesussh it aleyrwok'o it kenih kenihosh alewere,
Krstos bí ats wotts Ik' mowush took'onat bin kashitwo b́wottsok'o kenihonwere b́ máátsush tooke.
Ik' moow Krstossh bi aleyirwok'o máátswots jam keewon bo kenihosh alewne.
Kenihwotso! Krstos Ik' moowu b́ shuntsok'onat b́ tooko bish beshidek't b́ imtsok'o itwere it máátswotsi shunere,
Krstos han b́ k'al Ik' moow S'ayintsosh geeyatniye, b́ S'ayintswere b́ aap'iweeron aatson mashdek'tniye.
Hank'on kiimo wee shiits aak'o wee han arts k'osh gond keewo biyatse b́ datserawo S'ayinat biyatse eeg eeg deshaw sheeng woshdek'tniye b́ maants b́ t'intsi.
Eshe kenihwots bo tooko boshunirwok'o bo mááts máátso shunne, b́ máátsu shunirwo b́ tooke b́ shuniri.
B́ took atso shit'etwo konwor aaliye, dab Krstos Ik' moosh b́ k'alirwok'o b́ manziti, b́ dugniti.
Noowere Krstos atsi kaywots noone,
«Hank'on asho b́ nihinat bíndn k'ayir b́ máátswats b́ deeshiti, gitetswotswere ik atse bowotiti» eteere.
Ááshts keewanwere eene, hanowere t etir Krstosnat Ik' maats aridek'atniye.
Ernmó keewan itne b́ s'iliri, mansh keniho b́ máátsu b́ tookok'o woshde'er shune, máátsunwere b kenihi mangiwye.
