Ashuwotssh nemo ime Lewi kahaniyo weerone, Lewawino etefanoots kahni weeran s'een woto daatsere wotink'ere Aron kahny naasho b́woterawon Melkes'edik' naash detstso k'osh kahniyo b́woo geyirawnk'ee b́teshi,
kahani fino b́ woneewor nemonwere bínton towaar wonewo geyife.
Jaman b́ jangosh keewets kahniyo k'osh naare, han naarotse konwor wosht'intseyiru t'arap'ezoke t'int fintso aaliye.
No doonz Yhud naar b́ wottsok'o daneke, b́ wotefere Muse kahniwots jango b́ keewor Yhud naaro s'iilt b́ keewtso eegor aaliye.
Keewan ayide sháánr b́datsetiye k'osho Melkes'edik'kok'o kahniyo b́ tuworee,
Bí kahni woti naasho b́ dek', b́kash genzi s'uwoko deshawona bako naaron waats nemonaliye.
«Melkes'edik' kahani b́wottsok'o nee dúre dúrosh kahni neene» et bísh gawere.
Shin eteets tzaziyo nef wotat k'awntsalk b́ wottsotse bín shaark'reree.
Muse nemon ik keewonwor s'een wotofalratse, andmó Ik'ok b́ weeron t'inosh nofalitwo k'antso nojángtso noosh imere.
Haniyere okoon kahniyan Ik'i taaralon wotkaliyee, haniyere shino kahni wottsmanoots taaralone bowoti.
Iyesusmó kahni b́wot Ik'o b́ taartsotsnee, manwere «Doonzo ‹Neehe dúre dúrosh kahni neene› ett taarre, bíasabiyo woneratse» ett b́ jango keewetsok'one.
Taarmanatse tuutson Iyesus taaron kindeets k'antsosh wusho wotere.
K'iratse tuutson kahni iko b́wonerawon b́finatse beyo b́falrawotse shints kahniwots bo taawo aye b́teshi,
Iyesusmó dúre dúrosh beyirwo b́ wottsotse b́ khnetiyo woneratse.
Mansh bo jangosh Ik'o k'onosh dúre dúrosh beyar beetwo wotar b́betwotse b́weeron Ik'o maants weetu jamwotsi b́ jamon kashiyosh falitwe.
Hank'o S'ayino, ik kiimo bíyatse aaltso, s'ayino, morretswotsitse gaaletso, dari aboniyere eents kahniwotsatse naashi k'aabo noosh geyife.
Bí kahni k'oshwotskok'o shino b́ took morrosh, ilowere ash ash morrosh aaw aawon wosho t'intso bísh geyiratse, b́ tooko wosh woshdek't b́ t'intsor han aaniy b́geyirawok'on ishbazree.
Nemo kahniy naash woshdek't b́ naashitswots maaw ashuwotsiye, nemoniyere ili waatso taaron keweetsonmó dúre dúrosh s'een wottso Ik'o naayi naashire.
Eshe bojangatse nokeweyiru keewwotsitse bog keewo haniye, darotse Ik' eeno jori k'ani aaromantse beyirwo hank'o kaheniyi naash k'aabo detsfone.
Bí b́ finit S'ayin beyok arik wotts k'ewoko dunkaniyotse, dunkaniyan b́ k'oons'eyiye ash kishon b́woterawon doonzo kishonee.
Kahni naasho ik ikon b́naashiye imonat woshon b́t'intsitwok'owe, mansh kahniyanwere b́t'intsitwo ik keewo detso bísh geyife.
Nemok'on Ik'osh imetso t'intsit kahniwots bofa'otse bí datsatsa wotink'ere kahniyo woterawnk'e b́teshi,
Kahniyanots bo finirwo dunkani darotse fa'aman ariyonat b́ s'ilal mec'ree, man b́wotwere Muse gofu bí agoor, Ik'o «Guri abaatse neesh b́ be'etsok'on jam keewo t'iwintson finowe» ett bísh b́ keewtsok'onee.
Andmó Iyesus dag taalotse manitso b́ wotts taaro beshts nat taaratse bogonat k'ants jangiyetswotsats need'iyetso b́ wottsotse bísh imets fino boge.
Shin kindeets taaro shapo deshawo wotarr b́datseyink'ere gitlo taareyo geyirawnk'ee b́teshi.
Ik'o bí ash ashaatse shapo b́beyo kitsfetst hank'o etfe, «Hamb, Israe'el ash ashuwotsnat Yihud ash ashuwotsnton Handron notaaret aawo weetwe» etfe Doonzoni.
Taaranwere Gbs'itse bokisho detsdek'at boon tkishoor bo nihotsnton t taaretsok'oyiyaliye, bo taanton bo taaretsats bo kup'erawotse taawere boon aatsni tk'ri etfe Doonzoni.
«Eshe, haniyhakon Israe'el dats ash ashonton T taaret taaro hank'owiye etfe Doonzoni, Taa tnemone bo tookots beezitwe, bo nibotsowere guut'etwe, Bo Ik'onowere wotitwe, Bowere tiashwotsi wotitune.
‹Doonzo dande'e› err k'osh ashosh wotowa bí eshwsh daniyitwo konwor beeratsye, Muk'aatse tuur eenok b́borfetso jametso taan danetwe,
Bonandosh oorowe eteetwe, Bomorronowere haniyak boats taawratse.»
Haniyak «Handr taara» bí etor shints taarman nat woshre etee, mansh nat jamo b́ t'afit aawo t'iinwtsere.
Shin taarets, Ik' ik'iyi fini niwonat datsatsi Ik' Ik'iiyef beyoko detsfe b́teshi
Git k'aat'wotsi detsts dunkaniyu k'andek'rane b́teshi. C'eeshi gedokunat, woshi tusho bíyats b́beef t'arap'ez detsts shints maa kayu «S'ayinoki» eteefuni b teshi.
Gitl magarajiwoniyere jiik'o maantse gitsitsi kayu «S'aynat S'ayintsu» eteefuni.
Dunkani kay gitsitsts hanitse awntson dozets it'ano bíyats s'uwiyeyiru t'arap'ezonat, awntson futets taari taboto biitse fa'ebte b́tesh, taari tabotaniitse mano biitse detsts awntsi mosobiynu, atáát teshts Aron gumbu, nem tatswotsi bí'ats guut'ets gashets shútswots fa'ano boteshi.
Taabotatse fa'a morr t'afitwo bo bangon ipiru mangts Kirubeliwots fa'ano boteshi, ernmó jam keewanots jango and ik ikon keewo falratsonee.
Hank'on jam keewo k'an b́wtsiyakon kahniwots bo fino s'eentsosh dunkany shintsi kayuts uni aawo kinditune.
Gitl gitsitsi k'at'uts kinditwonmó kahniwotsats naashi k'aabo s'uziye, b́ kinditwere worwototse ik aaw s'uziye, bíye b́ took jangonat ash asho dáron b́fiints morrosh b́ t'intsit s'atso desh b́de'aawo kindratse.
Dunkani k'at' shintsu b́ befetsosh S'ayinat S'aynu maants daamet weerindo andoor k'esheerafa'a b́wottsok'owo S'ayin shayiro hank'one b́ kitsiri.
Hanwere and dúro artsoniyee, mank'oon t'iniru imonat woshon t'intsiru asho nibo S'ayintsosh falatsne,
Keewanots handrit aawo b́waafetsosh finats jints úratsi niwwotsiye, boowere móónat úshi jangosh k'osh k'osh mashdek'osh beezets niwwots s'uzsh k'aleknee.
Ernmó Krstos and beyiru sheeng keewwotssh kahniwotsatsi naashi k'aabo wotat be'ere, bí b́kindts dunkaniyu een wotat s'eenuniyee, goofhaan ash kishon finerawnat azeetsaniitsk wotkiyaliye,
S'aynat S'ayinuts iknoto b́ s'atso dek't aani iwisherawok'on b́ kindi bako, eeyishikonat máánzi s'atso dek't kindratse, mank'oon dúre dúrosh noon woritwo noosh b́ daatsiyi.
Eeyishwotsna, manz wur s'atsonat woshosh mis'ts miinzigelu tulo kiimts ashuwotsats fakewoor meets kimatse boon mayde b́ S'ayintsitka wotiyal,
Dúre dúri shayri weeron b́tooko kiimo bíatse aalts wosho woshdek't Ik'osh t'intstso Krstos s'atso beyat beyiru Ik'osh finosh no nibo k'irts finotse aawk'owe iki bogo b́ s'ayintsiti k'úna!
Ekeewots bos'eege Ik'o jangit dúre dúrosh b́ imts rstiyo bodek'etwok'o Krstos handr taari dagotse manitwo wotere, man b́wotwere ash ashuwotsi shin taari shirots wotde bofints morrotse kashiyosh b́k'irtsoshe.
Jeshu kasho b́ beewor jeshu kashirwo b́ k'iro dandek'o geyife,
Jeshuman arikon finats b́ jinet jeshu kashirman b́ k'irihakee, jeshu kashirwo kashon b́ befetsoshmó jeshuman fineratse.
Mank'o b́wottsotse shints taaronúwor dab s'atsalon finats jinatse.
Shin shin Muse b́ ímts nemotse fa'a tzaziwotsi ash jamosh keewre, maniyere hakon máánzonat eyishi s'atso aatsonton dek't nemi mas'aafonat ash jamono, hisop'i mit maaronat mereeri biri s'iron b́faki,
B́ fakwere «Ik'o itsh b́ azazts taaritsi s'atso haniye.» ettniye.
Mank'o dunkaniwotsnat, boon kis'kesheyiru k'ac' jamats s'atso fakeree.
Arikonoor Muse nemok'on muk' keewwotsiyere okoon jam keewo s'atsone b́ S'ayineti, s'atso b́kuud'erawonowere morratse S'ayino daatseratse.
Eshe darotsi keew hanotsi ariyets wotts jamanots hannk'o niwron s'ayino boosh geyitwe b́teshi, darotsik wotts keewwotswor botookon haniyere bogts woshon s'ayino boosh geyife.
Krstos arik «Ik' maa S'ayinun» ariyeek wottsunat ash kishon finets S'ayinu beyokuk kindratse, bí b́tookon and nojangosh Ik'o shinatse be'ewosh darots kindre.
Ayhudi kahniwotsats naashi k'aabo b́ tooki s'ats woterawo s'atso dek't worwot worwoton S'aynat S'ayintsuts b́kindfoni, Krstosmó b́ tooko ayoto woshok'o k'alde t'intsosh kindratse.
Mank'o b́wotink'ere datso bíazeewortson ayoto gond bek'o dek'osh bísh geyiyank'ee b́teshi, and dúri s'uwaatse morro k'aaúbazosh b́ tooko wosho woshdek't iknoto iwishirawok'on be'ere.
Ashosh iknoto k'iro beezk'rere, k'ironiyere okonowere bí ats angshetwe.
Mank'owere Krstos aywots morro k'aaúbazosh iknoto shukeere, aaninwere morro kurosh b́woterawo bín kotirwotsi kashiwosh gitlo be'etwe.
Nemo shinomaantsi weyiru sheeng keew ara (c'isha) b́ teshi bako b́tookon arikeewaliye b́teshi, mansh worwot worwoton jam aawo bo shukeet woshwotsi de'er Ik'ok t'iinet ashuwots s'een woshosh b́jamon falratse.
Nemo boon s'ayintsk'ro falituwe wotink'ere Ik'o mangiyosh t'iinet ashuwots jango, morrotse bos'ayintsotsnat morr deshawok'on bogitsotse boosh b́danetwotse wosh t'intso k'ayk'riyank'onee b́teshi.
Woshmanotsmó dúre dúr morro bín bogaawitwotsiye.
Minz wurwotsnat eyishuwots s'atso morro k'aaúbazo falratse.
Mansh Krstos datsumaanats b́ woor hank'o etre, «Woshonat imo geeratsne, Atsonmó taash k'anirnee,
Mis'et woshonat Morr t'afiyosh shukeet woshon Geneeúweratsne,
Taa manoor, ‹Ik'o Izar Izewero! mas'aafotse t jangosh guut'etsok'on ni alo s'eentsosh waare› » ti eti.
Bíwere shin ekeewots nemok'on kúúh keweekno bowotiyalor «Woshonat imon, mis'et woshonat morri k'awntso oorowe etosh shukeyiru wosho geeratsne, manotsnowere gene'úweratsne» bí eti,
Aaninwere, «Hamb, taa n shuntso s'eentsosh waare» bíeti, mank'oon gitlo man naari wosho beyok b́shato shegrshosh shintsi naar wotts wosho k'aaúbazre.
Mannowere «n shuna» etiru keewok'on Iyesus Krstos meetson iknoto aaniy b́ iwishirawok'on wosho wotat b́ t'intsotse s'ayinronee.
Kahniyo ik ikon morro k'aaúbazo falraw woshmanotsi uni aawo t'intsfetst aaw aawo need'dek'tni b́finefoni.
Krstosmó jam aawosh wotit wosh ikman b́t'intsiyakon Ik'o niho k'aniaaromaants beewtsere.
Haniyakon bín shit'irwots bí ali shirots bowotefetsoshe b́kotiri,
Manb́wotwere S'ayintsmanotsnowere wosh ikatse tuutson dúre dúrosh s'eenwotsi b́woshtsotsnee.
S'ayin shayironwere keewan jango noosh gawitwe, shin shinonowere,
«Aawu manotsiyere il Bonton t taaret taaro haniye etfe doonzoni, T nemone it nibots beezitwe, bo tookotsowere guut'etuwe.»
Manats dabtnwere «Bo fints gond finonat morron haniyere hakon gawratse» etfe.
Mansha morr jamo oorowe etehakon morr s'ayintsosh t'intset wosho haniyere okoon t'intso geyiratse.
Eshnee, ti eshwotso! Iyesus s'atsatse tuutsona jamoniyere bogts S'ayints Ik' moots kindosh nonfaliyt agito daatsdek'rone,
Nokinditwere b́ magarajiyon, etonwere b́ meetsatse tuutson noosh b́ k'eshts handronat kashomaants jiishts weerone.
Ik'i mootse al detsts kahni eeno detsfone.
Mansh eshe nogitso gond gawoniyere b́ s'ayinetwok'o nonibats fakde'er, no atsonowere s'ayin aatson mashde'er, nib s'ayinonat arik wotts imnetiyo deshde'er Ik'ok t'iinone.
Jangiyets keewo noosh imtso amanek b́ wottsotse jangat nokeewirwo jangiyetsatse hake baka noerawon kup'shde deshde'one.
Shunoonat sheeng keewon k'ande'er nobetwok'o iko ikosh gawiwe,
jam aawo gonkeyaar no atsatsewo kup'shwoone bako, ik ikwots bok'alfok'o nokakwewo k'azk'ayonee, ikinwor, doonzo weyi aawo b́ karntsok'o gawde'e iki bogshde'er k'aluworee.
Ariko dan nodek'iyakon danfetsr morro nofiniyal haniyere okoon morrosh t'iinet wosho b́jamon aaliye.
And ooritwonmó shinomaantsi wotitwo shatits angshonat k'efirwotsi mitsit shatits taawoniye.
Muse gedts nemó titsetwats, git ash wee keez ashuwots bíats bogawitka wotiyal maac' k'ewalo b́k'iritwok'o wotowe.
Eshe, Ik'o naayi gac'tso, bín b́s'ayints taaron waats s'atso k'awntsalk woshtso, s'aati shayiro c'ashtso, aawk'o bog fayeek'úna bísh wotiti arefa itsha?
«Weer weersho tikee, taaye wotit k'awntso dashetwe» ettso koni b́wottsok'o danfone, mank'o, «Doonzo bí ashuwotsats angshitwe».
Beyat beyiru Ik'o kishats diho ayide'er shatitkee.
Shááno itsh b́shaniyakon ay gondo bek'aat bojangosh it k'amts manotsi bali aawwotsi gawwore.
K'atsoor ash shinatse c'asheertee, gondonowere bek'rte, k'atsoorowere man naari gondbek'o boats b́bodts ashuwotsnton tooh itwottsotse gondo bek'rte.
It tipetswotssh maac'o k'ewerte, k'antsonat uni aawosh beet gaalo itdetstsok'o itdantsosh it detstso itatse dek'eworowere k'amdek'at man genee'uwon dek'rtee.
Eshe een shilmatiyo bín itdaatsitwo bíyats it amantsman juuk'ayere.
Ik'i ettso s'eentsr Ik'o itsh imosh b́ taarts keewo daatsosh k'amar kordek'o itsh geyife.
Mansh eshe, hank'o ett guut'ere, «Weetuman muk' gizewoniyere okoon weetwe, ja'aratse,
Tik wottso kááw ashonmó amanon kasho daatsituwe, Shuutso maants bí aaniyalmó taa bíatse tuutson, Geneeúweratse.»
Noomó amanar kash datsituwots jirwots noona bako shuuts aanar t'afitwots jirwots noonaliye.
Amana etoni, jangat koteyiru keewo «Ee arikon wotitwe» err dek'ee, ááwosh be'eraw keewonowere b́ be'eyirwok'o woshde'er taawe.
Shin ashuwotsi udeyiye bo amantsatse tuutsone.
Datso bí azee Ik'on b́ wottsok'o t'iwintsdek'o nofalit amanone. Mansh be'eyiru keew jamo be'erawatse b́ finootsk'owo danfone.
Abeel k'aayeliyere bogts wosho Ik'osh b́ t'ints b́ amantsoshe, Ik'o Abeel imtso b́ dek'or Abeel b́ imnetiyon kááw b́ wotok'o gawere, Abeel b́ k'iriyaloru b́ imnetiyon andoor keewirwe.
Henok k'iro bi'ats b́borawok'o dambaan bín k'aaúdek'e b́ imnetiyoshe, Ik'o bín k'aaúb́dek'tsotse daatseratse, bín k'aaúdek'ewoniyere shinoor Ik'o b́gene'úshtsok'o bísh gawere.
Amanerawon Ik'i geneúsho faleratse, Ik'ok t'iinet asho Ik'o b́beyonat bín geyiru ashuwotsshowe k'awntso bimetwok'o amano bísh geyitwe.
Noh manoori ááwon be'eraw keewwotsatse atso korbodek'etuwok'o Ik'o b́ keewor Ik'o shatt b́ meyitsi ashuwotsi woriyosh markabo b́ dooz b́ amantsoshe, Noh imnetiyonowere datso morretsi bwoto dant datswats bí angshi, Nohuwere amanon daatset kááw woto b́ naati.
Abraham keer, bísh risti woshde'er b́ dek'et beyokok bí ametuwok'o bín s'eegeyor bí ametuwoko dab b́dariyalor amoosh bíazaze amanatniye.
Jangiyets keewo bínton naatetwotsi wottswots Yisak'nat Yak'obnton jangiyets datswatse ash datsi ash wotat gofootse b́bee imnetiyone.
Man b́k'alwere b need'oko kup' wottsu, Ik'o ay dúrosh gaw dek't bí agts kitu b́ kotirwotsnee.
Sarash jangits Ik'o amanek b́wottsok'o bdantsotse na'a shuwo bish beshtsunat Abraham ayidek't gawero b́wotyalor na'o bodaatsitwok'o ango bdaats imnetiyone.
Mansh Abraham k'irts ashok'o taawets ikatse daritsi k'eenok'onat aatsi gúúratsi shiyok'o taaweraw naaro b́datseyi.
Jametsanots boamantsok'one bok'iri, Ik'o boosh imosh b́ jangits keew jamo daatsratsne, ernmó wokoon s'iilt bo daatsdek'tsok'o woshdek't genee'uwon k'aaúbodek'i. Datsatsnowere ibonat ash datsi ashok'o bowotonowere t'iwints bodek'i.
Hank'o keewiru ashuwots bo took datso wottso kotiruwotskok'owa shanidek't bokitsiri.
Bítse bokeshts datsman gawrno wotink'ere b́maants aniyank'nee b́ teshi.
Andmó iki bogtso, darotse fa'a datso miraac'irunee, mansh Ik'o kito boosh b́ k'anitsotse «Noko Izar Izeweri» err bín bos'eegal bín jitsiratse.
Abrahami fadewor Yisahak'i woshok'o woshdek't b́ t'ints imnetiyone, bísh jangiyets aap'o dek'tso Abraham b́ na'a iks'uzo shukoshe b́teshi,
Beree Ik'o, «Yisak'n n naaro neesh s'eegetwe» ettniye b́teshi.
Ik'o k'irotse tuuzo b́ falituwok'o Abraham bí amantsosh arikon k'irotse b́ tuutsok'o woshdek't Yisahak'i aaniy daatsb́dek'i.
Yisak' shinomaants wotit keewo gawudek't Yak'obnat Esawn imnetiyone b́ deeri.
Yak'ob k'irosh b́ t'intsok'on Yosef nana'úwotsi ik ikon deert b́ gumbi c'uushats te'edek't Ik'osh b́sagad imnetiyone.
Yosef k'irob́t'intsok'on Isra'el ashuwots Gbs'itse bokeshetwok'o b́ keew b́ mak'tsonowere awuk'o bok'alitwok'o boosh tzaziyo bí'im amanatniye.
Muse b́ shweetsok'on b́ indunat b́ nihn azsheeng b́ woto bobek'tsosh Nugúso tzaziyo bosharawo keez shashosh boáats imnetiyone.
Musewor bí eeniyakon «Fer'on na'i na'a» err s'eegeyo b́k'az imnetiyone.
Mansha manorush morron daatset genee'oniyere Ik'i ashuwotsnton gondbek'o daatso b́ marat'i.
Shino maantsowere b́ daatsit k'awntso b́ bek'tsotse Gbs' galoniyere Krstos jangosh gac'eyo bog b́ wottsok'o gaw b́dek'i.
Nugúso fayonowere b́sharawo Gbs'itse b́ kesh amanone, ááwon bek'erawo Izar Izewernowere b́ bek'tsok'o wosht b́ weeratse b́ kúp'i.
K'aab na'o úd'osh azazets Ik'i melakiyo Israe'el dats ashuwots k'aab na'o b́ úd'rawok'owa ett Fazigonat s'ats faki nemo b́k'al imnetiyone.
Israe'el dats ashuwots dats shuuk'atse kimírwok'o aats k'ar birotse bokim bo amnanoshe, Gbs' ashuwotsmó mank'o k'alosh botuwor bo jametsuwots aats limniye bowtsi.
Israe'el ashuwots Iyariko shútsi kas'o imnetiyon shawat aawo boguurtsosh shútsi kas'uwots gahbowtsi.
Widetsu Ra'ab dats k'oroor amtswotsi jeenon b́ dek'tsosh azazerawwotsnton k'ironiyere b oor imnetiyone.
Eshe k'osho aawne tkeewiti? Gediwon jangemo, Barak' jangemo, Samsom jangemó, Yoftahekemó, Daawitko, Samu'el jangemó, nebiyiyiwots jango t keewrawok'o gizeyo taash bk'awneti,
Bo bo imnetiyon mengstwotsi da'arnee, kááwonowere k'eezrnee, boosh jangiyetsonowere daatsrne, ééshwots nonónowere bo is'i.
Tawi angonowere takrnee, shiki shashatsnowere keshernee, nef wototse kesht kup' wotomaants bo woneyi, kes'oonowere kup'wotsi woternee, kec'r da'af t'alati kes'i ashuwotsi bogishi,
Máátswots bo jag k'irtswotsi k'irotse botuure daats bodek'i. K'oshwotswere bogts k'irotse tuwo daatsosh gawt k'osh k'osh onó bobek'etwok'o k'alewor bo tipotse kesho geeratsne.
K'oshwotswere boats kashetswotsi wotat bojot'eyi, k'oshuwots bo tufo muk'on tpeyat tipi moots juweerne,
Shútson botogeyi, magaaziyon bo kap'eyi, shikon boúd'eyi, mereeronat eyishi gok'o tahdek't bo jawri, t'owwotsnat giishets ashuwotsi wotat bo shambi.
Worwotse, guratse, datsats gitsotse fa'a gop'onat oorotsa guurat bo beyi. Mank'owono datsu boosh wotiitk beyoko wotat daatseratsane.
Jamanotswere bo imntiyon boosh gawetso bowotiyaloru boosh jangiyetso daatsde'afa'ane.
Ik'o noosh k'ants keewo k'ani b́k'rtsotse, mansha bo nontoni bako boaal s'eenwotsi woto falatsne.
Daawnok'o noon gúúrts gaw jamanotsi no detstsotse no'ats kur wotts keew jamwotsi no'ats deshts morro k'a'úbayr no shinatse beyiru nohewo k'amde kup'ar woc'one.
Nowos'etwere no imnetiyo ned'itsonat s'eentstso Iyesus ats no ááwo gerdeniye, bíwere b́ shinatse need'wtsts geneúwatse tuutson jitatse k'irr gac'ewo eegok'oor b́ taawrawo jitatse gondbek'on k'iro k'amb́dek'i, Ik' be jooroke k'ano maants be b́wtsi.
Eshe taahr, maac'o it k'ut'rawok'o morretswots bín bo k'eefere k'amdek'tso Iyesusi s'ilde'ere.
It morronton mak'orewoke s'ats kud'efetsosh b́borfetso k'eferafa'tee.
Ik'o b́ nana'ikok'o woshdek't itango kup'shosh hank'o bí ettso batk'rerte, «T naayo! doonzo sezo ketik'aye, b́ hadoshowere maac'o k'ut'k'aye,
Doonzo b́ shuntsoniye b́ sezfoni, B́ nayik'owosh dekt b́s'iliruwono b́fayefoni.»
Ik'o b́ nanaúwotsk'o itn b́tawtsotse b́ sezo k'amoore, b́ niho bín b́ sezraw na'o kone?
Nana'a wotts jamwots bo daatsiru sezo it were daatso it k'azal dik'al itna boko nana'a itnaliye.
Haniyere okoon, noúnetsi sezf meetsi nihwots detsfone b́teshi, bonowere mangiye nomangifoni, bere kashon beyosh kashi weeron nih wottsosh iki bogshde azazewo aawk'oneya noosh geyiwo b́k'azeti!
Bosh sheengo araat b́ be'etsok'on muk' gizewush noon sezrne, bímo b́ S'ayino kayitwotsi nowotish sheengosh noon sezfe.
Sez jamo manorish shiyanitka bako geneúshitk areratse, ilomo man dandek'ts ashuwotssh jeenon s'eentso kááw fini shwo boosh daatsituwe.
Mansh it kish neftswotsnat itgubr maawtswotsi kup'ide'ere.
Doklirwo b́ kashitwok'owa bako b́ beyoke keer b́ tisherawok'o, it tufooshowere weerindi kááwo woshde'ere.
S'ayn woteraniye konworu doonzo bek'osh b́ falawotse, ash jamonton jeenon bewore, S'ayinon beyoshowere kup'owere,
Ititsere konshoru Ik' s'aato b́ shaprawok'o it atso korde'ere, mank'owere s'aam shuu iko shuwit s'ap'o ititse boc'r iti b́ kic'irawok'o, aywotsno b́ kimshrawok'o korde'ere.
Gusiyetso wee iknoti móósha ett b́ took k'aabo kemtso Esawkok'o shayri ash woterawo ititsere b́ daatserawok'o it atso korde'ere.
Esaw il s'aato aaniy dek'osh b́ geyor s'aatman bísh baziyetsok'o danfte, b́k'altso woniyosh kup'dek't eepfetst b́geyiyalor weero daatso falratse.
Kishon shuu'etwok wee mis'etuo Sin gurok borafa'ate, bamplomants, shatits t'alwots, eegurahi jongokowere,
Ezbedi k'arokowere wee keeweyiru aap'o b́ shishetwoko borafa'ate, aap'ets keewman shishts ashuwots «Eshe bodre haniyak k'osho noosh aap'ek'aye» et bok'onfetso bodrnee.
«Gizo dab gurman b́ t'awiyal Shútson togeyar k'irwee» Etiru tzaziyo boats b́mangtsosh bín kuro falratsne.
Manoke bek'ets keewman eenonat shatiik b́teshtsotse dab́ Muse woor «Taa shataat, k'ewere» bí et.
Itiyelee S'iyon guromants t'inwtsertee, bihe kashetso Ik'o kito wotts daritstsu Iyerusalemiye, genee'úwon kakwedek'tswotsok, ay kumon taawet mlakiwotsok t'inrte,
Bo shúútso darots guut'etswotsok, k'aab nana'a wotts amantsuwots ko'eetsok, kááw angshitu Izar izewerokonat s'ayin wotat daatsts shayirwotsok t'inrte.
Handr taareyosh dag taalotse manik wottso Iyesusnat Abeel s'atsoniyere k'antso keewiru fakets s'atsookowere t'inrte.
Keewirman de'atsone it erawok'o itatso korde'ere, Ekeewots Ik'o ashon datsatse boosh b́ keewre k'ewatsone ettswots b́shirotse kesho bomaawiyakon, bére noo darotse noosh keewirwo dek'onok'azal awuk'o kalrniya b́ kishotse kesho nofaliti!
Manoor bí aap'o datso shek'ere, «andmó datsu mec'ro b́woterawo aani dabr darono dabde'er shek'ituwe» eton keewure.
Han «Iknoto dabr,» etiru keewoniye b́ kitsiriyee shek'eraw keewwots kup'arr bobetuwok'o shek'eyirwots wee azeets keewwots bobeyoke botuwitok'oniye.
Eshe noo shek'eraw mengstu nonaatetwotse Ik'o udoonee, b́ gene'úwitwok'oon mangiyonat shatoon bísh finone.
No Ik'o Izar Izewer mitsit tawok'oyiye.
Jam aawo it ats atsewo eshwi shunon shunewere,
Ibo de'er ibiyo batk'ayere, mank'oon ibuwotsi dek't ibiyoke ik ik ashuwots bodananiyere melakiwotsi dek't ibiyirne.
Bonton tohar it tipetsok'o woshder tipetswotsi gawwere, it were bokok'o gondo it bek'irwok'o woshder gond bek'irwotsi gawwere.
De'ewo jamokere mangiyek wotowe, widetswotsnat gobetswotsats Ik'o b́ angshitwotse kenihonat máátsun amank woto shapiir bo de'ewo kimsh k'ayine.
Gizi shunatse wokoore, it detstso itsh boree, Ik'o «Taahe b́ jamon neen juweratse, b́ jamon neen k'ayaatse» etre.
Manshowere amande'er, Taan tep'etwo doonzoniye, sharaatse, Asho taan eeg k'alosheb́ faliti? No eteti.
Ik' aap'o shin shino itsh keewts itn jishirwotsi batk'ayere, bo beyonat bo fini shuwo gawr bo imneti jafro sha'owere.
Iyesus Krstos ootsowere haambetsowere dúredúrosh bíne, wonawoneratse.
Daneraw k'osh k'osh naari danosh kisho imk'ayere, nonibo máá nemwotsi kotosh b́ woterawon s'aatats b́kup'ink'ere sheenge, mishi nem han shoyts ashuwots eegor boosh k'alratse.
Noo wosh t'iintsef t'arap'ezo detsfone, b́ woteferor dunkaniwtse finef kahniwots wosh t'intseyiru t'ar'p'ezoke fa'a misho k'aaúde'er bomarawok'o baziyeke.
Manwere eegoshe ayhudiyi kahniwotsats naashi k'aabo morrosh oorowe eto datseetwo gizi s'atso de'er jam beyokoniyere bog S'aynts beyokuk b́ kinditi, gizi dunmanó gáloniyere úratsne b́ mis'eti.
Mank'owere Iyesus ash asho b́ took s'atson S'ayntsosh kiti fengeshoniyere úratse gondo bek'o b́dek'i.
Noowere gálotse keer b́ maants amone, b́ ketts ketonowere kaydek'tswotsi wotoone.
Noo haniyak weet kituni nokotiri bako kup'ar need'it kitu datsanatse deshatsone.
Haniyako Iyesusn udi wosho uniaawo Ik'osh t'intswonee, hanwere b́ shútsosh gawiru nooni k'indwotsn t'iinet udi woshoniye.
Sheeng keewo k'alonat it detsts keewo jamwotssh kayiyo batk'ayere, Ik'o geneúshitwoniye hank'o wotts woshoniye.
Itn jishirwotssh alewere, bo ali shirots wotoore, boon aatet keewo (halafinet) b́beyrwotse it kashi jangosh kup'at bofiiniri, it boosh it azazeyink'ere bo bofino genee'úwon finiyank'nee, mank'o wotob́k'azalmó bo fino shiyanone bofinti, manwere itsh k'auntsalko b́ wotiti.
Noosh Ik'o k'onwore, nib s'ayino nodetstsok'o arikee, jam weeron sheeng doyonon beyosh tewnirwone.
Dabnwor kup'arr Ik'o itk'onitwok'oye itn kup'idek'at tk'oniri itok tiaanitwok'oye.
Mererwotsi jintso nodoonz Iyesusi dúre dúri taareyi s'atson k'irotse tuuztso Ik'o Izar Izewer jeenika
B́ shuntso k'alosh it bodetwok'o sheeng keew jamon itn editwee, geneúshitwonowere Iyesus Krstos weeron noon woshwe. Iyesus Krstossh dúre dúron mango wotowe, amen.
Ti eshwotso, itsh t guut'ts wosho k'awun b́ wottsosh ti izts keewan k'amde'er itdek'etwok'owe ayidek'at itn tk'oniri.
No eshu T'imotiwos tipi mootse b́ keshtsok'o it danetwok'o shunfee, kááwon han maants b́ weetka wotiyal bínton it maants waar iti s'iiletwe.
Iti jishirwotsnat S'ayin jamwotssh t jamo t'intswere, It'aaliyani datson waat hanoke fa'a krstiyanwots jamo itsh t'iintsrnee.
S'aato it jametsnton wotowe. Amen!
Dats jamats bad'ts tatse git jirwotssh Ik'onat doonzo Iyesus Krstos guutso wottso Yak'oboke wosheets jamó, jeno itsh wotowe.
Ti eshuwotso! k'osh k'osh naari fadewo itats b́bodor geenúshit keewwotsi it daatstsok'o woshde'er taawwere.
It imnetiyo b́fadewo k'amo itsh daatsituwo b́wottsok'owo dandek'etute.
K'amonowere it kup'o ik jago itsh b́shaprawo s'eenonat itn bodtswotsi woshituwo wotowe.
Ititse dani teleefo bísh b́shapts asho fa'e wotiyal Ik'o k'onuwe, Ik'onwere bísh imetwe, bí jametsosh shiitso bí aa'awo tewudi doon imetwo Izar Izeweriye.
Ernmó asho eegonor gito b́gímberawo amande'er k'onuwe, git gimbiru asho jongon gifniyeyat giwwtsts aatsk'aroniye bíariye.
Mannaari asho doonzoke ik jago b́daatsituwok'o bísh ark'aye.
Han b́wotituwere git níbo detst b́weerindatse hake baka bíetiruwoshe.
B́ beewon dashan wotts eshuwo Ik'o damban bín b́ detsetwosh geneúwowe,
Ash gaalo bodi fuundok'o b́ ooshetuowotse b́ beewon dambaan wotts eshuwo Ik'o b́bewo dashan b́woshiyalor gene'úwowe,
Aawo b́ k'ees'onton b́keshor bodo shuuk'iniye b́k'riti, b́ fúndonuwere ooyniye b́wutsiti, bíazisheengonwere t'afniye b́wutsiti, mank'owere gaalets asho b́fiinon b́jaakfere t'afniye b́wutsiti.
Doonzo b́ taartsok'on bín shuntswotssh b́ imet kashi akililiyo b́ dek'etuwosh fadeyo k'amar kúp'it asho deereke.
Ik'o gond keewon noon b́ fadrawotse mank'o bíwere konnoru b́ fadrawotse asho b́ fadeyor «Ik'o taan fadre» etk'aye.
Ernmó asho ik ikon b́ fadeyir b́ took tewnon geetseyar bí ant'elcewore.
Haniyhakon tewunu bmaac'or morro shuwitwaniye. Morronu s'eenon bi eeniyakon k'iro shuwituwane.
Shuneets eshuwwotso! it ant'elcherawok'owa!
Sheengts imonat s'een wotts deer jamo Ik'okne, han b́weetuwe c'ishok'o wona wonewo deshaw shááni niho Ik'okne.
Ik'o bí azts jam shintswotsitse gawdek't ari aap'on noon shuure.
Shuneets eshuwotso! han batk'ayere, ash jamo k'ebosh káártso, noonkeewonat fayosh mango wotowe.
Ash fayo Ik'i kááwo daatsiratse.
Hansha kiimonat weerigondi ayonowere ok k'aúbayr Ik'o it nibots b́ toktsonat it kasho kashiyo falitu aap'man it tooko dashan detson de'ere.
Ik'i aap'tso finats jiitswere bako it tooko dashfetsr shish mec'ro shishfwotsi wotk'ayere.
Ik' aap'ts aap'o finats jiitsraw asho bín bíazeets shiitso mastayiton bek'iru ashok'oyiye,
Ashaan b́shiitso mastyiton b́s'iliyakon ametuwe, awuk'o b́wottsok'owo manoor batni b́k'riti.
Wotowa eree nas' kishit b́ nemo sheengshr s'iilr bín kup'ituwo bínowere shiir baterawo, finats jitsitu asho b́ finon deereke b́ wotiti.
Bí albero korde'aniyere Ik'o Ik'irwe eteet asho b́ tookoniye b́ dashiri, b́ ik'iyonwere k'awuntso deshatse.
Ik'o niho shinatse s'ayinonat kimaw hayimanotiyo, nihonat indo k'irts nanaúwotssh, aaninu bokenih k'irts máátsuwotssh bo kic'or boon tep'o, b́ tookonowere datsanatsi kimatse kordek'oniye.
Tieshuwotso! mangts doonzo Iyesus Krstosn amaniruwotsitna wotiyal iko ikoniyere bogfe eton asho bogabogshk'ayere.
Git ashuwots it kakuweyiru bewokok weetune, iko b́kishi jabots awntsi k'ubelo geddek'tsonat tah sheengo tah dek'tso gaaletska, k'osho kiimts tahidoro tahts tugretska,
Sheengiru tah tahdek'ts asho mangiyon «Sheeng beyokanats bede'e» it eteti. Tugretsonmó «Neyere manoke need'owe, wee ttufishiroots bede'e» it eteti,
Eshe, mank'oon it dagotse k'osh k'oshewonat bogabogshr angisho it angshituwok'o itsh be'eratsa?
Shuneets eshuwotso! k'ewere, Ik'o amanon galetswotsi bo wotitwok'onat bín shuntswotssho b́ jangits mengsto bo naatetwok'o datsanatsi tugretswotsi marat'de'atsa?
Itmó tugretswotsiye it gac'iri, itn dadaat angshi moo maants iti geetsirwots gaaletswotsiyoshna?
It bín it s'eegeyiru sheeng shúútso c'ashiruwots bonoshna?
«K'osh asho ntookok'o woshde'er shune» et S'ayin mas'aafotse guut'etso Ik'i mengestitsi nemo it s'eentsiyal sheenge it finiri.
Ash dago it boga bogshiyalmó morre it finiri, nemo it beshiruwotse iti k'oretute.
Asho tzaziwotsitsere iko gaahr oorts jamwotsi b́ s'eentsiyal dab jamwotsi b́ gaktsok'owe taaweti.
«Wido amk'aye» etts doonzo mank'o «Ud'k'aye» etre, mansh wido amo nk'azal dab n ud'iyal nemo gaakrne.
S'ayin kishit nemoke angsho dek'osh fa'a ashuwotskok'o keewwere, mank'owere k'aluwere.
Ik' angsho maarraw ashuwotssh mhreti woshratse, b́ wotefere mhretiyo angsho daa'ituwe.
T eshúwotso! asho imnetiyo detsfe bí etal, ando aani b́ imnetiyo sheeng finon kitso b́ k'azal eebi bísh b́ k'aliti? B́ imnetiyo bín kashiyosh falituwa?
Bo tahituwonat bo meetuwo deshaw eeshuwotsnat mishúwotsn bobeyal,
ititsere iko bo beyosh geyit keewo imaniyere «Jeenon ameree! itsh k'ec'ee! woorwere!» bí etal eebi boosh b́ k'aliti?
Mank'o sheeng fin deshaw imnetiyo k'irkee.
Ernmó «Nee imnetiyo detsfne, taawere sheeg fino detsfe» etetuwo b́ beyal, «N imnetiyo finalo taash kitsuwe, taawere t finon t imnetiyo kitsituwe» etetuwe.
Nee «Ik Ik'o fa'ee» etaat amanirune, sheenge, amanonere Fo'erawwotswor amanirune, shatonowere k'ewirune.
Nee dartsano! imnetiyo finalo k'awuntso b́ deshawok'o danosh geefiya?

It dagotse fa'a kes'onat fayon awuke waake? It atsotse kaariru it meetsi tewunaatsnosha?
Ik keewo daatsosh tewunirute, ernmó daatsatste, asho úd'irute okoorirute eree daatsatste, fayeyirute, koyeyirute. Ik'o it k'onraawotsnowere it geyiru keewo daatsatste.

Sheeng keewo k'alosh it kúp'iyal gondo itats betsitwo kone?

Ik' shunotso b́ wotiyal it gond fino finar gondo itbek'oniyere sheeng keewo finar gondo it bek'o k'anefe.
Krstos b́ tookon Ik'o maants iti t'intsosh bí kááw wotefetst kááw woterawwotssh morratse tuutson aani iwisherawok'on iknoto gondo bek't k'irre, bí meetson k'irre, shayironomó beyar beetke b́ woshi.
Shayir mannowere tipi mootse beyiru kashuwotsok amt dooshishiyo b́ nabi.
Tipi mootse beyiru shayr shayirwots yoots Noh dúr markabo b́ dozor Ik'o boon k'amoon b́ kotfere aleratsone ettswotsiye. Markabmanits kindt aatsotse kashtswots botaawo shmt ash wotts múk' ashuwots s'uziye.
Atsanwere and itn kashitu gupon ariyetsoniye, gupanu atsatsi kiimo bazosh b́ woterawo s'ayin maac'o daatsosh Ik'o maants t'iinet k'ononiye, itn b́ kashitwere Iyesus Krstos k'irotse b́ tuutsi weerone,
Bí daro maants amt Ik'o k'anokee, melakiwotsnat alirwots, angwotswor, bísh keewernee.
Krstos b́meetson gond bek'o b́ datstsosh itwere kes'i taho taahadek'ts ashok'o hasabiyanats k'up'ar k'ande'ere, b́meetson gond bek'o dek'ts asho morro fino need'ik'rere.
Haniyakon eshe oorts datsatsi it beyon meetsi gond tewno s'eentson b́ woterawo Ik'i shuntsok'on beewere.
Ik' ash woterawwots bo k'alfok'o shiraatse jintsi woton, gusiyon, máshon, werali gáálon, weralo úyide'er duubonat wic'ik wotts dozets ik'uwotsi ik'iyon it beshits dúro bodfe.
Andomó keewann weralo bonton ik woton beshiyo it k'aztsosh bo adiri, bo c'ashiri.
Ernmó kashon fa'úwotsnat k'irtswotsats angshosh k'andek'tso shinatse aatetúne.

Mank'o it naashi shirotse beyirwotsi fiic'de'er kéwon b́ woterawo Ik' giz s'enwotssh sheeng ariyo kitson wotowe.

Itn dariyiru ashuwotsatse tuutsone han t guut'i,
Krstosoke itdek'ts shayiri S'ayno ititse b́ beyrwosh k'oshodanitwo itsh geyiratse, bíwere jam keewo itsh danituwe, itsh b́ danitwonu ara bako kootaliye mansh shayiri S'ayno itn b́ danitsok'on Krstoston wotde'er beewere,.
Eshe t nana'otso! bí b́be'ewor nosharaniyere aawo shu'úde'er bín nobek'etwok'onat bí b́weet aawots b́ shinatse nojitserawok'o bíń beewere,,
Bíwere kááwo b́wotok'o it daniyakon, kááw finiru jamo Ik'oke shuwek b́ wottsok'o dande'ere.
Ik' nana'uwotsi erŕ nos'eegeetwok'o niho awuk'o shuno noosh b́imtsok'o aab́ s'iilere! arikon noowere Ik' nana'a noone, datsan Ik'o b́dartsosh nonowere danatse.
T shuntswotso! and no Ik' nana'a noone, shinomaantsish eeg nowotitwok'o daneerafa'ee, ernmó Krstos b́be'et aawots bí aro arikon eeg bíarok'o nobek'etwotse bínowere noaritwok'ó danfone.
Krstosn man b́ wotitwok'o jangiru jamo Krstos s'ayn b́ wottsok'o bíwere b́ tooko s'ayn woshituwe.
Morra eto Ik' nemo gaak b́ wottsotse morr finit jamo Ik' nemo gáákre.
Ashuwots morro t'afiyosh Krstos b́be'etsok'onat bíwere morro b́ deshawok'o danfte.
Eshe Krstosnton beet ash jamo morro fineratse. Morr finitu asho Krstosi be'atse, bínowere danatse.
T nana'uwotso! konworu itn bí ant'elcerawok'owa, Krstos kááwo b́ wottsok'o kááwts fino k'alitu jamo kááwe.
Diyablos shintson dek'tut morro b́ finirwosh morr finiru ash jamo Diyablos jiire. Ik' na'o b́ be'e diyablos fino gakoshee.
Ik'i doyo b́gitsotse b́beyirwotsnat Ik'atse b́shuwetsotse Ik'i na'a wottso morro fineratse, finoshowere falratse.
Ik' nana'onat Diyablos nana'on galde danet hanne, Kááw finerawonat bí eshuwi shunaw jamonúwots Ik' nana'analiye.
Shin shintson it k'ebts wosho «No atsatsewo shunewone» etirwoniye.
Shed'ani jir teshtsonat bíeshuwi úd'tso K'ayelkok'o woto geyiratse, bí bíeshuwi eegishe b́ úd'i? B́ fino gond b́ teshtsotsnat bí eshu fino kááw b́ teshtsotsne.
Ti eshuwotso! datsatsi ashuwots iti boshit'al mansh adk'ayere.
Noo no eshuwotsi noshunirwotse k'iromaantse kashomaants k'az nokimtsok'o danfone. Shun deshaw asho k'iri c'ishotse b́beyri.
Bíeshuwi shit'iru jamo kash úd'kee, kash úd'tsonmó dúredúri kasho b́daatsrawok'o danfte.
Shuno eeg b́wottsok'o nodanet Iyesus Krstos b́ kasho noosh b́imtsoshe, noowere nokasho no eshuwotssh beshide imo noosh geyife.
Datsanatse gaalo deshfetsr kic'iru asho be'efetsr maac' k'eweraw asho «Ik'o shunfee» eto awuk'o k'alrniya b́faliti?
T nana'otso! No shuno arikonat finon be'etka bako noonon mec'ron keewon wotk'aye.
Mannowere arkeewtswotsi nowottsok'onat Ik'ishinats t'inosh shatalon aaw shuk'on t'inosh nofalitwok'o danfone.
Nonibo noats bíangshiyalor Ik'o noniboniyere danbe, bíye jamkeewo danfee.
T shuntswotso! No nibo noats angshratse wotiyal Ik'i shinatse ááw shuuk'o detsetwonee.
Ik'i tzazi jamo s'eentsr bín gene'úshit keewo nofinitwotse nok'onitu jamo bíyoke daatsitwone.
Ik'o azaztsonu b́ naay Iyesus Krstos shútson amanar Krstos noon bíazaztsok'on noatsatsewo noshunetwok'owe.
Ik'o azaztso k'alitu jamwots Ik'ona bobeti, Ik'onwere boyitse b́beeti, Ik'o noyitse b́beyirwok'o nodanet noosh b́ imts S'ayin shayirone.
T shuntswotso! datsatse kotetsk wotts nebiyiwots botutsotse shayr jamwotsi aman k'ayere, maniyere shayirwots Ik'okik bowotonat wotbok'azo fads'iilere.
Ik' Shayiro b́ woto galde'e it danet hanne Iyesus Krstos meetson b́ be'etsok'o amants shayir jamo Ik'i shayire,
Iyesus Krstos ash wotat meetso tahadek't b́be'etsok'o amaneraw shayir jamo Ik'oki shayiraliye, shayiraanu weetwe etefere itshishtso Krstosi k'efiru shayironiye, bíwere andoru dab́ datsuatse fa'ee.
Nana'otso! It Ik'k itne, ititse beyru shayiro datsanatse fa'a shayironiyere bogfe. Eshe kotets nebiyotsi da'artee.
Kootets nebiyots datsatsikne, bokeewirwonu datsanatsi keewoniye. Datsanwere bokeewo k'ebetwane.
No Ik'ik noone, Ik' dants jamo no keewo k'ebetwe, Ik'ik woteraw jamonmó no keewo k'ewatse. Ari shayronat kooti shayiron nodanet hanne.
Shunetswotsó! shuno Ik'okik b́wottsotse no atsatsewo shunewone, shuniru jamo Ik'i na'ee, Ik'onowere danfee.
Ik'o shun b́wottsotse ash shunaw jamo Ik'o danatse.
Ik'o b́naayn kasho nodaatsitwok'o b́ naay ik s'uzo datsanats woshere, mannowere Ik'i shuno nodagotse be'ere.
Shuna eto hank'oyiye, no Ik'o noshuntsosh b́ woterawo bí noon b́ shuntsonat nomorro b́ t'afitwok'o b́ naayi b́woshtsoshee.
Shunetswotsó! Ik'o hank'o noon b́shuniyakon no noatsatsewo shunewo noon geyife.
Ik' bek'ts asho konwor aaliye. Noo noatsatsewo noshuneyink'ere Ik'o noyitse beyank'ee, b́ shunonwere noyitse s'een wotiyank'ee.
Ik'o b́ shayiro nooshowere b́'imtsotse no bín bíwere noyitse b́ beyirwok'owo danfone.
Niho datsani b́ kashitwok'o woshdek't naayo b́wooshtsok'o bek'rone, manowere gawitwone.
Iyesus Ik'o naayi b́ wottsok'o amanitu ashotsne Ik'o b́beeti, bíwere Ik'ootse b́beeti.
Mann Ik'o noosh b́detsts shuno danfone, manowere amanerone. Ik'o shune, shunon beyirwo Ik'one b́beyiri, Ik'onwere b́ gitsotse b́beyiri.
Noo datsanatse nobeyir ari Krstos b́beyirwok'o b́wottsotse noshuno s'een b́wotink'ere angshi aawots shatalon b́shinaatse aaw shuk'on t'inosh falyank'onee.
S'een shuno shato kishde'erni juubk'rti bako shunotse shato aaliye, shato sezonton deshk b́wottsotse shatiru asho b́shuno s'een woteratse.
Ik'o shin shintson nonb́shuntsotse noowere shunetwonee.
Ik'o shunfee etfetst bíeshuwi shit'irwo kotetsiye, b́ bek'tso bí'eshuwi shunatse wotiyal b́ be'aaw Ik'o shuno falratse.
Eshe Krstos noosh b́'imts tzaziyo Ik' shuntso bíeshuno shune erkee.
Iyesus Mesihiyo b́ wottsok'o amants jamwots Ik' nana'anee, nihono shunetu jamo naayo noowere shunfee.
Ik' nana'úwotsi noshuntsok'o nodanetiye, Ik'o shunr b́ tzaziyo no s'entsoree.
Ik' shuna eto b́ tzaziyotsi s'entsee. B́ tzaziyotsu mangnaliye.
Ik' nana'a wotts jamo datsu da'itwe, datsu no da'itwere imnetiyone.
Iyesus Ik'o naayi b́ wottsok'o amantsoni bako kone datsu da'itwoni?
Aatsots b́ gupetsok'o kitsit aatsonat b́ k'iro kitsru s'atsi weeron waatso Iyesus Krstosiye. Bí b́waa aats mec'ron b́ woterawo aatsonat s'atsone. Hanwere ar b́ wottsotse, keewanwere ar b́wottsok'owo S'ayin shayiron gawitwe.
Keez gawwots fa'ane,
Bowere Shayirona, aatsonat s'atsone, keezanotswere bogawon ikne.
Ashuwots bo gawts gawo dek'etwonee, ernmó Ik'o gawts gawonmó jamoniyere bogfe. Ik'o b́ gawtsonwere b́ naay jangosh b́ gawtsoniyee haniye.
Ik'o naayn amantsonmó gawan b́ gitsotse fa'ee, Ik' amanerawonmó Ik'o b́ naay jangosh b́'imts gawo aman b́ k'aztsatse tuutson Ik'o kootetsi woshre.
B́ gawonwere Ik'o dúre dúri kasho noosh b́ imtsok'onat kashmanwere b́ naayitse b́ beyirwok'o gawirwoniyee.
Ik'o naayi detstso kasho detsfe. Ik'o naayi deshawonmó kasho deshatse.
It Ik'o naay shútson amants jamwots dúre dúri kasho it detstsok'o it danishe han itsh guut're.
Kon naari keewonor b́ wotiyal b́ shuntsok'on nok'onitkawotiyal noosh b́ shishetwok'o amanitwone.
Noo k'onts jamo b́ shishetwok'o danfonewotiyal, bíyokere nok'onts jamo andon nodek'etwok'o danfone.
Konworu wotowa, ash iko bí eshu k'irosh bín betsaw morro b́ finefe b́bek'al bísh Ik'o k'onwe, ashman morro k'irosh bín betsatse wotiyal Ik'o kasho bísh imetwe. Ernmó k'irosh betsit morro fa'ee. Man naari morrosh Ik'o k'onuwe eraatse taa.
Gond fin jamo morre. Wotowa eree k'irosh betsraw morro fa'ee.
Ik' na'o Iyesus Krstos bín b́ kotirwosh Ik' na'a wotts jamo morro b́ finerawok'o danfone, Shed'anonwere bíats boratse.
Noo Ik'k nowottsok'o danfone. Datsunmó jamon shed'ani ali shirotse b́ fa'oni.
Ik' na'o b́ wattsok'onat ari Ik'o nodanetwok'o t'iwitsts nibo noosh b́'imtsok'o danfone, b́ naay Iyesus Krstos weeron bínton ari Ik'onton ikwoto detsfone. Iyesus Krstos ari Izar Izeweru dúre dúri kashonu bíne.
T nana'otso! dozets ik'wotsatse it atso korde'ere.
Tiyoke eenashoke, marat'ets moogenunat b nana'otsnsh, Tí s'uzi b́woteftsere ar dants jamwotswere iti shunfne.
Aranwere no dagotse fa'onat shino maantsisho dúre dúron noonton beetwoniye.
Ik'o nihonat b́ naay Iyesus Krstotsoke s'aatona, mihretiyona, jenonwere, aronat shunon noonton wotowe.
N nana'uwotsitse ik ikuwotsi niho noon bí azaztsok'on arikeewon kup'at boere t datstsotse ayidek'at gene'owere.
Moo genee, andoor oona neesha, neesh t guut'irwan tzazi handr ark'aye, and t guut'irwan «No ats atsewo shunewone» etts shintson dek't nowooke teshts tzaziyoniye.
Ari shuna eto Ik' tzaziyo fina etee. Tzaziymanwere shintson it shishtsok'on «Shunon beewere,» ettsoniye.
Iyesus ash wotat meetson b́ be'etsok'o amanerawwots ash sheeliyru aywots datsanatse tuurne. Mank'o ashaan ant'elcirwonat Krstosi k'efirwoniye.
Itmó it k'awntso s'eenon dek'osh kup'ore, it fintso b́ t'afrawok'o korde'ere.
Krstos danits danaats s'ap'de'er beerawo bíatsnowere wokar ametuwonton Ik'o aaliye, Krstos danits danaats s'ap'de beet ashontonmó Nihonat Nayon bíntoniye bofa'oni.
Dan han b́deshawo konwor itok b́wetitkawotiyal it meyits kindshk'ayere, dab́ jamonor bín aatk'ayere.
Bín jam aatit asho bínton gond fino kaytsoni b́wotiti.
Itsh guut'osh t geyirwo ay keewo detsfe, wotowa eree jamo dabdayon wosho geeratse, Maniyere itok borr noonon itn keewiye tgeyiriye, manwere noshunewo s'een b́ wotituwok'o geeyatniye.
N mish marat'etsu nana'uwots neesh jamo woshernee.
Arikon t shuntso, shunetso Gayiyossh, Tiyoke eenashoke,
T shuntsono! n be jamo neesh b́ kááwitwok'o, jeenono nwotitwok'o, jam weeron neesh b́sheengetwok'owe Ik'o tk'oniri.
Arosh ni amanetsok'onat aron n beeyirwok'on krstiyani wotts eshu ik ikwots waat bokeewor aydek'atniye t geneúwi.
T nana'wots arikon ananefetst bobeyrwok'o shishoniye bogo taan geneúshit keewo aaliye.
T shuntsono! neesh dab ib bowotiyalor eshu eshuwotssh amanek fine nfiniri.
Bowere boosh shunon nfints fino Ik'i maa shinatse kishdek't keewrnee, andoor Ik'o genee'ushitwok'on bowerindosh boon ntep'al sheenge.
Krstossh finosh bokeshor amanerawwotsoke eegor tep'o dek'keyatsnee.
Ari fin finrwotsnton finirwotsi nowotitwok'o hanotsk'o ashuwotsnton fino noon geyife.
Haniyere shinon Ik' moosh wosho guut're b́teshi, ernmo Ik' maa jish geyirwo Diyotrefis ti ettso de'atse.
Eshe itok twoor bí noon c'ashfetst, ketifetst b́ k'alts gond fin jamo keewitwe, man bísh bodob́k'aye bí b́ tookish eshu eshuwotsi de'ake. K'oshwotswere bo de'awok'owe b́bazifoni. Ik'i mootsnowere boon b́gishefoni.
T shuntsono! sheengo arowe bako gondo ark'aye. Sheeng finiru jamo Ik'ikee. Gond finirwonmó Ik'o be'atse.
Dimet'ros jangosh ash jamo sheengkewon bísh gawirunee. Arunuwere b tookon bísh gawitwanee. Noowere gawitwone, nogawonwere ar b́ wotok'o danfnee.
Neesh guut'osh t geetso ay keewo detsfe b́ teshi, wotowa eree worek'atats neesh guut'o geeratse.
Karnon neen bek'oshe jangirwe, manoor noonon keewetwone.
Jeeno neesh wotowe. Hanoki n tooh tohuwots neesh jamo t'intsirune. Neewere no tohuwotssh jamo ik ikon t'intsuwe.
Iyesus Krstos guutso Yak'ob eshwi wottso Yuhudoke, S'eegetswotssh, Nihon Ik'on shuneetswotssh, Iyesus Krstosn kotets jametswotssh.
Maac' k'ewo, jeenonat shunon itsh ayowe.
Shuneetswotso! Ik wotdek'at nokashts kashi jango itsh guut'o ayidek'at geeyatniye tteshi, andmo aaniy iwisho b́ geyrawook'on Ik'o bí ashuwotssh iknoton b́ imts imnetiyi jangosh kup'de'er it kaaritwok'o itsh guut'o ayidek't geyiko taash b́woti.
Boats angshetwok'o ay duroniyere shino bojangosh guut'etswots mut'at itits kindrnee, bohe Izar Izewerko s'aato gusiyi beyon wonitwots Ik'o Ik'irawwotsiye, no doonz b́ s'uzi wottso Iyesus Krstosnor haalitune.
Jaman shin shino iknoton it dankawotiyalor doonzo Gbs' datsatse kisht b́ kashitsok'oonat amanerawwotsnowere il b́ t'afitsok'o itsh gawiyo, shunfee.
Boon naashiyetsatse beshat bobeyoko fakshk'rts melakiwotsi aab s'iilere, Ik'o boon angshi eeno aawotssh b́borfetso dúre dúri tipoon, nic' etts t'aluwots kotdek't beezree.
Mank'oon Sedom, Gemoornat bo gúúratsi kitwotswere gusiyetswotsi bowoti, niwalonowere gobo boami. Mansh bo dúre dúri taawon sezeyirwotsi ariyetswotsi woternee.
Mank'owere ashaanots bo gúmon jisheyat bomeetso bokimshiri, naashwotsshoor aleraknee, darotse mang detstswotsnowere boc'ashiri.
Melakiwotsitsi naasho Mika'elwor dab Muse duuni jangosh Diyablosnton b́ mooshor «Ik'o neen fayowe» eta b́ eti bako c'asho c'ayatse.
Ashaanotsmó t'iwitsdek'oosh bo falaaw keew jamo boc'ashiri, gaw dek'falaw dini s'otswotskok'o bo azeewon bodants keewo fa'e wotiyalor dab bíne bot'afiti.
K'aayen werindon boamtsotse, gizosha ett Bele'ami dáriits weeron bo dihitsotse, K'oree Ik'o b́ k'eftsok'o boowere k'efat bo t'aftsosh indowe boosha!
Ashaanots bo jitserawo gusiyon ikwotar moonat úshoke bodatsewor itsh t'uge bowotititi, bo boshiyaniriye botookk mec'eroshee, jongon gifiniyeyiru, awsh deshaw dawnok'one, shuu daatseef shashotse dab shuu biyatse daatseraw, b́ s'ap'ootse wat'ere gitoto shuuk'ts mitok'one.
Bo, fayiru aats k'ari fuundok'o boon jitsits fini úmbo kishirune, nyic' etts t'aluwo dúre dúrosh boon b́ kotirwotsnat hake bako jawriru k'eenwotskok'one.
Adamatse tuut shawatl gubratse shuwetso Henok bek'on b́keewor hank'o etre, «Eshe doonzo ay tats kum b́ wosh nana'a S'ayinwotsnton wotde jametsats angshosh weetwe.
Doonzo bín Ik'iraw ashmanots bofints gond keewatse tuutson sezitwe, Arikon doonzo bín Ik'iraw morrets hanotsi bíyats bokeewts gond keew jamwotsatse tuutson bo atsats angshitwe.»
Ashaanots jam aawo mumudefetst ik keewonor genee'úweraknee, botook gond tewni jafrats sha'irwotsiye, bonono míshi keewon s'eenke, botook keewo geeyat asho weeralo bo dáshiri.
Shuneetswotso! Itiyere! Nodoonź Iyesus Krstos woshetswots haniyere shin bokeewts keewo gawde'ere.
Bo «Dúri s'uwatse Ik'i hasabiyatse wokat bo took gond tewno shuuts sha'iru c'aashetswots weetune» itsh etrne boteshi.
Boye ash dago gaakirwotsiye, meetsi tewni jafrats sha'irwotsiye, S'ayin shayronowere deshawotsiye.
T mashotso! jamoniyere bogo s'ayin wotts it imnetiyon it tooko agosh kup'ore, S'ayin shayiri angonowere Ik'o k'onwere.
Nodoonz Iyesus Krstoswor b́mac' nefon dúre dúri kasho itsh b́ betsitwok'o korde'er it tooko Ik'i shunoots korde'ere.
Git nibetsdetswotssh ashuwotssh maac'o k'ewore,
Ik ikwotsi taawotse kishde'er kashiwere, k'oshwotssh shatoon maac'o k'ewore, b́woteferor morron kiimts bo atso t'awits tahman b́ oorerawo shid'ere.
It dihrawok'o woshitwonat eeg eeg deshawwotsi woshr geneúwon b́mangi shinats t'intsosh falitwosh,
B́ s'uz noosh no ato wottso Izar Izewersh, nodoonz Iyesus Krstos weeron shintson tuur, dúre dúrosh mangonat, baatson, kup'oonat alonwere wotowe! amen.
Bek'an karn gizewotse wotit keewo Ik'o b́ guutswotssh kitsosh Iyesus Krstossh b́ imtsoniye, Iyesus Krstoswere melakiyo woshat b́ guutso Yohanissh bek'an b́ kitsi.
Yohaniswere Ik' aap'onat Iyesus Krstos bísh b́ danitso, mank'o b́ bek'ts keew jamo gawere.
Jaman b́s'eenet aawo karn b́ wottsotse bek'i aap'an nababirwo deereke! mank'o bek'i aap'man shishirwotsnat beek'anits guut'etso s'eentsitwots derekne.
Yohanisoke Isiyotse fa'a shawat Ik' moowwotssh. Fa'oke, teshtsoknat weetu Ik'oke, b́ naashi jori shinatse fa'a shawat shayirwotsoke, mank'o k'irotse tuwon k'aab wottsoke datsatsi nugúswotsi keewirwo, amanets gawo wottsoke, noon shuntsonat b́ s'atson nomorotse noon nas' kishtso Iyesus Krstos s'aatoonat jeenon itsh wotowe.
